{BaudhŚS, 1, 1}
āmāvāsyena vā paurṇamāsena vā haviṣā yakṣyamāṇaḥ bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 1 654839_1]
sa purastāt eva havirātañcanam upakalpayate eka ahena vā dvi ahena vā yathartu | [BaudhŚS, 1, 1 654840_1]
atha vai brāhmaṇam bhavati dadhnā ātanakti sa indra tvāya agnihotra uccheṣaṇam abhyātanakti yajñasya saṃtatyai iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 1 654842_1]
candramasam vā a nirjñāya sampūrṇam vā vijñāya agnīn anvādadhāti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 1 654844_1]
trīṇi kāṣṭhāni gārhapatye abhyādadhāti trīṇi anvāhāryapacane trīṇi āhavanīye | [BaudhŚS, 1, 1 654845_1]
parisamūhanti upavasathasya rūpam kurvanti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 1 654846_1]
atha asya vrata upetasya parṇa śākhām acchaiti prāṅ vā udaṅ vā vācaṃyamaḥ yatra vā vetsyan manyate | [BaudhŚS, 1, 1 654848_1]
sā yā prācī vā udīcī vā bahu parṇā bahu śākhā a pratiśuṣka agrā bhavati tām ācchinatti iṣe tvā ūrje tvā iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 1 654849_1]
tayā vatsān apākaroti vāyavaḥ stha upāyavaḥ stha iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 1 654850_1]
atha eṣām mātṝḥ prerayati devaḥ vaḥ savitā prārpayatu śreṣṭhatamāya karmaṇe āpyāyadhvam aghniyāḥ deva bhāgam ūrjasvatīḥ payasvatīḥ prajāvatīḥ anamīvāḥ mā vaḥ stenaḥ īśata mā agha śaṃsaḥ rudrasya hetiḥ pari vaḥ vṛṇaktu iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 1 654851_1]
dhruvāḥ asmin gopatau syāta bahvīḥ iti yajamānam īkṣate | [BaudhŚS, 1, 1 654852_1]
atha etām śākhām agreṇa āhavanīyam paryāhṛtya pūrvayā dvārā prapādya jaghanena gārhapatyam agniṣṭhe anasi uttara ardhe vā agnyagārasya udgūhati yajamānasya paśūn pāhi iti nu yadi saṃnayati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 1 654853_1]
yadi u vai na saṃnayati barhiḥ pratipad eva bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 1 654854_1]
{BaudhŚS, 1, 2}
atha jaghanena gārhapatyam tiṣṭhan asidam vā aśva parśum vā ādatte devasya tvā savituḥ prasave aśvinoḥ bāhubhyām pūṣṇaḥ hastābhyām ādade iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 2 654855_1]
ādāya abhimantrayate yajñasya ghoṣat asi iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 2 654856_1]
gārhapatye pratitapati pratyuṣṭam rakṣaḥ pratyuṣṭāḥ arātayaḥ iti tris | [BaudhŚS, 1, 2 654857_1]
atha āhavanīyam abhipraiti pra iyam agāt dhiṣaṇā barhiḥ accha manunā kṛtā svadhayā vitaṣṭā te āvahanti kavayaḥ purastāt devebhyaḥ juṣṭam iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 2 654858_1]
iha barhiḥ āsade iti vedim pratyavekṣate | [BaudhŚS, 1, 2 654859_1]
atha tām diśam eti yatra barhiḥ vetsyan manyate | [BaudhŚS, 1, 2 654860_1]
darbha stambam parigṛhṇāti yāvantam alam prastarāya manyate devānām pariṣūtam asi iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 2 654861_1]
atha enam ūrdhvam unmārṣṭi varṣa vṛddham asi iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 2 654862_1]
asidena upayacchati deva barhiḥ mā tvā anvak mā tiryak parva te rādhyāsam iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 2 654863_1]
ācchinatti ācchettā te mā riṣam iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 2 654864_1]
ācchedanāni abhimṛśati deva barhiḥ śata valśam viroha iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 2 654865_1]
sahasra valśāḥ vi vayam ruhema iti ātmānam pratyabhimṛśate | [BaudhŚS, 1, 2 654866_1]
sarvaśas eva enam stambam lunoti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 2 654867_1]
kṛtvā prastaram nidadhāti pṛthivyāḥ saṃpṛcaḥ pāhi iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 2 654868_1]
tūṣṇīm atas ūrdhvam ayujaḥ muṣṭīn lunoti trīn vā pañca vā sapta vā nava vā ekādaśa vā yāvataḥ vā alam manyate | [BaudhŚS, 1, 2 654869_1]
atha tris anvāhitam śulbam kṛtvā apasalaiḥ āveṣṭayati adityai rāsnā asi iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 2 654871_1]
tat udīcīna agram nidhāya tasmin prastaram abhisaṃbharati su saṃbhṛtā tvā saṃbharāmi iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 2 654873_1]
saṃnahyati indrāṇyai saṃnahanam iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 2 654874_1]
granthim karoti pūṣā te granthim grathnātu iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 2 654875_1]
sa te mā asthāt iti paścāt prāñcam upagūhati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 2 654876_1]
atha enat udyacchate indrasya tvā bāhubhyām udyacche iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 2 654877_1]
śīrṣan adhinidhatte bṛhaspateḥ mūrdhnā harāmi iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 2 654878_1]
aiti uru antarikṣam anvihi iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 2 654879_1]
etya uttareṇa gārhapatyam anadhas sādayati devaṃgamam asi iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 2 654880_1]
tat upari iva nidadhāti yatra guptam manyate | [BaudhŚS, 1, 2 654881_1]
tūṣṇīm paribhojanīyāni lunoti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 2 654882_1]
sakṛt ācchinnam pitṛbhyaḥ ācchinatti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 2 654883_1]
atha tathā eva tris anvāhitam śulbam kṛtvā ekaviṃśati dārum idhmam saṃnahyati yat kṛṣṇaḥ rūpam kṛtvā prāviśaḥ tvam vanaspatīn tatas tvām ekaviṃśatidhā saṃbharāmi su saṃbhṛtaḥ iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 2 654884_1]
vedam karoti vatsajñum paśu kāmasya mūta kāryam annādya kāmasya trivṛtam tejaskāmasya ūrdhva agram svarga kāmasya | [BaudhŚS, 1, 2 654885_1]
vedim karoti prāk uttarāt parigrāhāt | [BaudhŚS, 1, 2 654886_1]
atha aparāhṇe piṇḍapitṛyajñena carati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 2 654887_1]
{BaudhŚS, 1, 3}
atha etasyai śākhāyai parṇāni pracchidya agreṇa gārhapatyam nivapati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 3 654888_1]
atha enām adhastāt parivāsya jaghanena gārhapatyam sthavimat upaveṣāya nidadhāti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 3 654889_1]
atha asyāḥ prādeśa mātram pramāya darbha nāḍīḥ praveṣṭya tat trivṛt śākhāpavitram karoti trivṛt palāśe darbhaḥ iyān prādeśa saṃmitaḥ yajñe pavitram potṛtamam payaḥ havyam karotu me iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 3 654890_1]
atha sāyam hute agnihotre uttareṇa gārhapatyam tṛṇāni saṃstīrya teṣu catuṣṭayam saṃsādayati dohanam pavitram sāṃnāyya tapanyau sthālyau iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 3 654892_1]
atha enāni adbhiḥ prokṣati śundhadhvam daivyāya karmaṇe deva yajyāyai iti tris | [BaudhŚS, 1, 3 654893_1]
atha jaghanena gārhapatyam upaviśya upaveṣeṇa udīcaḥ aṅgārān nirūhati mātariśvanaḥ gharmaḥ asi iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 3 654894_1]
teṣu sāṃnāyya tapanīm adhiśrayati dyauḥ asi pṛthivī asi viśva dhāyāḥ asi parameṇa dhāmnā dṛṃhasva mā hvār iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 3 654895_1]
tasyām prācīna agram śākhāpavitram nidadhāti vasūnām pavitram asi śata dhāram vasūnām pavitram asi sahasra dhāram iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 3 654896_1]
tat anvārabhya vācaṃyamaḥ āste | [BaudhŚS, 1, 3 654897_1]
atha gāḥ āyatīḥ pratīkṣate etāḥ ācaranti madhumat duhānāḥ prajāvatīḥ yaśasaḥ viśva rūpāḥ bahvīḥ bhavantīḥ upajāyamānāḥ iha vaḥ indraḥ ramayatu gāvaḥ iti mahendraḥ iti vā yadi mahendra yājī bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 3 654898_1]
atha āha upasṛṣṭām me prabrūtāt iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 3 654900_1]
upasṛṣṭām prāhuḥ | [BaudhŚS, 1, 3 654901_1]
dohyamānām anumantrayate hutaḥ stokaḥ hutaḥ drapsaḥ agnaye bṛhate nākāya svāhā dyāvāpṛthivībhyām iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 3 654902_1]
atha purastāt pratyak ānayantam pṛcchati kām adhukṣaḥ iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 3 654903_1]
amūm iti itaraḥ pratyāha | [BaudhŚS, 1, 3 654904_1]
tām anumantrayate sā viśva āyuḥ iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 3 654905_1]
dvitīyam ānayantam pṛcchati kām adhukṣaḥ iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 3 654906_1]
amūm iti eva itaraḥ pratyāha | [BaudhŚS, 1, 3 654907_1]
tām anumantrayate sā viśva vyacāḥ iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 3 654908_1]
tṛtīyam ānayantam pṛcchati kām adhukṣaḥ iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 3 654909_1]
amūm iti eva itaraḥ pratyāha | [BaudhŚS, 1, 3 654910_1]
tām anumantrayate sā viśva karmā iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 3 654911_1]
tisṛṣu dugdhāsu vācam visṛjate bahu dugdhi indrāya devebhyaḥ havyam āpyāyatām punar vatsebhyaḥ manuṣyebhyaḥ punar dohāya kalpatām iti mahendrāya iti vā yadi mahendra yājī bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 3 654912_1]
visṛṣṭa vāc an anvārabhya tūṣṇīm uttarāḥ dohayitvā dohane apaḥ ānīya saṃkṣālanam ānayati saṃpṛcyadhvam ṛtāvarīḥ ūrmiṇīḥ madhumattamāḥ mandrāḥ dhanasya sātaye iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 3 654915_1]
atha enat taptvā udak udvāsya śītīkṛtvā tiras pavitram dadhnā ātanakti somena tvā tanacmi indrāya dadhi iti mahendrāya iti vā yadi mahendra yājī bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 3 654916_1]
yāvatā mūrchayiṣyat manyate tāvat ānayati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 3 654917_1]
agnihotra uccheṣaṇam abhyātanakti yajñasya saṃtatiḥ asi yajñasya tvā saṃtatim anusaṃtanomi iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 3 654918_1]
atha enat udanvatā kaṃsena vā camasena vā apidadhāti a dastam asi viṣṇave tvā yajñāya apidadhāmi aham adbhiḥ ariktena pātreṇa yāḥ pūtāḥ pariśerate iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 3 654919_1]
tat upari iva nidadhāti yatra guptam manyate viṣṇo havyam rakṣasva iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 3 654921_1]
etasmin kāle darbhaiḥ prātardohāya vatsān apākaroti tūṣṇīm | [BaudhŚS, 1, 3 654922_1]
{BaudhŚS, 1, 4}
atha prātar hute agnihotre hastau saṃmṛśate karmaṇe vām devebhyaḥ śakeyam iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 4 654923_1]
naktam paristīrṇāḥ eva ete agnayaḥ bhavanti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 4 654924_1]
yadi u vai a paristīrṇāḥ bhavanti āhavanīyam eva agre purastāt paristṛṇāti atha dakṣiṇatas atha paścāt atha uttaratas | [BaudhŚS, 1, 4 654925_1]
evam eva anvāhāryapacanam paristṛṇāti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 4 654926_1]
evam gārhapatyam | [BaudhŚS, 1, 4 654927_1]
atha agreṇa gārhapatyam tṛṇāni saṃstīrya teṣu dvandvam nyañci yajñāyudhāni saṃsādayati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 4 654928_1]
sphyam ca kapālāni ca agnihotrahavaṇīm ca śūrpam ca kṛṣṇājinam ca śamyām ca ulūkhalam ca musalam ca dṛṣadam ca upalām ca juhūm ca upabhṛtam ca sruvam ca dhruvām ca prāśitraharaṇam ca iḍāpātram ca mekṣaṇam ca piṣṭodvapanīm ca praṇītā praṇayanam ca ājya sthālīm ca vedam ca dāru pātrīm ca yoktram ca veda parivāsanam ca dhṛṣṭim ca idhmapravraścanam ca anvāhārya sthālīm ca madantīm ca yāni ca anyāni pātrāṇi tāni evam eva dvandvam saṃsādya brahmāṇam dakṣiṇatas upaveśya pṛṣṭhyām stṛṇāti saṃtatām gārhapatyāt āhavanīyāt yajñasya saṃtatiḥ asi yajñasya tvā saṃtatyai stṛṇāmi saṃtatyai tvā yajñasya stṛṇāmi iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 4 654931_1]
atha barhiṣaḥ pavitre kurute prādeśa mātre same a praticchinna agre a nakha chinne imau prāṇa apānau yajñasya aṅgāni sarvaśas āpyāyayantau saṃcaratām pavitre havya śodhane iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 4 654932_1]
atha ene adbhiḥ anumārṣṭi pavitre sthaḥ vaiṣṇavī sthaḥ yajñiye sthaḥ vāyu pūte sthaḥ viṣṇoḥ manasā pūte sthaḥ yajñasya pavane stha iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 4 654934_1]
atha uttareṇa gārhapatyam upaviśya kaṃsam vā camasam vā praṇītā praṇayanam yācati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 4 654935_1]
tasmin tiras pavitram apaḥ ānayan āha brahman apaḥ praṇeṣyāmi yajamāna vācam yaccha iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 4 654936_1]
prasūtaḥ samam prāṇaiḥ dhārayamāṇaḥ a viṣiñcan hṛtvā uttareṇa āhavanīyam darbheṣu sādayitvā darbhaiḥ pracchādya pavitram ādāya pradakṣiṇam āvṛtya pratyaṅ ādrutya ādatte dakṣiṇena agnihotrahavaṇīm savyena śūrpam veṣāya tvā iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 4 654938_1]
gārhapatye pratitapati pratyuṣṭam rakṣaḥ pratyuṣṭāḥ arātayaḥ iti tris | [BaudhŚS, 1, 4 654939_1]
atha jaghanena gārhapatyam agniṣṭham anaḥ bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 4 654940_1]
tasya uttarām dhuram abhimṛśati dhūḥ asi dhūrva tam yaḥ asmān dhūrvati tam dhūrva yam vayam dhūrvāmaḥ iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 4 654941_1]
anaḥ abhimantrayate tvam devānām asi sasnitamam papritamam juṣṭatamam vahnitamam devahūtamam ahrutam asi havirdhānam dṛṃhasva mā hvār iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 4 654942_1]
{BaudhŚS, 1, 5}
atha viṣṇoḥ kramaḥ asi iti dakṣiṇam akṣa pālim kramitvā abhyāruhya prauge śūrpam nidadhāti śūrpe srucam sruci pavitre | [BaudhŚS, 1, 5 654943_1]
atha puroḍāśīyān prekṣate mitrasya tvā cakṣuṣā prekṣe mā bheḥ mā saṃvikthāḥ mā tvā hiṃsiṣam iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 5 654945_1]
uru vātāya iti tṛṇam vā kiṃśāru vā nirasyati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 5 654946_1]
atha apaḥ upaspṛśya daśahotāram vyākhyāya haviḥ nirvapsyāmi iti yajamānam āmantrya pavitravatyā agnihotrahavaṇyā nirvapati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 5 654947_1]
yadi u vai na anaḥ bhavati jaghanena gārhapatyam sphyam nidadhāti sphya upari pātrīm | [BaudhŚS, 1, 5 654948_1]
pātryām puroḍāśīyān āvapati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 5 654949_1]
atha pūrva ardham pātryāḥ abhimṛśati dhūḥ asi dhūrva tam yaḥ asmān dhūrvati tam dhūrva yam vayam dhūrvāmaḥ tvam devānām asi sasnitamam papritamam juṣṭatamam vahnitamam devahūtamam ahrutam asi havirdhānam dṛṃhasva mā hvār iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 5 654950_1]
atha puroḍāśīyān prekṣate mitrasya tvā cakṣuṣā prekṣe mā bheḥ mā saṃvikthāḥ mā tvā hiṃsiṣam iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 5 654951_1]
uru vātāya iti tṛṇam vā kiṃśāru vā nirasyati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 5 654952_1]
atha apaḥ upaspṛśya daśahotāram vyākhyāya haviḥ nirvapsyāmi iti yajamānam āmantrya pavitravatyā agnihotrahavaṇyā nirvapati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 5 654953_1]
om nirvapa iti yajamānaḥ anujānāti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 5 654954_1]
atha nirvapati devasya tvā savituḥ prasave aśvinoḥ bāhubhyām pūṣṇaḥ hastābhyām agnaye juṣṭam nirvapāmi iti tris etena yajuṣā sakṛt tūṣṇīm | [BaudhŚS, 1, 5 654955_1]
etām eva pratipadam kṛtvā agnīṣomābhyām iti paurṇamāsyām indrāya vaimṛdhāya iti ca indra agnibhyām iti amāvāsyāyām a saṃnayataḥ indrāya iti saṃnayataḥ mahendrāya iti vā yadi mahendra yājī bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 5 654959_1]
atha niruptān abhimṛśati idam devānām iti idam u naḥ saha iti ye atiśiṣṭāḥ bhavanti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 5 654960_1]
sphātyai tvā na arātyai iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 5 654962_1]
atha āhavanīyam īkṣate suvar abhivikhyeṣam vaiśvānaram jyotiḥ iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 5 654963_1]
atha gṛhān anvīkṣate dṛṃhantām duryāḥ dyāvāpṛthivyoḥ iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 5 654964_1]
atha enān ādāya upottiṣṭhati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 5 654965_1]
aiti uru antarikṣam anvihi iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 5 654966_1]
etya uttareṇa gārhapatyam upasādayati adityāḥ tvā upasthe sādayāmi iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 5 654967_1]
gārhapatyam abhimantrayate agne havyam rakṣasva iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 5 654968_1]
{BaudhŚS, 1, 6}
atha etasyām eva sruci tiras pavitram apaḥ ānīya udīcīna agrābhyām pavitrābhyām tris utpunāti devaḥ vaḥ savitā utpunātu acchidreṇa pavitreṇa vasoḥ sūryasya raśmibhiḥ iti pacchas | [BaudhŚS, 1, 6 654969_1]
atha enāḥ unmahayan upottiṣṭhati āpaḥ devīḥ agrepuvaḥ agreguvaḥ agre imam yajñam nayatā agre yajña patim dhatta yuṣmān indraḥ avṛṇīta vṛtratūrye yūyam indram avṛṇīdhvam vṛtratūrye iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 6 654970_1]
adbhiḥ eva apaḥ prokṣati prokṣitāḥ stha prokṣitāḥ stha iti tris | [BaudhŚS, 1, 6 654971_1]
atha puroḍāśīyān prokṣati devasya tvā savituḥ prasave aśvinoḥ bāhubhyām pūṣṇaḥ hastābhyām agnaye vaḥ juṣṭam prokṣāmi agnīṣomābhyām amuṣmai amuṣmai iti yathādevatam tris | [BaudhŚS, 1, 6 654972_1]
uttānāni pātrāṇi kṛtvā prokṣati śundhadhvam daivyāya karmaṇe deva yajyāyai iti tris | [BaudhŚS, 1, 6 654973_1]
atiśiṣṭāḥ prokṣaṇīḥ nidhāya kṛṣṇājinam avadhūnoti ūrdhva grīvam udaṅ āvṛtya avadhūtam rakṣaḥ avadhūtāḥ arātayaḥ iti tris | [BaudhŚS, 1, 6 654975_1]
atha enat purastāt pratīcīna grīvam uttara loma upastṛṇāti adityāḥ tvac asi prati tvā pṛthivī vettu iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 6 654976_1]
tasmin ulūkhalam adhyūhati adhiṣavaṇam asi vānaspatyam prati tvā adityāḥ tvac vettu iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 6 654977_1]
tasmin puroḍāśīyān āvapati agneḥ tanūḥ asi vācaḥ visarjanam deva vītaye tvā gṛhṇāmi iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 6 654978_1]
musalam avadadhāti adriḥ asi vānaspatyaḥ saḥ idam devebhyaḥ havyam suśami śamiṣva iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 6 654979_1]
atha haviṣkṛtam āhvayati haviṣkṛt ehi haviṣkṛt ehi iti tris | [BaudhŚS, 1, 6 654980_1]
uccais samāhantavai iti ca | [BaudhŚS, 1, 6 654981_1]
atha dṛṣad upale vṛṣāraveṇa uccais samāhanti iṣam āvada ūrjam āvada dyumat vadata vayam saṃghātam jeṣma iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 6 654981_2]
avahatya uttuṣān kṛtvā uttaratas śūrpam upayacchati varṣa vṛddham asi iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 6 654982_1]
tasmin puroḍāśīyān udvapati prati tvā varṣa vṛddham vettu iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 6 654983_1]
atha udaṅ paryāvṛtya parāpunāti parāpūtam rakṣaḥ parāpūtāḥ arātayaḥ iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 6 654984_1]
savyena tuṣān upahatya imām diśam nirasyati rakṣasām bhāgaḥ asi iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 6 654985_1]
atha apaḥ upaspṛśya vivinakti vāyuḥ vaḥ vivinaktu iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 6 654986_1]
pātryām taṇḍulān praskandayati devaḥ vaḥ savitā hiraṇya pāṇiḥ pratigṛhṇātu iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 6 654987_1]
avahantryai prayacchan āha triṣphalīkartavai triṣphalīkṛtān me prabrūtāt iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 6 654988_1]
triṣphalīkṛtān prāhuḥ | [BaudhŚS, 1, 6 654989_1]
triṣphalīkriyamāṇānām yaḥ nyaṅgaḥ avaśiṣyate rakṣasām bhāgadheyam āpaḥ tat pravahatāt itas iti taṇḍula prakṣālanam antarvedi ninayati utkara deśe vā | [BaudhŚS, 1, 6 654990_1]
etasmin kāle prātardoham dhenūḥ dohayati udak agreṇa pavitreṇa | [BaudhŚS, 1, 6 654991_1]
na atra ātanakti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 6 654992_1]
{BaudhŚS, 1, 7}
atha prokteṣu triṣphalīkṛteṣu tathā eva kṛṣṇājinam avadhūnoti ūrdhva grīvam udaṅ āvṛtya avadhūtam rakṣaḥ avadhūtāḥ arātayaḥ iti tris | [BaudhŚS, 1, 7 654993_1]
atha enat purastāt pratīcīna grīvam uttara loma upastṛṇāti adityāḥ tvac asi prati tvā pṛthivī vettu iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 7 654994_1]
tasmin udīcīna kumbām śamyām nidadhāti divaḥ skambhaniḥ asi prati tvā adityāḥ tvac vettu iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 7 654995_1]
tasyām prācīm dṛṣadam adhyūhati dhiṣaṇā asi parvatyā prati tvā divaḥ skambhaniḥ vettu iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 7 654996_1]
dṛṣadi upalām adhyūhati dhiṣaṇā asi pārvateyī prati tvā parvatiḥ vettu iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 7 654997_1]
tasyām puroḍāśīyān adhivapati devasya tvā savituḥ prasave aśvinoḥ bāhubhyām pūṣṇaḥ hastābhyām agnaye juṣṭam adhivapāmi agnīṣomābhyām amuṣmai amuṣmai iti yathādevatam | [BaudhŚS, 1, 7 654998_1]
adhivadate dhānyam asi dhinuhi devān dhinuhi yajñam dhinuhi yajñapatim dhinuhi mām yajñaniyam iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 7 654999_1]
piṃṣati prāṇāya tvā apānāya tvā vyānāya tvā iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 7 655000_1]
bāhū anvavekṣate dīrghām anu prasitim āyuṣe dhām iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 7 655001_1]
kṛṣṇājine piṣṭāni praskandayati devaḥ vaḥ savitā hiraṇya pāṇiḥ pratigṛhṇātu iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 7 655002_1]
haviḥ peṣyai prayacchan āha a saṃvapantī piṃṣa aṇūni kurutāt iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 7 655003_1]
piṃṣanti puroḍāśīyān | [BaudhŚS, 1, 7 655004_1]
ni caravyān dadhati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 7 655005_1]
yadi carum kariṣyan bhavati prāk adhivapanāt caru puroḍāśīyān vibhajeran | [BaudhŚS, 1, 7 655006_1]
{BaudhŚS, 1, 8}
atha etāni kapālāni prakṣālitāni jaghanena gārhapatyam upasādayati aṣṭau dakṣiṇatas ekādaśa uttaratas | [BaudhŚS, 1, 8 655007_1]
atha jaghanena gārhapatyam upaviśya dhṛṣṭim ādatte dhṛṣṭiḥ asi brahma yaccha iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 8 655009_1]
gārhapatyam abhimantrayate apa agne agnim āma adam jahi iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 8 655010_1]
niḥ kravya adam sedha iti dakṣiṇā aṅgāram nirasyati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 8 655011_1]
atha anyam āvartayati ā deva yajam vaha iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 8 655012_1]
tam dakṣiṇeṣām kapālānām madhyamena abhyupadadhāti dhruvam asi pṛthivīm dṛṃha āyuḥ dṛṃha prajām dṛṃha sajātān asmai yajamānāya paryūha iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 8 655013_1]
aṅgāram adhivartayati nirdagdham rakṣaḥ nirdagdhāḥ arātayaḥ iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 8 655014_1]
atha pūrva ardhyam upadadhāti dhartram asi antarikṣam dṛṃha prāṇam dṛṃha apānam dṛṃha sajātān asmai yajamānāya paryūha iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 8 655015_1]
atha apara ardhyam upadadhāti dharuṇam asi divam dṛṃha cakṣuḥ dṛṃha śrotram dṛṃha sajātān asmai yajamānāya paryūha iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 8 655016_1]
atha dakṣiṇa ardhyam upadadhāti dharma asi diśaḥ dṛṃha yonim dṛṃha prajām dṛṃha sajātān asmai yajamānāya paryūha iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 8 655017_1]
atha pūrvam upadhim upadadhāti citaḥ stha prajām asmai rayim asmai sajātān asmai yajamānāya paryūha iti atha aparam evam eva | [BaudhŚS, 1, 8 655018_1]
dve uttaratas saṃspṛṣṭe upadadhāti citaḥ stha prajām asmai rayim asmai sajātān asmai yajamānāya paryūha iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 8 655020_1]
atha enāni aṅgāraiḥ adhivāsayati bhṛgūṇām aṅgirasām tapasā tapyadhvam iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 8 655021_1]
atha enāni yogena yunakti yāni gharme kapālāni upacinvanti vedhasaḥ pūṣṇaḥ tāni api vrate indra vāyū yuṅktām iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 8 655022_1]
evam eva uttarāṇi kapālāni upadadhāti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 8 655023_1]
abhīndhate kapālāni | [BaudhŚS, 1, 8 655024_1]
upendhate carusthālīm | [BaudhŚS, 1, 8 655025_1]
adhyasyanti śrapaṇāni | [BaudhŚS, 1, 8 655026_1]
tapanti piṣṭa saṃyavanīyāḥ āpaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 1, 8 655027_1]
{BaudhŚS, 1, 9}
atha uttareṇa gārhapatyam upaviśya vācaṃyamaḥ tiras pavitram pātryām kṛṣṇājināt piṣṭāni saṃvapati devasya tvā savituḥ prasave aśvinoḥ bāhubhyām pūṣṇaḥ hastābhyām agnaye juṣṭam saṃvapāmi agnīṣomābhyām amuṣmai amuṣmai iti yathādevatam | [BaudhŚS, 1, 9 655028_1]
atha parikarmiṇam āha āhara apaḥ ānaya iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 9 655029_1]
āharati praiṣa kāraḥ praṇītābhyaḥ sruveṇa upahatya vedena upayamya pāṇim vā antardhāya | [BaudhŚS, 1, 9 655030_1]
evam madantībhyaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 1, 9 655031_1]
tāḥ ubhayīḥ ānīyamānāḥ pratimantrayate sam āpaḥ adbhiḥ agmata sam oṣadhayaḥ rasena sam revatīḥ jagatībhiḥ madhumatīḥ madhumatībhiḥ sṛjyadhvam iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 9 655032_1]
atha anupariplāvayati adbhyaḥ pari prajātāḥ stha sam adbhiḥ pṛcyadhvam iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 9 655033_1]
saṃyauti janayatyai tvā saṃyaumi iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 9 655034_1]
saṃyutya vyūhya abhimṛśati agnaye tvā agnīṣomābhyām amuṣmai amuṣmai iti yathādevatam | [BaudhŚS, 1, 9 655035_1]
piṇḍam karoti makhasya śiraḥ asi iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 9 655036_1]
tam dakṣiṇeṣām kapālānām pratyūhya aṅgārān teṣu adhipṛṇakti gharmaḥ asi viśva āyuḥ iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 9 655037_1]
prathayati uru prathasva uru te yajñapatiḥ prathatām iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 9 655038_1]
tam tanvantam kūrma prakāram karoti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 9 655039_1]
sarvāṇi kapālāni abhiprathayati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 9 655040_1]
iti brāhmaṇam | [BaudhŚS, 1, 9 655040_2]
{BaudhŚS, 1, 10}
atha tiras pavitram ājya sthālyām ājyam nirvapati mahīnām payaḥ asi oṣadhīnām rasaḥ tasya te a kṣīyamāṇasya nirvapāmi deva yajyāyai iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 10 655041_1]
atha uttaratas bhasma miśrān aṅgārān nirūhya teṣu adhiśrayati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 10 655042_1]
evam eva uttaram puroḍāśam adhipṛṇakti atha śṛtam atha dadhi | [BaudhŚS, 1, 10 655043_1]
atha pātryām apaḥ ānīya dakṣiṇasya puroḍāśasya tvacam grāhayati tvacam gṛhṇīṣva tvacam gṛhṇīṣva iti tris atha uttarasya | [BaudhŚS, 1, 10 655045_1]
atha paryagni karoti antaritam rakṣaḥ antaritāḥ arātayaḥ iti tris | [BaudhŚS, 1, 10 655047_1]
atha dakṣiṇam puroḍāśam śrapayati devaḥ tvā savitā śrapayatu varṣiṣṭhe adhi nāke agniḥ te tanuvam mā ati dhāk iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 10 655048_1]
gārhapatyam abhimantrayate agne havyam rakṣasva iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 10 655049_1]
evam eva uttaram puroḍāśam śrapayati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 10 655050_1]
atha dakṣiṇam puroḍāśam bhasmanā abhivāsya vedena abhivāsayati sam brahmaṇā pṛcyasva sam brahmaṇā pṛcyasva iti tris atha uttaram | [BaudhŚS, 1, 10 655051_1]
a vidahantaḥ śrapayata iti vācam visṛjate | [BaudhŚS, 1, 10 655053_1]
atra etat pātrī saṃkṣālanam gārhapatyāt aṅgāreṇa abhitapya hṛtvā antarvedi pratīcīnam tisṛṣu lekhāsu ninayati ekatāya svāhā dvitāya svāhā tritāya svāhā iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 10 655054_1]
atha vedam ādatte ayam vedaḥ pṛthivīm anvavindat guhā satīm gahane gahvareṣu sa vindatu yajamānāya lokam acchidram yajñam bhūri karmā karotu iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 10 655055_1]
vedena vedim tris saṃmārṣṭi vedena vedim vividuḥ pṛthivīm sā paprathe pṛthivī pārthivāni garbham bibharti bhuvaneṣu antar tatas yajñaḥ jāyate viśvadāniḥ iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 10 655056_1]
{BaudhŚS, 1, 11}
atha jaghanena vedyai tiṣṭhan sphyam ādatte devasya tvā savituḥ prasave aśvinoḥ bāhubhyām pūṣṇaḥ hastābhyām ādade iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 11 655057_1]
ādāya abhimantrayate indrasya bāhuḥ asi dakṣiṇaḥ sahasra bhṛṣṭiḥ śata tejāḥ iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 11 655058_1]
śata tejāḥ iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 11 655058_2]
atha enam barhiṣā saṃśyati vāyuḥ asi tigma tejāḥ śata bhṛṣṭiḥ asi vānaspatyaḥ dviṣataḥ vadhaḥ iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 11 655059_1]
atha antarvedi udīcīna agram barhiḥ nidadhāti pṛthivyai varma asi varma yajamānāya bhava iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 11 655060_1]
tasmin sphyena praharati pṛthivi deva yajani oṣadhyāḥ te mūlam mā hiṃsiṣam iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 11 655061_1]
apahataḥ araruḥ pṛthivyāḥ iti ādatte | [BaudhŚS, 1, 11 655062_1]
vrajam gaccha gosthānam iti harati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 11 655063_1]
vedim pratyavekṣate varṣatu te dyauḥ iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 11 655064_1]
hṛtvā utkare nivapati badhāna deva savitar paramasyām parāvati śatena pāśaiḥ yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam ca vayam dviṣmaḥ tam atas mā mauk iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 11 655065_1]
dvitīyam praharati pṛthivi deva yajani oṣadhyāḥ te mūlam mā hiṃsiṣam iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 11 655066_1]
apahataḥ araruḥ pṛthivyai deva yajanyai iti ādatte | [BaudhŚS, 1, 11 655067_1]
vrajam gaccha gosthānam iti harati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 11 655068_1]
vedim pratyavekṣate varṣatu te dyauḥ iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 11 655069_1]
hṛtvā utkare nivapati badhāna deva savitar paramasyām parāvati śatena pāśaiḥ yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam ca vayam dviṣmaḥ tam atas mā mauk iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 11 655070_1]
tṛtīyam praharati pṛthivi deva yajani oṣadhyāḥ te mūlam mā hiṃsiṣam iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 11 655071_1]
apahataḥ araruḥ pṛthivyāḥ a deva yajanaḥ iti ādatte | [BaudhŚS, 1, 11 655072_1]
vrajam gaccha gosthānam iti harati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 11 655073_1]
vedim pratyavekṣate varṣatu te dyauḥ iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 11 655074_1]
hṛtvā utkare nivapati badhāna deva savitar paramasyām parāvati śatena pāśaiḥ yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam ca vayam dviṣmaḥ tam atas mā mauk | [BaudhŚS, 1, 11 655075_1]
araruḥ te divam mā skān iti atra anuvartayati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 11 655075_2]
tūṣṇīm caturtham harati saha barhiṣā | [BaudhŚS, 1, 11 655076_1]
atha pūrvam parigrāham parigṛhṇāti vasavaḥ tvā parigṛhṇantu gāyatreṇa chandasā iti dakṣiṇatas rudrāḥ tvā parigṛhṇantu traiṣṭubhena chandasā iti paścāt ādityāḥ tvā parigṛhṇantu jāgatena chandasā iti uttaratas | [BaudhŚS, 1, 11 655077_1]
atha karaṇam japati imām narāḥ kṛṇuta vedim etya vasumatīm rudravatīm ādityavatīm divaḥ nābhau pṛthivyāḥ yathā ayam yajamānaḥ na riṣyet iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 11 655078_1]
atha prācīm sphyena vedim uddhanti devasya savituḥ save karma kṛṇvanti vedhasaḥ iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 11 655079_1]
atha āgnīdhram āha agnīdh itas tris hara iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 11 655080_1]
tatas tris āgnīdhraḥ harati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 11 655081_1]
yat āgnīdhraḥ tris harati atha saṃpraiṣam āha brahman uttaram parigrāham parigrahīṣyāmi iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 11 655082_1]
prasūtaḥ uttaram parigrāham parigṛhṇāti ṛtam asi iti dakṣiṇatas ṛta sadanam asi iti paścāt ṛta śrīḥ asi iti uttaratas | [BaudhŚS, 1, 11 655083_1]
atha pratīcīm sphyena vedim yoyupyate dhāḥ asi sva dhāḥ asi urvī ca asi vasvī ca asi purā krūrasya visṛpaḥ virapśin udādāya pṛthivīm jīra dānuḥ yām airayan candramasi svadhābhiḥ tām dhīrāsaḥ anudṛśya yajante iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 11 655084_1]
atha antarvedi tiryañcam sphyam stabdhvā saṃpraiṣam āha prokṣaṇīḥ āsādaya idhmābarhiḥ upasādaya sruvam ca srucaḥ ca saṃmṛḍḍhi patnīm saṃnahya ājyena udehi iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 11 655085_1]
āharanti etāḥ prokṣaṇīḥ abhipūrya | [BaudhŚS, 1, 11 655086_1]
dakṣiṇena adhvaryuḥ tāḥ sphye upaninīya sphyasya vartman sādayati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 11 655087_1]
atha utkare sphyam nihanti yaḥ mā hṛdā manasā yaḥ ca vācā yaḥ brahmaṇā karmaṇā dveṣṭi devāḥ yaḥ śrutena hṛdayena iṣṇatā ca tasya indra vajreṇa śiraḥ chinadmi iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 11 655088_1]
hastau prakṣālya sphyam ca prakṣālayati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 11 655089_1]
upasādayanti etat idhmābarhiḥ dakṣiṇam idhmam uttaram barhiḥ | [BaudhŚS, 1, 11 655090_1]
{BaudhŚS, 1, 12}
atha etāḥ srucaḥ samādatte dakṣiṇena sruvam juhū upabhṛtau savyena dhruvām prāśitraharaṇam veda parivāsanāni iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 12 655091_1]
gārhapatye pratitapati pratyuṣṭam rakṣaḥ pratyuṣṭāḥ arātayaḥ agneḥ vaḥ tejiṣṭhena tejasā niṣṭapāmi iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 12 655092_1]
atha sruvam saṃmārṣṭi goṣṭham mā nirmṛkṣam vājinam tvā sapatna sāham saṃmārjmi iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 12 655093_1]
tris antarataḥ tris bāhyatas | [BaudhŚS, 1, 12 655094_1]
tris evam mūlaiḥ daṇḍam saṃmṛjya adbhiḥ saṃsparśya pratitapya utprayacchati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 12 655094_2]
atha juhūm saṃmārṣṭi vācam prāṇam mā nirmṛkṣam vājinīm tvā sapatna sāhīm saṃmārjmi iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 12 655095_1]
tathā eva saṃmṛjya adbhiḥ saṃsparśya pratitapya utprayacchati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 12 655096_1]
atha upabhṛtam saṃmārṣṭi cakṣuḥ śrotram mā nirmṛkṣam vājinīm tvā sapatna sāhīm saṃmārjmi iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 12 655097_1]
tathā eva saṃmṛjya adbhiḥ saṃsparśya pratitapya utprayacchati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 12 655098_1]
atha dhruvām saṃmārṣṭi prajām yonim mā nirmṛkṣam vājinīm tvā sapatna sāhīm saṃmārjmi iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 12 655099_1]
tathā eva saṃmṛjya adbhiḥ saṃsparśya pratitapya utprayacchati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 12 655100_1]
atha prāśitraharaṇam saṃmārṣṭi rūpam varṇam paśubhyaḥ mā nirmṛkṣam vājinam tvā sapatna sāham saṃmārjmi iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 12 655101_1]
tathā eva saṃmṛjya adbhiḥ saṃsparśya pratitapya utprayacchati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 12 655102_1]
atha etāni sruc saṃmārjanāni adbhiḥ saṃsparśya gārhapatye anupraharati divaḥ śilpam avatatam pṛthivyāḥ kakudbhiḥ śritam tena vayam sahasra valśena sapatnam nāśayāmasi svāhā iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 12 655103_1]
atha agreṇa utkaram tṛṇāni saṃstīrya teṣu srucaḥ sādayitvā atha etām patnīm antareṇa vedi utkarau prapādya jaghanena dakṣiṇena gārhapatyam udīcīm upaveśya yoktreṇa saṃnahyati āśāsānā saumanasam prajām saubhāgyam tanūm agneḥ anuvratā bhūtvā saṃnahye sukṛtāya kam iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 12 655104_1]
atha enām vācayati yuktam āśīḥ kāme iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 12 655105_1]
atha enām tiras pavitram apaḥ ācāmayati payasvatīḥ oṣadhayaḥ payasvat vīrudhām payaḥ apām payasaḥ yat payaḥ tena mām indra saṃsṛja iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 12 655106_1]
atha enām gārhapatye samidhaḥ ādhāpayati agne vratapate vratam cariṣyāmi tat śakeyam tat me rādhyatām svāhā vāyo vrata pate āditya vrata pate vratānām vrata pate vratam cariṣyāmi tat śakeyam tat me rādhyatām svāhā iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 12 655107_1]
atha jaghanena gārhapatyam upasīdati su prajasaḥ tvā vayam su patnīḥ upasedima agne sapatna dambhanam adabdha aso adābhyam indrāṇī iva avidhavā bhūyāsam aditiḥ iva su putrā asthūri tvā suprajāstvāya mama putrāḥ śatru haṇaḥ atha u me duhitā virāj uta aham asmi saṃjayā patyuḥ me ślokaḥ uttamaḥ iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 12 655108_1]
atha enām vācayati ūne atiriktam dhīyātai iti ca | [BaudhŚS, 1, 12 655109_1]
atha enām gārhapatyam īkṣayati agne gṛhapate upa mā hvayasva devānām patnīḥ upa mā hvayadhvam patni patni eṣa te lokaḥ namaḥ te astu mā mā hiṃsīḥ iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 12 655110_1]
atha enām ājyam avekṣayati mahīnām payaḥ asi oṣadhīnām rasaḥ tvā cakṣuṣā avekṣe suprajāstvāya iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 12 655111_1]
atha enat gārhapatye adhiśrayati tejaḥ asi iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 12 655112_1]
samidham upayatya prāṅ harati tejaḥ anu prehi iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 12 655113_1]
atha enat āhavanīye adhiśrayati agniḥ te tejaḥ mā vinait iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 12 655114_1]
atra etām samidham madhyataḥ āhavanīyasya abhyādadhāti svāhā iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 12 655115_1]
atha enat agreṇa prokṣaṇīḥ paryāhṛtya dakṣiṇa ardhe vedyai nidhāya yajamānam ājyam avekṣayati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 12 655116_1]
nimīlya avekṣeta iti brāhmaṇam | [BaudhŚS, 1, 12 655116_2]
atha enat yathāhṛtam pratiparyāhṛtya uttara ardhe vedyai nidhāya adhvaryuḥ avekṣate agneḥ jihvā asi subhūḥ devānām dhāmne dhāmne devebhyaḥ yajuṣe yajuṣe bhava iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 12 655117_1]
atha enat udīcīna agrābhyām pavitrābhyām punar āhāram tris utpunāti śukram asi jyotiḥ asi tejaḥ asi iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 12 655118_1]
atha prokṣaṇīḥ utpunāti devaḥ vaḥ savitā utpunātu acchidreṇa pavitreṇa vasoḥ sūryasya raśmibhiḥ iti pacchas | [BaudhŚS, 1, 12 655119_1]
prokṣaṇīṣu pavitre avadhāya ādatte dakṣiṇena sruvam savyena juhūm | [BaudhŚS, 1, 12 655120_1]
vede pratiṣṭhāpya tasyām gṛhṇīte | [BaudhŚS, 1, 12 655120_2]
śukram tvā śukrāyām dhāmne dhāmne devebhyaḥ yajuṣe yajuṣe gṛhṇāmi iti etena yajuṣā caturgṛhītam gṛhītvā saṃmṛśya utprayacchati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 12 655120_3]
atha upabhṛti gṛhṇīte | [BaudhŚS, 1, 12 655121_1]
jyotiḥ tvā jyotiṣi dhāmne dhāmne devebhyaḥ yajuṣe yajuṣe gṛhṇāmi iti etena yajuṣā aṣṭa gṛhītam gṛhītvā bhūyasaḥ grahān gṛhṇānaḥ kanīyaḥ ājyam gṛhṇīte | [BaudhŚS, 1, 12 655121_2]
tathā eva saṃmṛśya utprayacchati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 12 655122_1]
atha dhruvāyām gṛhṇīte | [BaudhŚS, 1, 12 655123_1]
arciḥ tvā arciṣi dhāmne dhāmne devebhyaḥ yajuṣe yajuṣe gṛhṇāmi iti etena yajuṣā caturgṛhītam gṛhītvā abhipūrya tathā eva saṃmṛśya utprayacchati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 12 655123_2]
{BaudhŚS, 1, 13}
atha etām ājya sthālīm sa sruvām jaghanena vedyai nidhāya prokṣaṇīḥ unmahayan upottiṣṭhati āpaḥ devīḥ agrepuvaḥ agreguvaḥ agre imam yajñam nayatā agre yajñapatim dhatta yuṣmān indraḥ avṛṇīta vṛtratūrye yūyam indram avṛṇīdhvam vṛtratūrye iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 13 655124_1]
adbhiḥ eva apaḥ prokṣati prokṣitāḥ stha prokṣitāḥ stha iti tris | [BaudhŚS, 1, 13 655125_1]
atha idhmam visrasya prokṣati kṛṣṇaḥ asi ākhareṣṭhaḥ agnaye tvā svāhā iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 13 655126_1]
vedim prokṣati vediḥ asi barhiṣe tvā svāhā iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 13 655127_1]
barhiḥ prokṣati barhiḥ asi srugbhyaḥ tvā svāhā iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 13 655128_1]
āharanti etat barhiḥ antareṇa praṇītāḥ ca āhavanīyam ca | [BaudhŚS, 1, 13 655129_1]
tat antarvedi purogranthi āsādya prokṣati dive tvā iti agrāṇi antarikṣāya tvā iti madhyāni pṛthivyai tvā iti mūlāni | [BaudhŚS, 1, 13 655130_1]
saha srucā purastāt pratyañcam granthim pratyukṣya atiśiṣṭāḥ prokṣaṇīḥ ninayati dakṣiṇāyai śroṇeḥ ā uttarāyai śroṇeḥ svadhā pitṛbhyaḥ ūrj bhava barhiṣadbhyaḥ ūrjā pṛthivīm gacchata iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 13 655131_1]
udūhya prokṣaṇī dhānam barhiḥ visrasya purastāt prastaram gṛhṇāti viṣṇo stūpaḥ asi iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 13 655131_2]
tasmin pavitre apisṛjati yajamāne prāṇa apānau dadhāmi iti vā tūṣṇīm vā | [BaudhŚS, 1, 13 655132_1]
tam yajamānāya vā brahmaṇe vā prayacchati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 13 655133_1]
atha etāni barhiḥ saṃnahanāni āyātayati dakṣiṇāyai śroṇeḥ ā uttarāt aṃsāt | [BaudhŚS, 1, 13 655134_1]
atha dakṣiṇe vedi ante barhiḥ muṣṭim stṛṇāti deva barhiḥ ūrṇāmradasam tvā stṛṇāmi svāsastham devebhyaḥ iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 13 655135_1]
tām bahulām purastāt pratyañcam trivṛtam anatidṛśnam stṛṇāti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 13 655136_1]
atha prastara pāṇiḥ prāñc abhisṛpya paridhīn paridadhāti gandharvaḥ asi viśvāvasuḥ viśvāt īṣataḥ yajamānasya paridhiḥ iḍaḥ īḍitaḥ iti madhyamam indrasya bāhuḥ asi dakṣiṇaḥ yajamānasya paridhiḥ iḍaḥ īḍitaḥ iti dakṣiṇam mitrāvaruṇau tvā uttaratas paridhattām dhruveṇa dharmaṇā yajamānasya paridhiḥ iḍaḥ īḍitaḥ iti uttaram | [BaudhŚS, 1, 13 655137_1]
atha sūryeṇa purastāt paridadhāti sūryaḥ tvā purastāt pātu kasyāścid abhiśastyāḥ iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 13 655138_1]
ūrdhve samidhau ādadhāti vītihotram tvā kave dyumantam samidhīmahi agne bṛhantam adhvare iti dakṣiṇām tūṣṇīm uttarām | [BaudhŚS, 1, 13 655139_1]
abhyādhāya antarvedi udīcīna agre vidhṛtī tiryañcau sādayati viśaḥ yantre stha iti vidhṛtyoḥ prastaram vasūnām rudrāṇām ādityānām sadasi sīda iti prastare juhvam juhūḥ asi ghṛtāñc nāmnā priyeṇa nāmnā priye sadasi sīda iti uttarām upabhṛtam upabhṛt asi ghṛtāñc nāmnā priyeṇa nāmnā priye sadasi sīda iti uttarām dhruvām dhruvā asi ghṛtāñc nāmnā priyeṇa nāmnā priye sadasi sīda iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 13 655140_1]
atha srucaḥ sannāḥ abhimṛśati etāḥ asadan sukṛtasya loke tāḥ viṣṇo pāhi pāhi yajñam pāhi yajñapatim pāhi mām yajñanyam iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 13 655145_1]
atha viṣṇūni stha vaiṣṇavāni dhāmāni stha prājāpatyāni iti ājyāni abhimantrayate | [BaudhŚS, 1, 13 655146_1]
{BaudhŚS, 1, 14}
atha ādatte dakṣiṇena ājya sthālīm sa sruvām savyena pātrīm vedam iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 14 655147_1]
etat samādāya pradakṣiṇam āvṛtya pratyañc ādrutya jaghanena gārhapatyam upaviśya pātryām dvedhā upastṛṇīte syonam te sadanam karomi ghṛtasya dhārayā su śevam kalpayāmi tasmin sīda amṛte pratitiṣṭha vrīhīnām medhaiḥ sumanasyamānaḥ iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 14 655148_1]
atha dhṛṣṭim ādāya dakṣiṇasya puroḍāśasya aṅgārān apohati idam aham senāyai _ mukham apohāmi iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 14 655149_1]
atha enam vidarśayati sūrya jyotiḥ vibhāhi mahate indriyāya iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 14 655150_1]
vedena virajasam kṛtvā abhighārayati āpyāyatām ghṛta yoniḥ agniḥ havyāni anumanyatām kham aṅkṣva tvacam aṅkṣva surūpam tvā vasu vidam paśūnām tejasā agnaye juṣṭam abhighārayāmi iti yad devatyaḥ _ bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 14 655151_1]
atha enam udvāsayati śṛtaḥ utsnāti janitā matīnām iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 14 655153_1]
ājyena su saṃtarpayati ārdraḥ prathasnuḥ bhuvanasya gopaḥ iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 14 655154_1]
upariṣṭāt abhyajya adhastāt upānakti yaḥ te ātmā paśuṣu praviṣṭaḥ tam aṅkṣva iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 14 655155_1]
evam eva uttaram puroḍāśam udvāsayati atha śṛtam atha dadhi | [BaudhŚS, 1, 14 655156_1]
atha sāṃnāyye alaṃkaroti yaḥ te ātmā paśuṣu praviṣṭaḥ devānām viṣṭhām _ yaḥ vitasthe ātmanvān somaiḥ ghṛtavān hi bhūtvā devān gaccha svar yajamānāya me iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 14 655158_1]
pratyajya kapālāni udvāsayati irā bhūtiḥ pṛthivyai rasaḥ mā utkramīt iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 14 655159_1]
saṃkhyāya udvāsayati yajamānasya gopīthāya iti brāhmaṇam | [BaudhŚS, 1, 14 655160_1]
atha enam sruvam ājyasya pūrayitvā antareṇa puroḍāśau avadadhāti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 14 655161_1]
atha enā samparigṛhya antarvedi āsādayati bhūḥ bhuvar svar iti etābhiḥ vyāhṛtibhiḥ | [BaudhŚS, 1, 14 655162_1]
madhyatas puroḍāśau āsādayati dakṣiṇatas śṛtam uttaratas dadhi | [BaudhŚS, 1, 14 655163_1]
atha enam sruvam agreṇa srucaḥ paryāhṛtya dakṣiṇena juhvam prastare sādayati syonaḥ me sīda suṣadaḥ pṛthivyām prathayi prajayā paśubhiḥ suvarge loke divi sīda pṛthivyām antarikṣe aham uttaraḥ bhūyāsam adharāḥ mat sapatnāḥ iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 14 655164_1]
atha enam yathāhṛtam pratiparyāhṛtya dhruvāyām avadadhāti ṛṣabhaḥ asi śākvaraḥ ghṛtācīnām sūnuḥ priyeṇa nāmnā priye sadasi sīda iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 14 655165_1]
{BaudhŚS, 1, 15}
athedhmāt samidham ādadāna āha agnaye samidhyamānāyānubrūhīti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 15 1]
atha yatra hotur abhijānāti pra vo vājā abhidyava iti tatprathamām abhyādadhāti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 15 2]
praṇave praṇave 'bhyādadhāti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 15 3]
atha yatra hotur abhijānāti samiddho agna āhuta iti tadantato 'bhyādadhāti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 15 4]
pari samidhaṃ śinaṣṭi | [BaudhŚS, 1, 15 5]
atha yatra hotur abhijānāti ājuhotā duvasyata iti tad etena vedena trir āhavanīyam upavājayati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 15 6]
anūktāsu sāmidhenīṣu dhruvājyāt sruveṇopahatya vedenopayamya prājāpatyaṃ tiryañcam āghāram āghārayati prajāpataye svāheti manasā | [BaudhŚS, 1, 15 7]
atha saṃpraiṣam āhāgnīdagnīṃs tristriḥ saṃmṛḍḍhīti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 15 8]
athaiṣa āgnīdhra idhmasaṃnahanāni sphya upasaṃgṛhya paridhīn saṃmārṣṭi trir madhyamaṃ trir dakṣiṇārdhyaṃ trir uttarārdhyaṃ trir āhavanīyam upavājayaty agne vājajid vājaṃ tvāgne sariṣyantaṃ vājaṃ jeṣyantaṃ vājinaṃ vājajitaṃ vājajityāyai saṃmārjmy agnim annādam annādyāyeti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 15 9]
athāgreṇa juhūpabhṛtau prāñcam añjaliṃ karoti bhuvanam asi viprathasvāgne yaṣṭar idaṃ nama iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 15 10]
athādatte dakṣiṇena juhūm juhv ehi agnis tvā hvayati devayajyāyā iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 15 11]
savyenopabhṛtam upabhṛd ehi devas tvā savitā hvayati devayajyāyā iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 15 12]
savyenātyākrāmañ japaty agnāviṣṇū mā vām avakramiṣaṃ vijihāthāṃ mā mā saṃtāptaṃ lokaṃ me lokakṛtau kṛṇutam iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 15 13]
sthānaṃ kalpayate viṣṇo sthānam asīti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 15 14]
anvārabdhe yajamāne madhyame paridhau saṃsparśyarjum āghāram āghārayati saṃtataṃ prāñcam avyavacchindan ita indro akṛṇod vīryāṇi samārabhyordhvo adhvaro divispṛśam ahruto yajño yajñapater indrāvānt svāheti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 15 15]
bṛhad bhā iti srucam udgṛhṇāti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 15 16]
athāsaṃsparśayan srucāv udaṅṅ atyākrāmañ japati pāhi māgne duścaritāt ā mā sucarite bhajeti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 15 17]
juhvā dhruvāṃ samanakti makhasya śiro 'si saṃ jyotiṣā jyotir aṅktām iti triḥ | [BaudhŚS, 1, 15 18]
atha yathāyatanaṃ srucau sādayitvā pravaraṃ pravṛṇīte | [BaudhŚS, 1, 15 19]
utkara idhmasaṃnahanāni sphya upasaṃgṛhya pṛṣṭham āgnīdhro 'nūpaśliṣyati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 15 20]
athāśrāvayaty o śrāvaya astu śrauṣaṭ agnir devo hotā devān yakṣad vidvāṃś cikitvān manuṣvad bharatavad amuvad amuvat brahmaṇvad eha vakṣat brāhmaṇā asya yajñasya prāvitāra iti asau mānuṣa iti hotur nāma gṛhṇāti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 15 21]
upotthāya hotā vimuñcati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 15 22]
vimukto 'dhvaryur upaviśati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 15 23]
prasavam ākāṅkṣann āste | [BaudhŚS, 1, 15 24]
{BaudhŚS, 1, 16}
atha yatra hotur abhijānāti ghṛtavatīm adhvaryo srucam āsyasveti taj juhūpabhṛtāv ādāyātyākramyāśrāvyāha samidho yajeti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 16 1]
vaṣaṭkṛte juhoti yaja yajeti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 16 2]
caturthaṃ yakṣyann ardham aupabhṛtasyājyasya juhvāṃ samānayate | [BaudhŚS, 1, 16 3]
pañca prayājān iṣṭvodaṅṅ atyākramya saṃsrāveṇānupūrvaṃ havīṃṣy abhighārayati dhruvām evāgre 'tha dakṣiṇaṃ puroḍāśam atha dhruvām athottaraṃ puroḍāśam atha śṛtam atha dadhy upabhṛtam antataḥ | [BaudhŚS, 1, 16 4]
atha catura ājyasya gṛhṇāna āhāgnaye 'nubrūhīti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 16 5]
atyākramyāśrāvyāhāgniṃ yajeti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 16 6]
vaṣaṭkṛta uttarārdhapūrvārdhe pratimukhaṃ prabāhug juhoti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 16 7]
athodaṅṅ atyākramya catura evājyasya gṛhṇāna āha somāyānubrūhīti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 16 8]
atyākramyāśrāvyāha somaṃ yajeti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 16 9]
vaṣaṭkṛte dakṣiṇārdhapūrvārdhe pratimukhaṃ prabāhug juhoti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 16 10]
athopastīrya dakṣiṇasya puroḍāśasya pūrvārdhād avadyann āha agnaye 'nubrūhīti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 16 11]
athainam upatiṣṭhate mā bher mā saṃvikthā mā tvā hiṃsiṣam mā te tejo 'pakramīd iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 16 12]
athainam abhimṛśati bharatam uddharem anuṣiñca avadānāni te pratyavadāsyāmi namas te 'stu mā mā hiṃsīr iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 16 13]
pūrvārdhād avadāyāparārdhād avadyati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 16 14]
abhighārayati pratyanakti yad avadānāni te 'vadyan vilomākārṣam ātmana ājyena pratyanajmy enat tat ta āpyāyatāṃ punar iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 16 15]
atyākramyāśrāvyāhāgniṃ yajeti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 16 16]
vaṣaṭkṛte juhoti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 16 17]
atha catura ājyasya gṛhṇāna āha prajāpataya ity upāṃśu anubrūhīty uccaiḥ | [BaudhŚS, 1, 16 18]
atyākramyāśrāvyāha prajāpatim ity upāṃśu yajety uccaiḥ | [BaudhŚS, 1, 16 19]
vaṣaṭkṛte juhoti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 16 20]
athopastīryottarasya puroḍāśasyāparārdhād avadyann āhāgnīṣomābhyām iti paurṇamāsyām indrāya vaimṛdhāyeti ca indrāgnibhyām ity amāvāsyāyām asaṃnayata indrāyeti saṃnayato mahendrāyeti vā yadi mahendrayājī bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 16 21]
{BaudhŚS, 1, 17}
samāna upasthānaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 1, 17 1]
samāno 'bhimarśanaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 1, 17 2]
aparārdhād avadāya pūrvārdhād avadyati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 17 3]
abhighārayati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 17 4]
samānaḥ pratyañjanaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 1, 17 5]
atyākramyāśrāvyāhāgnīṣomau yajeti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 17 6]
vaṣaṭkṛte juhoti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 17 7]
athopastīrya dviḥ puroḍāśasyāvadyann āhendrāyānubrūhīti mahendrāyeti vā yadi mahendrayājī bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 17 8]
dviḥ puroḍāśasyāvadyati dviḥ śṛtasya dvir dadhnaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 1, 17 9]
abhighārayati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 17 10]
pratyanakti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 17 11]
atyākramyāśrāvyāhendraṃ yajeti mahendram iti vā yadi mahendrayājī bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 17 12]
vaṣaṭkṛte juhoti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 17 13]
athopastīrya dakṣiṇasya puroḍāśasyottarārdhād avadyann āhāgnaye sviṣṭakṛte 'nubrūhīti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 17 14]
sakṛd dakṣiṇasya puroḍāśasyottarārdhād avadyati sakṛd dhruvājyāt sakṛd uttarasya puroḍāśasya sakṛcchṛtasya sakṛd dadhnaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 1, 17 15]
dvir abhighārayati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 17 16]
na pratyanakti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 17 17]
avatte sviṣṭakṛti sruveṇa pārvaṇau homau juhoty ṛṣabhaṃ vājinaṃ vayam pūrṇamāsaṃ yajāmahe sa no dohatāṃ suvīryam rāyaspoṣaṃ sahasriṇaṃ prāṇāya surādhase pūrṇamāsāya svāheti paurṇamāsyām | [BaudhŚS, 1, 17 18]
amāvāsyā subhagā suśevā dhenur iva bhūya āpyāyamānā sā no dohatāṃ suvīryam rāyaspoṣaṃ sahasriṇam apānāya surādhase 'māvāsyāyai svāhety amāvāsyāyām | [BaudhŚS, 1, 17 19]
atyākramyāśrāvyāhāgniṃ sviṣṭakṛtaṃ yajeti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 17 20]
vaṣaṭkṛta uttarārdhapūrvārdhe 'tihāya pūrvā āhutīr juhoti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 17 21]
atraitan mekṣaṇam āhavanīye 'nupraharati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 17 22]
athainat saṃsrāveṇābhijuhoti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 17 23]
athodaṅṅ atyākramya juhvām apa ānīya saṃkṣālanam antaḥparidhi ninayati vaiśvānare havir idaṃ juhomi sāhasram utsaṃ śatadhāram etaṃ sa naḥ pitaraṃ pitāmahaṃ prapitāmaham suvarge loke gacchatu pinvamānaṃ svadhā nama iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 17 24]
nirṇijya srucaṃ niṣṭapyādbhiḥ pūrayitvā bahiḥparidhi ninayatīmaṃ samudraṃ śatadhāram utsam vyacyamānaṃ bhuvanasya madhye ghṛtaṃ duhānām aditiṃ janāyāgne mā hiṃsīḥ parame vyoman iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 17 25]
atraitad aupabhṛtam ājyaṃ sarvaśa eva juhvāṃ samānayate | [BaudhŚS, 1, 17 26]
atha yathāyatanaṃ srucau sādayitvā prāśitram avadyati dakṣiṇasya puroḍāśasyottarārdhād yavamātram ajyāyo yavamātrād āvyādhāt kṛtyatām idaṃ mā rūrupāma yajñasya śuddhaṃ sviṣṭam idaṃ havir iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 17 27]
athainat sruvadaṇḍenābhighārya jaghanena praṇītāḥ sādayitvādbhiḥ sruvadaṇḍaṃ saṃsparśyāvadadhāti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 17 28]
{BaudhŚS, 1, 18}
atha kaṃsaṃ vā camasaṃ veḍopahavanaṃ yācati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 18 1]
tam antarvedi nidhāya tasminn upastīrya dakṣiṇasya puroḍāśasya dakṣiṇārdhāt prarujyāvadadhāti manunā dṛṣṭāṃ ghṛtapadīm mitrāvaruṇasamīritāṃ dakṣiṇārdhād asaṃbhindan avadyāmy ekatomukhām iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 18 2]
dvitīyam avadānāni saṃbhidyāvadadhāti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 18 3]
atha dakṣiṇasyaiva puroḍāśasya pūrvārdhāt tryaṅgulaṃ vā caturaṅgulaṃ vājyena susaṃtṛptaṃ saṃtarpyāgreṇa dhruvāṃ yajamānabhāgaṃ nidadhāti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 18 4]
dvir dhruvājyād avadyati dvir uttarasya puroḍāśasya dviḥ śṛtasya dvir dadhnaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 1, 18 5]
abhighārayati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 18 6]
atha hotur dvir aṅgulāv anakti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 18 7]
jighreṇa bhakṣayitvā | [BaudhŚS, 1, 18 8]
caturavāntareḍām avadyati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 18 9]
upastṛṇāti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 18 10]
dvir ādadhāti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 18 11]
abhighārayati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 18 12]
samanvārabhante 'dhvaryuś ca yajamānaś ca brahmā cāgnīdhraś ca | [BaudhŚS, 1, 18 13]
atha yatra hotur abhijānāti daivyā adhvaryava upahūtā upahūtā manuṣyā iti tad dakṣiṇaṃ puroḍāśaṃ caturdhā kṛtvā barhiṣadaṃ karoti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 18 14]
atha yatra hotur abhijānāty upahūto 'yaṃ yajamāna iti tarhi yajamāno hotāram īkṣamāṇo vāyuṃ manasā dhyāyed iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 18 15]
upahūtāyām iḍāyām agnīdha ādadhāti ṣaḍavattam | [BaudhŚS, 1, 18 16]
upastṛṇāty ādadhāty abhighārayaty upastṛṇāty ādadhāty abhighārayati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 18 17]
prāśnanti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 18 18]
mārjayante | [BaudhŚS, 1, 18 19]
athāha brahmaṇe prāśitraṃ parihareti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 18 20]
pari prāśitraṃ haranti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 18 21]
anv apo 'nu vedena brahmabhāgam | [BaudhŚS, 1, 18 22]
athānvāhāryaṃ yācati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 18 23]
udvāsayanty etaddhavirucchiṣṭam | [BaudhŚS, 1, 18 24]
{BaudhŚS, 1, 19}
atha saṃpraiṣam āha brahman prasthāsyāmaḥ samidham ādhāyāgnīd agnīn sakṛtsakṛt saṃmṛḍḍhīti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 19 1]
prasūto 'traitāṃ samidhaṃ madhyata āhavanīyasyābhyādadhāti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 19 2]
athaiṣa āgnīdhro 'sphyair evedhmasaṃnahanaiḥ paridhīn saṃmārṣṭi sakṛn madhyaṃ sakṛd dakṣiṇārdhyaṃ sakṛd uttarārdhyam | [BaudhŚS, 1, 19 3]
sakṛd āhavanīyam upavājayaty agne vājajid vājaṃ tvāgne sasṛvāṃsaṃ vājaṃ jigivāṃsaṃ vājinaṃ vājajitaṃ vājajityāyai saṃmārjmy agnim annādam annādyāyeti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 19 4]
athaitānīdhmasaṃnahanāny adbhiḥ saṃsparśyāhavanīye 'nupraharati yo bhūtānām adhipatī rudras tanticaro vṛṣā paśūn asmākaṃ mā hiṃsīr etad astu hutaṃ tava svāheti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 19 5]
atha juhūpabhṛtāv ādāyātyākramyāśrāvyāha devān yajeti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 19 6]
vaṣaṭkṛte juhoti yaja yajeti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 19 7]
trīn pratīco 'nūyājān yajati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 19 8]
prācāntataḥ sambhinatti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 19 9]
athodaṅṅ atyākramya yathāyatanaṃ srucau sādayitvā vājavatībhyāṃ srucau vyūhati vājasya mā prasavena udgrābheṇodagrabhīditi | [BaudhŚS, 1, 19 10]
dakṣiṇena juhūm udgṛhṇāti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 19 11]
athā sapatnāṁ indro me nigrābheṇādharāṁ akar iti savyenopabhṛtaṃ nigṛhṇāti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 19 12]
udgrābhaṃ ca nigrābhaṃ ca brahma devā avīvṛdhan iti prācīṃ juhūm ūhati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 19 13]
athā sapatnān indrāgnī me viṣūcīnān vyasyatām iti pratīcīm upabhṛtaṃ pratyūhati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 19 14]
prācyā paridhīn anakti vasubhyas tveti madhyamam rudrebhyas tveti dakṣiṇam ādityebhyas tvety uttaram | [BaudhŚS, 1, 19 15]
athopabhṛtam adbhiḥ saṃsparśya yathāyatanaṃ srucau sādayitvā srukṣu prastaram anakti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 19 16]
aktaṃ rihāṇā iti juhvām agrāṇi viyantu vaya ity upabhṛti madhyāni prajāṃ yoniṃ mā nirmṛkṣam iti dhruvāyāṃ mūlāni | [BaudhŚS, 1, 19 17]
atha prastarāt tṛṇaṃ pracchidya juhvām avadadhāti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 19 18]
athāśrāvayaty o śrāvayāstu śrauṣaḍ iṣitā daivyā hotāro bhadravācyāya preṣito mānuṣaḥ sūktavākāya sūktā brūhīti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 19 19]
tam uparīva prāñcaṃ praharati nāty agraṃ praharati na purastāt pratyasyati na pratiśṛṇāti na viṣvañcaṃ viyauty ūrdhvam udyauti āpyāyantām āpa oṣadhayo marutāṃ pṛṣataya stha divaṃ gaccha tato no vṛṣṭim erayeti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 19 20]
athāgnīdhram īkṣate 'gnīditi | [BaudhŚS, 1, 19 22]
tam āhāgnīdhraḥ saṃvadasveti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 19 23]
agan agnīd ity āhādhvaryuḥ | [BaudhŚS, 1, 19 24]
agan ity āhāgnīdhraḥ | [BaudhŚS, 1, 19 25]
śrāvayety āhādhvaryuḥ | [BaudhŚS, 1, 19 26]
śrauṣaḍity āhāgnīdhraḥ | [BaudhŚS, 1, 19 27]
idaṃ brūhīty āhādhvaryuḥ | [BaudhŚS, 1, 19 28]
anupraharety āhāgnīdhraḥ | [BaudhŚS, 1, 19 29]
anupraharati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 19 30]
svagā daivyā hotṛbhyaḥ svastir mānuṣebhyaḥ śaṃyor brūhīti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 19 31]
athopotthāyāhavanīyam upatiṣṭhate āyuṣpā agne 'sy āyur me pāhi cakṣuṣpā agne 'si cakṣur me pāhīti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 19 32]
athemām abhimṛśati dhruvāsīti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 19 33]
madhyamaṃ paridhim anupraharati yaṃ paridhiṃ paryadhatthā agne deva paṇibhir vīyamāṇas taṃ ta etam anu joṣaṃ bharāmi ned eṣa tvad apacetayātā iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 19 34]
athetarāv upasamasyati yajñasya pātha upa samitam iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 19 35]
athainān saṃsrāveṇābhijuhoti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 19 36]
juhvām upabhṛtaṃ saṃprasrāvayati saṃsrāvabhāgā stheṣā bṛhantaḥ prastareṣṭhā barhiṣadaś ca devā imāṃ vācam abhi viśve gṛṇanta āsadyāsmin barhiṣi mādayadhvaṃ svāheti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 19 37]
atha pradakṣiṇam āvṛtya pratyaṅṅ ādrutya dhuri srucau vimuñcaty agner vām apannagṛhasya sadasi sādayāmi sumnāya sumninī sumne mā dhattam dhuri dhuryau pātam iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 19 38]
yady u vai nāno bhavaty utkara evaine sphye vimuñcaty etenaiva mantreṇa | [BaudhŚS, 1, 19 39]
{BaudhŚS, 1, 20}
athādatte dakṣiṇenājyasthālīṃ sasruvāṃ savyena juhūṃ hotre vedaṃ pradāya | [BaudhŚS, 1, 20 1]
pradakṣiṇam āvṛtya pratyañcāv ādravataḥ | [BaudhŚS, 1, 20 2]
dakṣiṇenādhvaryur gārhapatyaṃ parikrāmaty uttareṇa hotā | [BaudhŚS, 1, 20 3]
tau jaghanena gārhapatyaṃ paścāt prāñcāv upaviśato dakṣiṇa evādhvaryur uttaro hotā | [BaudhŚS, 1, 20 4]
athādhvaryur vedam upabhṛtaṃ kṛtvā catura ājyasya gṛhṇāna āha somāyety upāṃśv anubrūhīty uccaiḥ | [BaudhŚS, 1, 20 5]
āśrāvyāha somam ity upāṃśu yajety uccaiḥ | [BaudhŚS, 1, 20 6]
vaṣaṭkṛte juhoti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 20 7]
catura evājyasya gṛhṇāna āha tvaṣṭra ity upāṃśv anubrūhīty uccaiḥ | [BaudhŚS, 1, 20 8]
āśrāvyāha tvaṣṭāram ity upāṃśu yajety uccaiḥ | [BaudhŚS, 1, 20 9]
vaṣaṭkṛte juhoti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 20 10]
catura evājyasya gṛhṇāna āha devānāṃ patnībhya ity upāṃśv anubrūhīty uccaiḥ | [BaudhŚS, 1, 20 11]
āśrāvyāha devānāṃ patnīr ity upāṃśu yajety uccaiḥ | [BaudhŚS, 1, 20 12]
vaṣaṭkṛte pariśrite devānāṃ patnīr juhoti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 20 13]
atha catura evājyasya gṛhṇāna āhāgnaye gṛhapataya ity upāṃśv anubrūhīty uccaiḥ | [BaudhŚS, 1, 20 14]
āśrāvyāhāgniṃ gṛhapatim ity upāṃśu yajety uccaiḥ | [BaudhŚS, 1, 20 15]
vaṣaṭkṛta uttarārdhapūrvārdhe 'tihāya pūrvā āhutīr juhoti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 20 16]
athāgreṇa hotāram upātītya hotur dvir aṅgulāv anakti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 20 17]
jighreṇa bhakṣayitvā | [BaudhŚS, 1, 20 18]
caturhasteḍāṃ sampādayaty ājyasyaiva | [BaudhŚS, 1, 20 19]
samanvārabhete adhvaryuś caiva patnī ca | [BaudhŚS, 1, 20 20]
upahūtāyām iḍāyām agnīdha ādadhāti ṣaḍavattam | [BaudhŚS, 1, 20 21]
prāśnītaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 1, 20 22]
mārjayete | [BaudhŚS, 1, 20 23]
atha sruci caturgṛhītaṃ gṛhītvāpasalaiḥ paryāvṛtyānvāhāryapacane prāyaścittaṃ juhoty ulūkhale musale yac ca śūrpe āśiśleṣa dṛṣadi yat kapāle 'vapruṣo vipruṣaḥ saṃyajāmi viśve devā havir idaṃ juṣantām yajñe yā vipruṣaḥ santi bahvīr agnau tāḥ sarvāḥ sviṣṭāḥ sahutā juhomi svāheti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 20 24]
aparaṃ caturgṛhītaṃ gṛhītvānvāhāryapacana evedhmapravraścanāny abhyādhāya phalīkaraṇān opya phalīkaraṇahomaṃ juhoty agne 'dabdhāyo 'śītatano pāhi mādya divaḥ pāhi prasityai pāhi duriṣṭyai pāhi duradmanyai pāhi duścaritād aviṣaṃ naḥ pituṃ kṛṇu suṣadā yoniṃ svāheti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 20 25]
athaitenaiva yathetam etya vede yajamānaṃ vācayati vedo 'si vittir asīty āntād anuvākasya hotre vedaṃ pradāya patnīṃ viṣyatīmaṃ viṣyāmi varuṇasya pāśam yam abadhnīta savitā suketaḥ dhātuś ca yonau sukṛtasya loke syonaṃ me saha patyā karomīti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 20 26]
athāsyai yoktram añjalāv ādhāyodapātram ānayati sam āyuṣā saṃ prajayā sam agne varcasā punaḥ saṃ patnī patyāhaṃ gacche sam ātmā tanuvā mamety atha mukhaṃ vimṛṣṭe yad apsu te sarasvati goṣv aśveṣu yan madhu tena me vājinīvati mukham sarasvatīti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 20 27]
apo ninayaty avabhṛthasyaiva rūpaṃ kṛtvottiṣṭhatīti brāhmaṇam | [BaudhŚS, 1, 20 28]
{BaudhŚS, 1, 21}
athaināṃ tathaiva tiraḥ pavitram apa ācāmayati payasvatīr oṣadhayaḥ payasvad vīrudhāṃ payo 'pāṃ payaso yat payas tena mām indra saṃsṛjeti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 21 1]
athaināṃ gārhapatye samidha ādhāpayaty agne vratapate vratam acāriṣam tad aśakam tan me 'rādhi svāhā vāyo vratapata āditya vratapate vratānāṃ vratapate vratam acāriṣam tad aśakam tan me 'rādhi svāheti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 21 2]
atha yathāprapannaṃ niṣkrāmayati | [BaudhŚS, 1, 21 3]
atha prāṅ etya dhruvām āpyāyayaty āpyāyatāṃ dhruvā ghṛtena yajñaṃ yajñaṃ prati devayadbhyaḥ sūryāyā ūdho 'dityā upasthe urudhārā pṛthivī yajñe asmin iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 21 4]
athājyasthālyāḥ sruveṇopaghātaṃ prāyaścittāni juhoty āśrāvitam atyāśrāvitam vaṣaṭkṛtam atyanūktaṃ ca yajñe 'tiriktaṃ karmaṇo yac ca hīnaṃ yajñaḥ parvāṇi pratirann eti kalpayan svāhākṛtāhutir etu devānt svāheti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 21 5]
atha yajñasamṛddhīr juhotīṣṭebhyaḥ svāhā vaṣaḍ aniṣṭebhyaḥ svāhā bheṣajaṃ duriṣṭyai svāhā niṣkṛtyai svāhā daurārddhyai svāhā daivībhyas tanūbhyaḥ svāhā ṛddhyai svāhā samṛddhyai svāhā sarvasamṛddhyai svāhā bhūḥ svāhā bhuvaḥ svāhā suvaḥ svāhā bhūr bhuvaḥ suvaḥ svāhā imaṃ me varuṇa tat tvā yāmi tvaṃ no agne sa tvaṃ no agne tvam agne ayāsi ayā san manasā hito 'yā san havyam ūhiṣe ayā no dhehi bheṣajaṃ svāhā ayāś cāgne 'sy anabhiśastīś ca satyam it tvam ayā asy ayasā manasā dhṛto ayasā havam ūhiṣe ayā no dhehi bheṣajaṃ svāhā yad asmin karmaṇy antar agāma mantrataḥ karmato vānayāhutyā tacchamayāmi sarvam tṛpyantu devā āvṛṣantāṃ ghṛtena svāhā yad asya karmaṇo 'tyarīricam yad vā nyūnam ihākaram agniṣ ṭat sviṣṭakṛd vidvān sarvaṃ sviṣṭaṃ suhutaṃ karotu me 'gnaye sviṣṭakṛte suhutahuta āhutīnāṃ kāmānāṃ samardhayitre svāhā prajāpate na tvad etāny anyo viśvā jātāni pari tā babhūva yatkāmās te juhumas tan no astu vayaṃ syāma patayo rayīṇāṃ svāheti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 21 6]
atha barhiṣo dhātūnāṃ sampralupya dhruvāyāṃ samanakti samaṅktāṃ barhir haviṣā ghṛtena sam ādityair vasubhiḥ saṃ marudbhiḥ sam indreṇa viśvebhir devebhir aṅktām iti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 21 7]
athainad āhavanīye 'nupraharati divyaṃ nabho gacchatu yat svāheti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 21 8]
athopotthāya dakṣiṇena padā vedim avakramya dhruvayā samiṣṭayajur juhoti devā gātuvido gātuṃ vittvā gātum ita manasaspata imaṃ no deva deveṣu yajñaṃ svāhā vāci svāhā vāte dhāḥ svāheti | [BaudhŚS, 1, 21 9]
udūhati srucam | [BaudhŚS, 1, 21 10]
ninayati praṇītāḥ | [BaudhŚS, 1, 21 11]
upotthāya yajamāno dakṣiṇena padā viṣṇukramān kramate | [BaudhŚS, 1, 21 12]
saṃtiṣṭhata āmāvāsyaṃ vā paurṇamāsyaṃ vā haviḥ | [BaudhŚS, 1, 21 13]
{BaudhŚS, 2, 1}
athopavyāharaṇam | [BaudhŚS, 2, 1 1]
vijñāyate kratvādau kratukāmaṃ kāmayīta yajñāṅgādau yajñāṅgakāmam iti | [BaudhŚS, 2, 1 2]
prāktūlān darbhān saṃstīrya teṣu prāṅmukho yajamāna upaviśya japati yāḥ purastāt prasravanty upariṣṭāt sarvataś ca yāḥ ābhī raśmipavitrābhiḥ śraddhāṃ yajñam ārabhe devā gātuvido gātuṃ yajñāya vindata manasaspatinā devena vātād yajñaḥ prayujyatām iti śraddha ehi satyena tvāhvayāmīti | [BaudhŚS, 2, 1 3]
ākūtyā vedanaṃ karoty ākūtyai tvā kāmāya tvā samṛdhe tvā puro dadhe amṛtatvāya jīvase | [BaudhŚS, 2, 1 4]
ākūtim asyāvase kāmam asya samṛddhyā indrasya yuñjate dhiyaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 2, 1 5]
ākūtiṃ devīṃ manasaḥ puro dadhe yajñasya mātā suhavā me astu yad icchāmi manasā sakāmo videyam enaddhṛdaye niviṣṭam iti | [BaudhŚS, 2, 1 6]
manasā triḥ saṃkalpayate trir uccaiḥ | [BaudhŚS, 2, 1 7]
sarvakāmo 'gnīn ādhāsya ity agnyādheye | [BaudhŚS, 2, 1 8]
svargakāmo darśapūrṇamāsābhyāṃ yakṣya iti darśapūrṇamāsayoḥ | [BaudhŚS, 2, 1 9]
svargakāmaś cāturmāsyair yakṣya iti cāturmāsyeṣu | [BaudhŚS, 2, 1 10]
svargakāmaḥ paśunā yakṣya iti paśubandhe | [BaudhŚS, 2, 1 11]
svargakāmaḥ somena yakṣya iti some | [BaudhŚS, 2, 1 12]
svargakāmo 'gniṃ ceṣya ity agnicaye | [BaudhŚS, 2, 1 13]
ahīne 'hargaṇe vā yathākāmo yatkāmo vā yajate | [BaudhŚS, 2, 1 14]
tan ma ṛdhyatāṃ tan me samṛdhyatāṃ tan me saṃpadyatāṃ kāma iti | [BaudhŚS, 2, 1 15]
athartvijāṃ prativacanaṃ tat ta ṛdhyatāṃ tat te samṛdhyatāṃ tat te saṃpadyatāṃ kāma iti | [BaudhŚS, 2, 1 16]
oṃ tatheti prativacanam | [BaudhŚS, 2, 1 17]
{BaudhŚS, 2, 2}
athartvijo devayajanaṃ yācate | [BaudhŚS, 2, 2 1]
adhvaryo devayajanaṃ me dehīty adhvaryum | [BaudhŚS, 2, 2 2]
ādityo devo daivo 'dhvaryuḥ sa te devayajanaṃ dadātviti | [BaudhŚS, 2, 2 3]
oṃ tatheti prativacanam | [BaudhŚS, 2, 2 4]
brahman devayajanaṃ me dehīti brahmāṇam | [BaudhŚS, 2, 2 5]
candramā devo daivo brahmā sa te devayajanaṃ dadātviti | [BaudhŚS, 2, 2 6]
oṃ tatheti prativacanam | [BaudhŚS, 2, 2 7]
hotar devayajanaṃ me dehīti hotāram | [BaudhŚS, 2, 2 8]
agnir devo daivo hotā sa te devayajanaṃ dadātviti | [BaudhŚS, 2, 2 9]
oṃ tatheti prativacanam | [BaudhŚS, 2, 2 10]
udgātar devayajanaṃ me dehīty udgātāram | [BaudhŚS, 2, 2 11]
parjanyo devo daiva udgātā sa te devayajanaṃ dadātviti | [BaudhŚS, 2, 2 12]
oṃ tatheti prativacanam | [BaudhŚS, 2, 2 13]
sadasya devayajanaṃ me dehīti sadasyam | [BaudhŚS, 2, 2 14]
ākāśo devo daivaḥ sadasyaḥ sa te devayajanaṃ dadātviti | [BaudhŚS, 2, 2 15]
oṃ tatheti prativacanam | [BaudhŚS, 2, 2 16]
hotrakā devayajanaṃ me datteti hotrakān | [BaudhŚS, 2, 2 17]
āpo devyo daivyā hotrāśaṃsinyas tās te devayajanaṃ dadatviti | [BaudhŚS, 2, 2 18]
oṃ tatheti prativacanam | [BaudhŚS, 2, 2 19]
camasādhvaryavo devayajanaṃ me datteti camasādhvaryūn | [BaudhŚS, 2, 2 20]
raśmayo devā daivāś camasādhvaryavas te te devayajanaṃ dadatviti | [BaudhŚS, 2, 2 21]
oṃ tatheti prativacanam | [BaudhŚS, 2, 2 22]
api vā na devayajanaṃ yācate | [BaudhŚS, 2, 2 23]
ādita eva tīrthe snātvodetyāhataṃ vāsaḥ paridhāya | [BaudhŚS, 2, 2 24]
śuddho haiva śuciḥ pūto medhyo vipāpmā brahmacārī sahakāripratyaya ā caturthāt karmaṇo 'bhisamīkṣamāṇo vedakarmāṇi prayojayet | [BaudhŚS, 2, 2 25]
prāgapavargāṇy udagapavargāṇi vā prāṅmukhaḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ yajñopavītī daivāni karmāṇi karoti | [BaudhŚS, 2, 2 26]
dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ prasavyaṃ prācīnāvītī pitryāṇi | [BaudhŚS, 2, 2 27]
tiṣṭhann āsīnaḥ prahvo vā yathānyāyam | [BaudhŚS, 2, 2 28]
chandogabrāhmaṇaṃ yathā vai dakṣiṇaḥ pāṇir evaṃ devayajanam | [BaudhŚS, 2, 2 29]
yathā savyas tathā pitṛyajanam | [BaudhŚS, 2, 2 30]
yathā pitṛyajanaṃ tathā śmaśānakaraṇam | [BaudhŚS, 2, 2 31]
yathā śmaśānakaraṇaṃ tathābhicaraṇīyeṣv iṣṭipaśusomeṣu | [BaudhŚS, 2, 2 32]
ādita eva purodakaṃ devayajanaṃ yasmād anyat purastāt samantikaṃ devayajanaṃ na vindeyuḥ | [BaudhŚS, 2, 2 33]
uttarato devayajanamātram atiśinaṣṭi | [BaudhŚS, 2, 2 34]
{BaudhŚS, 2, 3}
athartvijāṃ varaṇam | [BaudhŚS, 2, 3 1]
vijñāyate brāhmaṇā ṛtvijo yonigotraśrutavṛttasampannā aviguṇāṅgā atrikiṇinaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 2, 3 2]
na parikhātikrāntā nāntagā nāntyajā nānanūcānāḥ | [BaudhŚS, 2, 3 3]
hāleyavāleyaputrikāputraparakṣetrasahoḍhakānīnānujāvaradvipravarān parihāpya | [BaudhŚS, 2, 3 4]
āṅgiraso 'dhvaryur vāsiṣṭho brahmā vaiśvāmitro hotāyāsya udgātā kauṣītakaḥ sadasyaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 2, 3 5]
avaśiṣṭā bhṛgavo 'ṅgiraso vā | [BaudhŚS, 2, 3 6]
yonivṛttaṃ vidyā ca pramāṇam ity eke | [BaudhŚS, 2, 3 7]
tāṃś ced vṛṇītāvyāpannāṅgān eva vṛṇītākunakhinam adhvaryum akilāsinaṃ brahmāṇam akhaṇḍaṃ hotāram akarālam udgātāram aśipiviṣṭaṃ sadasyam | [BaudhŚS, 2, 3 8]
atha pratiprasthātā neṣṭonnetety adhvaryupuruṣāḥ | [BaudhŚS, 2, 3 9]
brāhmaṇācchaṃsy āgnīdhraḥ poteti brahmaṇaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 2, 3 10]
maitrāvaruṇo 'cchāvāko grāvastud iti hotuḥ | [BaudhŚS, 2, 3 11]
prastotā pratihartā subrahmaṇya ity udgātuḥ | [BaudhŚS, 2, 3 12]
abhigaro dhruvagopaḥ saṃśrāva iti sadasyasya | [BaudhŚS, 2, 3 13]
svapradhānāḥ | [BaudhŚS, 2, 3 14]
asvapradhānā ity eke | [BaudhŚS, 2, 3 15]
daśa vaikādaśa vā camasādhvaryavaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 2, 3 16]
anyadakṣiṇābhiḥ parikrītā bhavantīti vijñāyate | [BaudhŚS, 2, 3 17]
tasmād agnihotrasya yajñakrator eka ṛtvik | [BaudhŚS, 2, 3 18]
darśapūrṇamāsayoś catvāra ṛtvijo 'dhvaryur brahmā hotāgnīdhra iti | [BaudhŚS, 2, 3 19]
cāturmāsyeṣu pratiprasthātā pañcamaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 2, 3 20]
paśubandhe maitrāvaruṇaḥ ṣaṣṭhaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 2, 3 21]
sarve saumye 'dhvare | [BaudhŚS, 2, 3 22]
tān karmaṇaḥ karmaṇo vṛṇīta | [BaudhŚS, 2, 3 23]
ekaikam upasaṃgṛhya codayed asāv aham ādhvaryaveṇa tvā gacchāmi yājayatu māṃ bhavān iti | [BaudhŚS, 2, 3 24]
brahmatvena hautreṇaudgātreṇa sādasyeneti | [BaudhŚS, 2, 3 25]
na sadasyo vidyata ity eke | [BaudhŚS, 2, 3 26]
svena svena karmaṇā hotrakān | [BaudhŚS, 2, 3 27]
na hotrakān ity eke | [BaudhŚS, 2, 3 28]
tatpuruṣā hotrakāś camasādhvaryavaś ca | [BaudhŚS, 2, 3 29]
adhvaryur vā ṛtvijāṃ prathamo yujyate tena stomo yoktavya iti | [BaudhŚS, 2, 3 30]
{BaudhŚS, 2, 4}
ādityo devo daivo 'dhvaryuḥ sa me 'dhvaryur adhvaryo 'dhvaryuṃ tvā vṛṇa ity adhvaryum | [BaudhŚS, 2, 4 1]
ādityo devo daivo 'dhvaryuḥ sa te 'dhvaryus tenānumataḥ karmaivāhaṃ kariṣyāmīti | [BaudhŚS, 2, 4 2]
oṃ tatheti prativacanam | [BaudhŚS, 2, 4 3]
candramā devo daivo brahmā sa me brahmā brahman brahmāṇaṃ tvā vṛṇa iti brahmāṇam | [BaudhŚS, 2, 4 4]
candramā devo daivo brahmā sa te brahmā tenānumataḥ karmaivāhaṃ kariṣyāmīti | [BaudhŚS, 2, 4 5]
oṃ tatheti prativacanam | [BaudhŚS, 2, 4 6]
agnir devo daivo hotā sa me hotā hotar hotāraṃ tvā vṛṇa iti hotāram | [BaudhŚS, 2, 4 7]
agnir devo daivo hotā sa te hotā tenānumataḥ karmaivāhaṃ kariṣyāmīti | [BaudhŚS, 2, 4 8]
oṃ tatheti prativacanam | [BaudhŚS, 2, 4 9]
parjanyo devo daiva udgātā sa ma udgātā udgātar udgātāraṃ tvā vṛṇa ity udgātāram | [BaudhŚS, 2, 4 10]
parjanyo devo daiva udgātā sa ta udgātā tenānumataḥ karmaivāhaṃ kariṣyāmīti | [BaudhŚS, 2, 4 11]
oṃ tatheti prativacanam | [BaudhŚS, 2, 4 12]
ākāśo devo daivaḥ sadasyaḥ sa me sadasyaḥ sadasya sadasyaṃ tvā vṛṇa iti sadasyam | [BaudhŚS, 2, 4 13]
ākāśo devo daivaḥ sadasyaḥ sa te sadasyas tenānumataḥ karmaivāhaṃ kariṣyāmīti | [BaudhŚS, 2, 4 14]
oṃ tatheti prativacanam | [BaudhŚS, 2, 4 15]
āpo devyo daivyā hotrāśaṃsinyas tā me hotrāśaṃsinyo hotrakā hotrakān vo vṛṇa iti hotrakān | [BaudhŚS, 2, 4 16]
āpo devyo daivyā hotrāśaṃsinyas tās te hotrāśaṃsinyas tābhir anumatāḥ karmaiva vayaṃ kariṣyāma iti | [BaudhŚS, 2, 4 17]
oṃ tatheti prativacanam | [BaudhŚS, 2, 4 18]
raśmayo devā daivāś camasādhvaryavas te me camasādhvaryavaś camasādhvaryavaś camasādhvaryūn vo vṛṇa iti camasādhvaryūn | [BaudhŚS, 2, 4 19]
raśmayo devā daivāś camasādhvaryavas te te camasādhvaryavas tair anumatāḥ karmaiva vayaṃ kariṣyāma iti | [BaudhŚS, 2, 4 20]
oṃ tatheti prativacanam | [BaudhŚS, 2, 4 21]

tāṃ diśam etā apa utsiñcati yasyām asya diśi dveṣyo bhavati durmitrās tasmai bhūyāsur yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣma iti | [BaudhŚS, 2, 5 76]
athāpa upaspṛśya yathetaṃ praviśanti | [BaudhŚS, 2, 5 77]
{BaudhŚS, 2, 6}
athedam agnyādheyam | [BaudhŚS, 2, 6 1]
tasya kaḥ karmaṇa upakramo bhavatīti | [BaudhŚS, 2, 6 2]
uktāny ṛtunakṣatrāṇy uktam ātmanaḥ puraścaraṇam | [BaudhŚS, 2, 6 3]
katham atrānupūrvyaṃ bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 2, 6 4]
snānapavanamantraprokṣaṇapuṇyāhavācanāni śraddhām āhūyākūtyā vedanaṃ kṛtvopavyāhṛtyartvijo vṛtvārhayitvā devayajanaṃ yācitvā devayajanam ādāya sphyam ādāyāntareṇa vedyutkarāv uddeśena prapadya jaghanena gārhapatyaṃ tiṣṭhan prācīnaṃ sphyena gārhapatyasyāyatanam uddhanti | [BaudhŚS, 2, 6 5]
uddhanyamānam asyā amedhyam apa pāpmānaṃ yajamānasya hantu śivā naḥ santu pradiśaś catasraḥ śaṃ no mātā pṛthivī tokasāteti | [BaudhŚS, 2, 6 6]

evam evānvāhāryapacanasyāyatanam uddhanti | [BaudhŚS, 2, 6 8]
evam evāhavanīyasya | [BaudhŚS, 2, 6 9]
evam itarayor yadi kariṣyan bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 2, 6 10]
athāntareṇa vedyutkarāv uddeśenodaṅṅ upaniṣkramya tāṃ diśaṃ yanti yatrāsya saṃbhārā upakﾱptā bhavanti | [BaudhŚS, 2, 6 11]
api vottareṇa śālāyāḥ sarve saṃbhārā upakﾱptā bhavanti | [BaudhŚS, 2, 6 12]
api vāntarvedi prācīnaṃ tān mantrānupūrvyam ekaikaṃ saṃbhāram ekaikena yajuṣā saṃbharati | [BaudhŚS, 2, 6 13]
vaiśvānarasya rūpam pṛthivyāṃ parisrasā | [BaudhŚS, 2, 6 14]
syonam āviśatu na iti sikatāḥ saṃbhṛtya nidadhāti | [BaudhŚS, 2, 6 15]
evam evottaramuttaraṃ saṃbhāram uttareṇottareṇa yajuṣā saṃbhṛtya saṃbhṛtyaiva nidadhāti | [BaudhŚS, 2, 6 16]
ūṣāś ca sikatāś cākhūtkaraṃ ca valmīkavapāṃ ca sūdaṃ ca varāhavihataṃ ca puṣkaraparṇaṃ ca śarkarāś cety aṣṭau pārthivāḥ | [BaudhŚS, 2, 6 17]
athottareṇa yajuṣā ṣaḍḍhiraṇyaśalkān āharati | [BaudhŚS, 2, 6 18]
atha vānaspatyābhir vānaspatyāḥ | [BaudhŚS, 2, 6 19]
śākhā ārdrāḥ sapalāśāḥ saprārohāḥ prādeśamātrīr apratiśuṣkāgrā āharati | [BaudhŚS, 2, 6 20]
api vā yathālābham | [BaudhŚS, 2, 6 21]
parṇaṃ dvābhyām | [BaudhŚS, 2, 6 22]
citriyasyāśvatthasya tisraḥ samidha ārdrāḥ sapalāśāḥ saprārohāḥ prādeśamātrīr apratiśuṣkāgrā āharati citriyād aśvatthāt saṃbhṛtā bṛhatyaḥ śarīram abhisaṃskṛtā stha | [BaudhŚS, 2, 6 23.1]
prajāpatinā yajñamukhena saṃmitās tisras trivṛdbhir mithunāḥ prajātyā iti | [BaudhŚS, 2, 6 23.2]
atha muñjakulāyam āharati yā te agna ojasvinī tanūr oṣadhīṣu praviṣṭā | [BaudhŚS, 2, 6 24.1]
tāṃ ta iha saṃbharāmīti | [BaudhŚS, 2, 6 24.2]
athāsmā araṇī āharaty āśvatthīṃ śamīgarbhīm apy aśamīgarbhīṃ vā caturaṅgulam utsedhāṃ dvādaśāṅgulaṃ vistīrṇāṃ ṣoḍaśāṅgulam āyatām api vā prādeśamātrīṃ sarvataḥ samāṃ caturaṅgulam evotsedhām | [BaudhŚS, 2, 6 25]
tasyā uttānāyā anulomam adhastāt pratīcīnapravaṇaṃ prajananaṃ kurvanti | [BaudhŚS, 2, 6 26]
tāvatīm evottarāraṇim | [BaudhŚS, 2, 6 27]
athaine āharati aśvatthāddhavyavāhāddhi jātām agnes tanūṃ yajñiyāṃ saṃbharāmi | [BaudhŚS, 2, 6 28.1]

yo aśvatthaḥ śamīgarbha āruroha tve sacā | [BaudhŚS, 2, 6 29]
taṃ te harāmi brahmaṇā yajñiyaiḥ ketubhiḥ saha iti | [BaudhŚS, 2, 6 30]

{BaudhŚS, 4, 1}
paśunā yakṣyamāṇaḥ bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 4, 1 655559_1]
saḥ upakalpayate pautudravān paridhīn gulgulu sugandhi tejanam śuklām ūrṇā stukām yā petvasya antarā śṛṅge dve raśane dviguṇām ca triguṇām ca dve vapāśrapaṇī viśākhām ca a viśākhām ca hṛdayaśūlam kārṣmarya mayān paridhīn audumbaram maitrāvaruṇa daṇḍam mukhena saṃmitam idhmābarhiḥ idhmam praṇayanīyam plakṣa śākhām iḍa sūnam yavān yavamatībhyaḥ saktūn saktu homāya pṛṣadājyāya dadhi hiraṇyam iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 1 655560_1]
atha āmāvāsyena vā haviṣā iṣṭvā nakṣatre vā gārhapatye ājyam vilāpya utpūya sruci caturgṛhītam gṛhītvā ṣaḍḍhotāram manasā anudrutya āhavanīye juhoti anvārabdhe yajamāne svāhā iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 1 655561_1]
aparam caturgṛhītam gṛhītvā yūpa āhutim juhoti uru viṣṇo vikramasva uru kṣayāya naḥ kṛdhi | [BaudhŚS, 4, 1 655562_1]
ghṛtaṃ ghṛtayone piba pra pra yajñapatiṃ tira svāheti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 1 4.2]

hvayanti takṣāṇam sa paraśum | [BaudhŚS, 4, 1 655565_1]
āha aihi yajamāna iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 1 655566_1]
pūrvayā dvārā upaniṣkramya tām diśam yanti yatra asya yūpaḥ spaṣṭaḥ bhavati yatra vā vetsyan manyate | [BaudhŚS, 4, 1 655566_2]
sa yaḥ same bhūmyai svāt yoneḥ rūḍhaḥ bahu parṇaḥ bahu śākhaḥ a pratiśuṣka agraḥ pratyaṅ upanataḥ tam upatiṣṭhate ati anyān agām na anyān upāgām arvāk tvā paraiḥ avidam paras avaraiḥ tam tvā juṣe vaiṣṇavam deva yajyāyai iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 1 655567_1]
atha enam ājyena anakti devaḥ tvā savitā madhvā anaktu iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 1 655568_1]
ūrdhva agram barhiḥ anūcchrayati oṣadhe trāyasva enam iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 1 655569_1]
svadhitinā tiryañcam praharati svadhite mā enam hiṃsīḥ iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 1 655570_1]
yaḥ prathamaḥ śakalaḥ parāpatati tam prajñātam nidadhāti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 1 655571_1]
tam a paribhindan an akṣa saṅgam vṛścati | [BaudhŚS, 4, 1 655572_1]
prāñcam vā udañcam vā prayāntam anumantrayate divam agreṇa mā lekhīḥ antarikṣam madhyena mā hiṃsīḥ pṛthivyā saṃbhava iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 1 655573_1]
atha āvraścane hiraṇyam nidhāya saṃparistīrya abhijuhoti vanaspate śata valśaḥ viroha svāhā iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 1 655574_1]
sahasra valśāḥ vi vayam ruhema iti ātmānam pratyabhimṛśate | [BaudhŚS, 4, 1 655575_1]
anu agram śākhāḥ prasūdayati yam tvā ayam svadhitiḥ tetijānaḥ praṇināya mahate saubhagāya iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 1 655576_1]
pañca aratnim tasmai vṛścet iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 1 655577_1]
eṣa brāhmaṇavatām avamaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 4, 1 655578_1]
tam pariṣvaṅga paramam prādeśa avamam caṣālasya kāle parivāsayati a chinnaḥ rāyaḥ su vīraḥ iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 1 655579_1]
yat param bhavati tasya catur aṅgulam caṣālāya pracchedayati | [BaudhŚS, 4, 1 655580_1]
tam catur aśrim vā aṣṭa aśrim vā kṛtvā āvāhayati ā vā hārayati | [BaudhŚS, 4, 1 655581_1]
ohya nistiṣṭhati | [BaudhŚS, 4, 1 655582_1]
avatakṣaṇānām eva svarum kurute | [BaudhŚS, 4, 1 655583_1]

bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 4, 1 655584_2]

{BaudhŚS, 4, 2}
idam eva prasiddham pauroḍāśikam | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655587_1]
tris yajuṣā tūṣṇīm caturtham | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655588_1]
pūrvam parigrāham parigṛhṇāti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655589_1]
karaṇam japati | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655590_1]
uddhanti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655591_1]
uddhatāt āgnīdhraḥ tris harati | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655592_1]
yat āgnīdhraḥ tris harati atha yācati sphyam uda pātram barhiḥ śamyām iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655593_1]
etat samādāya āha ehi yajamāna iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655594_1]
uttareṇa vedim dvayoḥ vā triṣu vā prakrameṣu sphyena uddhatya avokṣya śamyayā cātvālam parimimīte | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655595_1]
vittāyanī me asi iti purastāt udīcīna kumbayā antarataḥ sphyena ālikhati | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655596_1]
tiktāyanī me asi iti dakṣiṇatas prācīna kumbayā antarataḥ sphyena ālikhati | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655597_1]
avatāt mā nāthitam iti paścāt udīcīna kumbayā antarataḥ sphyena ālikhati | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655598_1]
avatāt mā vyathitam iti uttaratas prācīna kumbayā antarataḥ sphyena ālikhati | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655599_1]
atha cātvāle barhiḥ nidhāya tasmin sphyena praharati videḥ agniḥ nabhaḥ nāma agne aṅgiraḥ yaḥ asyām pṛthivyām asi iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655600_1]
ādatte āyuṣā nāmnā ihi iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655601_1]
hṛtvā uttaravedyām nivapati yat te anādhṛṣṭam nāma yajñiyam tena tvā ādadhe iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655602_1]
dvitīyam praharati videḥ agniḥ nabhaḥ nāma agne aṅgiraḥ yaḥ dvitīyasyām pṛthivyām asi iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655603_1]
ādatte āyuṣā nāmnā ihi iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655604_1]
hṛtvā uttaravedyām nivapati yat te anādhṛṣṭam nāma yajñiyam tena tvā ādadhe iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655605_1]
tṛtīyam praharati videḥ agniḥ nabhaḥ nāma agne aṅgiraḥ yaḥ tṛtīyasyām pṛthivyām asi iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655606_1]
ādatte āyuṣā nāmnā ihi iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655607_1]
hṛtvā uttaravedyām nivapati yat te anādhṛṣṭam nāma yajñiyam tena tvā ādadhe iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655608_1]
tūṣṇīm caturtham harati saha barhiṣā | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655609_1]
atha adhvaryuḥ sphyena cātvālāt purīṣam uddhanti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655610_1]
atha āgnīdhram āha agnīdh itas tris hara iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655611_1]
tatas tris āgnīdhraḥ harati | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655612_1]
yat āgnīdhraḥ tris harati atha adhvaryuḥ uttaravedyai purīṣam saṃprayauti siṃhīḥ asi mahiṣīḥ asi iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655613_1]
prathayati uru prathasva uru te yajñapatiḥ prathatām iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655614_1]
sphyena saṃhanti dhruvā asi iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655615_1]
atha enām adbhiḥ avokṣati | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655616_1]
devebhyaḥ śundhasva iti devebhyaḥ śumbhasva iti sikatābhiḥ anuprakirati | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655617_1]
tām prādeśa mātrīm catur aśrām niṣṭhāya śamyayā parimimīte | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655618_1]
uttaranābhim utsādya atha enām praticchādya abhrim ādatte devasya tvā savituḥ prasave aśvinoḥ bāhubhyām pūṣṇaḥ hastābhyām ādade iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655620_1]
ādāya abhimantrayate abhriḥ asi nāriḥ asi iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655621_1]
tayā yūpa avaṭam parilikhati yathā antarvedi ardham syāt bahirvedi ardham parilikhitam rakṣaḥ parilikhitāḥ arātayaḥ idam aham rakṣasaḥ grīvāḥ apikṛntāmi yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam ca vayam dviṣmaḥ idam asya grīvāḥ apikṛntāmi iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655622_1]
atha āgnīdhram āha agnīdh ehi imam yūpa avaṭam khana upara saṃmitam prāk purīṣam udvapatāt catur aṅgulena uparam atikhanatāt iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655623_1]
tam sa khanati vā khānayati vā | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655624_1]
yāvat eva atra adhvaryuḥ ceṣṭati tāvat eṣa pratiprasthātā abhyādadhāti idhmam praṇayanīyam | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655625_1]
upa upayamanīḥ kalpayanti cātvālāt | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655626_1]
ātmanā indra ghoṣavatīḥ prokṣaṇīḥ adhvaryuḥ ādatte | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655627_1]
parikarmiṇe pañca gṛhītam ājyam prayacchati | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655628_1]
brahmaṇi saṃbhārāḥ bhavanti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655629_1]
atha saṃpraiṣam āha agnaye praṇīyamānāya anubrūhi agnīdh ekasphyayā anusaṃdhehi iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655630_1]
tris uktāyām udyacchante | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655631_1]
hotuḥ vaśam yanti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655632_1]
uttareṇa vedim pratipadyante | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655633_1]
dhārayanti etam agnim | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655634_1]
atha adhvaryuḥ indra ghoṣavatībhiḥ prokṣaṇībhiḥ uttaravedim prokṣati | [BaudhŚS, 4, 2 655635_1]
{BaudhŚS, 4, 3}
indraghoṣaḥ tvā vasubhiḥ purastāt pātu iti purastāt manojavāḥ tvā pitṛbhiḥ dakṣiṇatas pātu iti dakṣiṇatas pracetāḥ tvā rudraiḥ paścāt pātu iti paścāt viśvakarmā tvā ādityaiḥ uttaratas pātu iti uttaratas | [BaudhŚS, 4, 3 655636_1]
atha yat prokṣaṇīnām ucchiṣyate tat dakṣiṇatas uttaravedyai ninayati | [BaudhŚS, 4, 3 655640_1]
yat eva tatra krūram tat tena śamayati iti brāhmaṇam | [BaudhŚS, 4, 3 655641_1]
atha enām hiraṇyam antardhāya akṣṇayā pañca gṛhītena vyāghārayati siṃhīḥ asi sapatna sāhī svāhā iti dakṣiṇe aṃse siṃhīḥ asi su prajā vaniḥ svāhā iti uttarasyām śroṇyām siṃhīḥ asi rāyaspoṣa vaniḥ svāhā iti dakṣiṇasyām śroṇyām siṃhīḥ asi āditya vaniḥ svāhā iti uttare aṃse siṃhīḥ asi āvaha devān devayate yajamānāya svāhā iti madhye | [BaudhŚS, 4, 3 655642_1]
atha bhūtebhyaḥ tvā iti srucam udgṛhṇāti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 3 655648_1]
atha pautudravān paridhīn paridadhāti viśva āyuḥ asi pṛthivīm dṛṃha iti madhyamam dhruva kṣit asi antarikṣam dṛṃha iti dakṣiṇam a cyuta kṣit asi divam dṛṃha iti uttaram | [BaudhŚS, 4, 3 655649_1]
atha atiśiṣṭān saṃbhārān nivapati gulgulu sugandhi tejanam śuklām ūrṇā stukām agneḥ bhasma asi agneḥ purīṣam asi iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 3 655653_1]
atha enān saṃsrāveṇa abhighārayati | [BaudhŚS, 4, 3 655654_1]
atha pradakṣiṇam āvṛtya idhmam pratiṣṭhāpayati yajña pratitiṣṭha sumatau su śevā ā tvā vasūni purudhā viśantu dīrgham āyuḥ yajamānāya kṛṇvan atha amṛtena jaritāram aṅdhi iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 3 655655_1]
atha enam visrasya āhuti sāham kṛtvā adhvara āhutibhiḥ abhijuhoti agniḥ yajñam nayatu prajānan mā enam yajña hanaḥ vidan devebhyaḥ prabrūtāt yajñam pra pra yajñapatim tira svāhā vāyuḥ yajñam nayatu prajānan mā enam yajña hanaḥ vidan devebhyaḥ prabrūtāt yajñam pra pra yajñapatim tira svāhā sūryaḥ yajñam nayatu prajānan mā enam yajña hanaḥ vidan devebhyaḥ prabrūtāt yajñam pra pra yajñapatim tira svāhā yajñaḥ yajñam nayatu prajānan mā enam yajña hanaḥ vidan devebhyaḥ prabrūtāt yajñam pra pra yajñapatim tira svāhā iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 3 655657_1]
atha etāḥ yajamānaḥ eva svayam juhoti agniḥ anna ādaḥ anna patiḥ annasya īśe sa me annam dadātu svāhā vāyuḥ prāṇa dāḥ prāṇasya īśe sa me prāṇam dadātu svāhā ādityaḥ bhūri dāḥ bhūyiṣṭhānām paśūnām īśe sa me bhūyiṣṭhān paśūn dadātu svāhā iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 3 655666_1]
agnivati uttaram parigrāham parigṛhya yoyupitvā tiryañcam sphyam stabdhvā saṃpraiṣam āha prokṣaṇīḥ āsādayaḥ idhmābarhiḥ upasādaya sruvam svadhitim srucaḥ ca saṃmṛḍḍhi tūṣṇīm pṛṣadājya grahaṇīm patnīm saṃnahya ājyena ca dadhnā ca udehi iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 3 655669_1]
āhṛtāsu prokṣaṇīṣu udasya sphyam mārjayitvā idhmābarhiḥ upasādya pradakṣiṇam āvṛtya pratyaṅ ādrutya sruvam svadhitim srucaḥ ca saṃmārṣṭi tūṣṇīm pṛṣadājya grahaṇīm | [BaudhŚS, 4, 3 655670_1]
patnīm saṃnahya ājyena ca dadhnā ca udeti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 3 655671_1]
ājyam ca prokṣaṇīḥ ca utpūya prasiddham ājyāni gṛhītvā pṛṣadājya grahaṇyām upastṛṇīte mahīnām payaḥ asi iti viśveṣām devānām tanūḥ iti dvitīyam | [BaudhŚS, 4, 3 655671_2]
barhiṣī antardhāya dadhi ānayati ṛdhyāsam adya pṛṣatīnām graham pṛṣatīnām grahaḥ asi iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 3 655673_1]
apoddhṛtya barhiṣī atha abhighārayati viṣṇoḥ hṛdayam asi iti ekam iṣa viṣṇuḥ tvā anu vicakrame iti dvitīyam | [BaudhŚS, 4, 3 655674_1]
{BaudhŚS, 4, 4}
atha prokṣaṇībhiḥ upottiṣṭhati | [BaudhŚS, 4, 4 655676_1]
idhmam prokṣati | [BaudhŚS, 4, 4 655676_2]
vedim prokṣati | [BaudhŚS, 4, 4 655677_1]
barhiḥ prokṣati | [BaudhŚS, 4, 4 655677_2]

pañcavidham barhiḥ stīrtvā prastara pāṇiḥ prāṅ abhisṛpya kārṣmarya mayān paridhīn paridadhāti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 4 655679_1]
ūrdhve samidhau ādadhāti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 4 655680_1]
vidhṛtī tiraścī sādayati vidhṛtyoḥ prastaram prastare juhūm barhiṣi itarāḥ | [BaudhŚS, 4, 4 655681_1]
etāḥ asadan iti samabhimṛśya pradakṣiṇam āvṛtya pratyaṅ ādrutya yācati yavamatīḥ prokṣaṇīḥ barhiḥ hastam ājya sthālīm sa sruvām svaru raśanam maitrāvaruṇa daṇḍam yūpa śakalam hiraṇyam uda pātram iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 4 655685_1]
etat saṃnidhāya yūpam prakṣālayati yat te śikvaḥ parāvadhīt takṣā hastena vāsyā āpaḥ te tat vanaspate apanudantu śundhanīḥ iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 4 655686_1]
yūpaḥ eṣa prakṣālitaḥ prapannaḥ sampanna caṣālaḥ prāk avaṭāt upaśete | [BaudhŚS, 4, 4 655688_1]
tam uttareṇa āhavanīyam tiṣṭhan parāñcam prokṣati pṛthivyai tvā antarikṣāya tvā dive tvā iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 4 655689_1]
avaṭe apaḥ avanayati śundhatām lokaḥ pitṛṣadanaḥ iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 4 655690_1]
yavān praskandayati yavaḥ asi yavaya asmat dveṣaḥ yavaya arātīḥ iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 4 655691_1]
barhiḥ hastam vyatiṣajya avastṛṇāti pitṝṇām sadanam asi iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 4 655692_1]
atha enat hiraṇyam antardhāya sruva āhutyā abhijuhoti pitṛbhyaḥ svāhā iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 4 655693_1]
yūpa śakalam avāsyati su āveśaḥ asi agregāḥ netṝṇām vanaspatiḥ adhi tvā sthāsyati tasya vittāt iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 4 655694_1]
atha ādatte ājya sthālīm sa sruvām svaru raśanam maitrāvaruṇa daṇḍam uda pātram iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 4 655695_1]
etat samādāya āha ehi yajamāna iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 4 655696_1]
anvak yajamānaḥ anūcī patnī agreṇa yūpam parītya dakṣiṇatas udak mukhāḥ tiṣṭhanti pūrvaḥ eva adhvaryuḥ aparaḥ yajamānaḥ aparā patnī | [BaudhŚS, 4, 4 655697_1]
atha pravṛhya caṣālam yūpasya agram anakti devaḥ tvā savitā madhvā anaktu iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 4 655698_1]
antarataḥ ca bāhyatas ca su abhyaktam kṛtvā caṣālam pratimuñcati su pippalābhyaḥ tvā oṣadhībhyaḥ iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 4 655699_1]
sruveṇa agniṣṭhām aśrim abhighārayan āha yūpāya ajyamānāya anubrūhi iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 4 655700_1]
ā antam anakti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 4 655701_1]
ā antam eva yajamānam tejasā anakti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 4 655701_2]
na uparam anakti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 4 655702_1]
patnī uparam anakti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 4 655703_1]
sarvatas parimṛśati | [BaudhŚS, 4, 4 655704_1]
aparivargam eva asmin tejaḥ dadhāti iti brāhmaṇam | [BaudhŚS, 4, 4 655704_2]
ucchrayan āha ucchrīyamāṇāya anubrūhi iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 4 655705_1]
ucchrayati ud divam stabhāna antarikṣam pṛṇa pṛthivīm upareṇa dṛṃha iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 4 655706_1]
atha enam vaiṣṇavībhyām ṛgbhyām kalpayati te te dhāmāni viṣṇoḥ karmāṇi paśyata iti dvābhyām | [BaudhŚS, 4, 4 655707_1]
sa yatra agniṣṭhām aśrim āhavanīyena sampādayati tat dhruvasya caṣālam prekṣayati tat viṣṇoḥ paramam padam sadā paśyanti sūrayaḥ divi iva cakṣuḥ ātatam iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 4 655708_1]
atha enam pradakṣiṇam purīṣeṇa paryūhati brahma vanim tvā kṣatra vanim su prajā vanim rāyaspoṣa vanim paryūhāmi iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 4 655710_1]
maitrāvaruṇa daṇḍena saṃhanti brahma dṛṃha kṣatram dṛṃha prajām dṛṃha rāyaspoṣam dṛṃha iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 4 655711_1]
a nyūnam an atiriktam parinyasya uda pātram upaninīya atha etām triguṇām raśanām tris saṃbhujya madhyamena guṇena nābhi daghne parivyayan āha parivīyamāṇāya anubrūhi iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 4 655713_1]
tris pradakṣiṇam parivyayati parivīḥ asi pari tvā daivīḥ viśaḥ vyayantām pari imam rāyaspoṣaḥ yajamānam manuṣyāḥ iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 4 655714_1]
upānte vyatiṣajati | [BaudhŚS, 4, 4 655715_1]
ā antam praveṣṭayati | [BaudhŚS, 4, 4 655716_1]
aṇimati sthavimat pravayati | [BaudhŚS, 4, 4 655717_1]
atha uttareṇa agniṣṭhām aśrim madhyame guṇe svarum avagūhati antarikṣasya tvā sānau avagūhāmi iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 4 655718_1]
svarvantam yūpam utsṛjati | [BaudhŚS, 4, 4 655719_1]
{BaudhŚS, 4, 5}
atha etam paśum palpūlitam antareṇa cātvāla utkarau prapādya agreṇa yūpam purastāt pratyak mukham upasthāpayati | [BaudhŚS, 4, 5 655720_1]
tam iṣe tvā iti barhiṣī ādāya upākaroti upavīḥ asi upa u devān daivīḥ viśaḥ prāguḥ uśijaḥ bṛhaspate dhāraya vasūni havyā te svadantām deva tvaṣṭar vasu raṇva revatī ramadhvam prajāpateḥ jāyamānāḥ imam paśum paśupate te adya indra agnibhyām tvā juṣṭam upākaromi iti yad devatyaḥ vā bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 4, 5 655721_1]
prajñāte barhiṣī nidhāya adhimanthanam śakalam nidadhāti agneḥ janitram asi iti vṛṣaṇau anvañcau vṛṣaṇau sthaḥ iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 5 655723_1]

atha āha agnaye mathyamānāya anubrūhi iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 5 655728_1]
jāte āha jātāya anubrūhi iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 5 655729_1]
