praharati bhavatam naḥ samanasau iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 5 655731_1]
prahṛtya abhijuhoti agnau agniḥ carati praviṣṭaḥ iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 5 655732_1]
atha raśanām ādatte devasya tvā savituḥ prasave aśvinoḥ bāhubhyām pūṣṇaḥ hastābhyām ādade iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 5 655733_1]
tayā akṣṇayā paśum abhidadhāti dakṣiṇam adhyardha śīrṣam ṛtasya tvā deva haviḥ pāśena ārabhe iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 5 655734_1]
dvi guṇāyai ca tri guṇāyai ca antau saṃdadhāti dharṣa mānuṣān iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 5 655735_1]
niyunakti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 5 655736_1]
atha enam adbhiḥ prokṣati adbhyaḥ tvā oṣadhībhyaḥ indra agnibhyām tvā juṣṭam prokṣāmi iti yad devatyaḥ vā bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 4, 5 655737_1]
pāyayati apām peruḥ asi iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 5 655739_1]

{BaudhŚS, 4, 6}

atha a saṃsparśayan srucau udaṅ atyākramya juhvā paśum samanakti sam te prāṇaḥ vāyunā gacchatām iti lalāṭe sam yajatraiḥ aṅgāni iti kakudi sam yajñapatiḥ āśiṣā iti dakṣiṇasyām śroṇyām | [BaudhŚS, 4, 6 655749_1]

asau mānuṣaḥ iti maitrāvaruṇasya nāma gṛhṇāti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 6 655755_2]
atha āśrāvayati | [BaudhŚS, 4, 6 655756_1]
yadi atra ati āśrāvayati o śrāvaya astu | [BaudhŚS, 4, 6 655757_1]
śrauṣaṭ agniḥ ha daivīnām viśām puraetā ayam yajamānaḥ manuṣyāṇām tayoḥ a sthūri gārhapatyam dīdayat śatam himāḥ dvā rādhāṃsi id saṃpṛñcānau a saṃpṛñcānau tanvaḥ iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 6 655757_2]

eṣaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 4, 6 655769_1]
atha āgnīdhraḥ āhavanīyāt ulmukam ādāya antareṇa cātvāla utkarau uttareṇa śāmitra deśam agreṇa paśum jaghanena srucaḥ iti evam tris pradakṣiṇam paryeti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 6 655769_2]
atha anu parisaraṇam apāvyāni juhoti prajānantaḥ pratigṛhṇanti pūrve yeṣām īśe paśupatiḥ paśūnām ye badhyamānam anu badhyamānāḥ ye āraṇyāḥ paśavaḥ viśva rūpāḥ pramuñcamānāḥ bhuvanasya retaḥ iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 6 655770_1]

anvak śamitā | [BaudhŚS, 4, 6 655773_1]
paśunā | [BaudhŚS, 4, 6 655773_2]
paśum adhvaryuḥ vapāśrapaṇībhyām anvārabhate | [BaudhŚS, 4, 6 655774_1]
vapāśrapaṇī yajamānaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 4, 6 655775_1]

atha etam paśum antareṇa cātvāla utkarau udañcam nīyamānam anumantrayate nānā prāṇaḥ yajamānasya paśunā revatīḥ yajñapatim priyadhā viśata iti dvābhyām | [BaudhŚS, 4, 6 655777_1]
sa yatra etat āgnīdhraḥ ulmukam nidadhāti tat agreṇa vā uttareṇa vā paśave nihanyamānāya barhiḥ upāsyati pṛthivyāḥ saṃpṛcaḥ pāhi iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 6 655778_1]
tat etam paśum pratīcīna śirasam udīcīna pādam nighnanti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 6 655779_1]
a kṛṇvantam māyum saṃjñapayata iti uktvā etena eva yathetam etya pṛṣadājya avakāśe āsate iha prajāḥ viśva rūpāḥ ramantām asmin yajñe viśva vidaḥ ghṛtācīḥ | [BaudhŚS, 4, 6 655779_2]
agnim kulāyam abhisaṃvasānāḥ asmāṁ avantu payasā ghṛtena iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 6 655780_1]
saṃjñaptam prāhuḥ | [BaudhŚS, 4, 6 655781_1]

pāśāt paśum pramucyamānam anumantrayate aditiḥ pāśam pramumoktu etam iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 6 655784_1]
a viśākhayā upasajya imām diśam nirasyati arātīyantam adharam kṛṇomi yam dviṣmaḥ tasmin pratimuñcāmi pāśam iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 6 655785_1]
atha pratiprasthātā patnīm udānayati uda kamaṇḍalum utthāpya | [BaudhŚS, 4, 6 655786_1]
atha enām ādityam udīkṣayati namaḥ te ātāna iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 6 655787_1]
atha enām antareṇa cātvāla utkarau udaṅ upaniṣkramya prācīm udānayan vācayati anarvā prehi ghṛtasya kulyām anu saha prajayā saha rāyaspoṣeṇa iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 6 655788_1]
āgatām adhvaryuḥ apsu vācayati āpaḥ devīḥ śuddhāyuvaḥ śuddhāḥ yūyam devāṁ ūḍhvam śuddhāḥ vayam pariviṣṭāḥ pariveṣṭāraḥ vaḥ bhūyāsma iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 6 655789_1]
sā anupūrvam paśoḥ prāṇān āpyāyayati | [BaudhŚS, 4, 6 655790_1]
vāc te āpyāyatām iti vācam | [BaudhŚS, 4, 6 655791_1]
prāṇaḥ te āpyāyatām iti prāṇam | [BaudhŚS, 4, 6 655792_1]

atiśiṣṭāḥ | [BaudhŚS, 4, 6 655799_1]

uttānam paśum paryasyanti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 6 655801_1]

sthavimat ubhayatas lohitena aṅktvā imām diśam nirasyati rakṣasām bhāgaḥ asi idam aham rakṣaḥ adhamam tamaḥ nayāmi yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam ca vayam dviṣmaḥ idam enam adhamam tamaḥ nayāmi iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 6 655807_1]

atha enām antareṇa yūpam ca āhavanīyam ca upātihṛtya tām dakṣiṇatas udak mukhaḥ pratiprasthātā śrapayati | [BaudhŚS, 4, 7 655817_1]

vaṣaṭkṛte juhoti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 7 655821_1]

dvis abhighārayati | [BaudhŚS, 4, 7 655824_1]

atha purastāt svāhākṛtim sruva āhutim juhoti svāhā devebhyaḥ iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 7 655826_1]

atha ene saṃsrāveṇa abhijuhoti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 7 655831_1]

atha pratiprasthātā paśuṃ viśāsti śamitar hṛdayaṃ jihvāṃ vakṣas tāni sārdhaṃ kurutāt tanima matasnau tāni sārdhaṃ savyaṃ dor ekacaraṃ kurutāt nānā pārśve avadhattāt dakṣiṇāṃ śroṇim adhyuddhiṃ kurutāt dakṣiṇaṃ doḥ savyāṃ śroṇim aṇimad gudasya tāni tryaṅgāni kurutāt vaniṣṭhuṃ ca jāghanīṃ cāvadhattāt bahu yūḥ kurutāt triḥ paśuṃ pracyāvayatāt triḥ pracyutasya paśor hṛdayam uttamaṃ kurutāt iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 8 3]
śṛte paśau paśupuroḍāśaṃ yācati | [BaudhŚS, 4, 8 4]

na pratyanakti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 8 12]

mārjayante | [BaudhŚS, 4, 8 21]
atha saṃpraiṣam āha agnīd uttarabarhir upasādaya pratiprasthātaḥ paśau saṃvadasva iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 8 22]

tad uttarabarhir bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 4, 8 24]
atha pratiprasthātā pṛṣadājyaṃ vihatya juhvāṃ samānīyāntareṇa cātvālotkarāv udaṅṅ upaniṣkramya pṛcchati śṛtaṃ havī3ḥ śamitar iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 8 25]

taṃ tathaiva dvitīyam utkramya pṛcchati | [BaudhŚS, 4, 8 28]

abhighārayati | [BaudhŚS, 4, 9 13]

{BaudhŚS, 4, 10}

atha saṃpraiṣam āhāgnīd aupayajān aṅgārān āhara upayaṣṭar upasīda brahman prasthāsyāmaḥ samidham ādhāyāgnīd agnīn sakṛtsakṛt saṃmṛḍḍhīti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 10 2]

prāśnītaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 4, 10 20]

atha sruci caturgṛhītaṃ gṛhītvāpasalaiḥ paryāvṛtyānvāhāryapacane prāyaścittaṃ hutvā na phalīkaraṇahomena carati | [BaudhŚS, 4, 10 22]
atha prāṅ etya dhruvām āpyāyya trīṇi samiṣṭayajūṃṣi juhoti yajña yajñaṃ gaccha yajñapatiṃ gaccha svāṃ yoniṃ gaccha svāheti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 10 23]

{BaudhŚS, 4, 11}

athāpratīkṣam āyanti varuṇasyāntarhityai | [BaudhŚS, 4, 11 3]
prapathe samidhaḥ kurvate edho 'sy edhiṣīmahīti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 11 4]
etyāhavanīye 'bhyādadhāti samid asi tejo 'si tejo mayi dhehīti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 11 5]

athaupayajike 'gnau barhir upoṣati yat kusīdam apratīttaṃ mayi yena yamasya balinā carāmi | [BaudhŚS, 4, 11 7.1]
ihaiva san niravadaye tat etat tad agne anṛṇo bhavāmīti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 11 7.2]
athāñjalinopastīrṇābhighāritān saktūn pradāvye juhoti viśvalopa viśvadāvasya tvāsañ juhomi svāheti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 11 8]
hastau pradhvaṃsayate agdhād eko 'hutād ekaḥ samanasād ekas te naḥ kṛṇvantu bheṣajam sadaḥ saho vareṇyam iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 11 9]
dvitīyaṃ juhoti yāny apāmityāny apratīttāny asmi yamasya balinā carāmi | [BaudhŚS, 4, 11 10.1]
ihaiva santaḥ prati tad yātayāmo jīvā jīvebhyo niharāma enat svāheti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 11 10.2]
hastau pradhvaṃsayate agdhād eko 'hutād ekaḥ samanasād ekas te naḥ kṛṇvantu bheṣajam sadaḥ saho vareṇyam iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 11 11]
tṛtīyaṃ juhoty anṛṇā asminn anṛṇāḥ parasmin tṛtīye loke anṛṇāḥ syāma | [BaudhŚS, 4, 11 12.1]
ye devayānā uta pitṛyāṇāḥ sarvān patho anṛṇā ākṣīyema svāheti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 11 12.2]
hastau pradhvaṃsayate agdhād eko 'hutād ekaḥ samanasād ekas te naḥ kṛṇvantu bheṣajam sadaḥ saho vareṇyam iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 11 13]
atha devatā upatiṣṭhate | [BaudhŚS, 4, 11 14]
ayaṃ no nabhasā pura ity agnim sa tvaṃ no nabhasaspata iti vāyum | [BaudhŚS, 4, 11 15]
deva saṃsphānety ādityam | [BaudhŚS, 4, 11 16]
atha yūpam upatiṣṭhate āśāsānaḥ suvīryam rāyaspoṣaṃ svaśviyam | [BaudhŚS, 4, 11 17.1]
bṛhaspatinā rāyā svagākṛto mahyaṃ yajamānāya tiṣṭheti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 11 17.2]
atha pūrvāgniṃ śakale samāropayaty ayaṃ te yonir ṛtviya iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 11 18]
taṃ madhyame 'gnāv apisṛjaty ājuhvāna udbudhyasvāgna iti dvābhyām | [BaudhŚS, 4, 11 19]
atha madhyamam agnim upasamādhāya madhyame 'gnau pūrṇāhutiṃ juhoti sapta te agne samidhaḥ sapta jihvā iti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 11 20]
pūrṇāhutau varaṃ dadāti | [BaudhŚS, 4, 11 21]
dhenuvaraṃ vānaḍudvaraṃ vā dadyād iti ha smāha baudhāyanaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 4, 11 22]
saṃtiṣṭhate paśubandhaḥ saṃtiṣṭhate paśubandhaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 4, 11 23]
{BaudhŚS, 8, 21}
yāvad evātrādhvaryuś ceṣṭati tāvad eṣa pratiprasthātā prāyaṇīyasya niṣkāsa udayanīyam abhinirvapati | [BaudhŚS, 8, 21 1]
eṣa eva veda etan mekṣaṇam etad barhiḥ | [BaudhŚS, 8, 21 2]
athaitāṃ carusthālīṃ sakṣāmakāṣām utkhidya nirṇijya tayodayanīyaṃ śrapayati | [BaudhŚS, 8, 21 3]
tasmiṃstathaiva śrapyamāṇe jaghanena gārhapatyam aupasadāyāṃ vedyāṃ stambayajur harati | [BaudhŚS, 8, 21 4]
idam eva prasiddhaṃ pauroḍāśikam | [BaudhŚS, 8, 21 5]
trir yajuṣā tūṣṇīṃ caturtham | [BaudhŚS, 8, 21 6]
pūrvaṃ parigrāhaṃ parigṛhṇāti | [BaudhŚS, 8, 21 7]
karaṇaṃ japati | [BaudhŚS, 8, 21 8]
uddhanti | [BaudhŚS, 8, 21 9]
uddhatād āgnīdhras trir harati | [BaudhŚS, 8, 21 10]
samānaṃ karma yathā prāyaṇīyasya | [BaudhŚS, 8, 21 11]
etāvad eva nānā | [BaudhŚS, 8, 21 12]
pathyām amutra svastiṃ prathamāṃ yajati tām ihopottamāṃ yajati | [BaudhŚS, 8, 21 13]
no tu diśaś cyavante | [BaudhŚS, 8, 21 14]
atha purastāt sviṣṭakṛtaḥ sruvāhutim upajuhoti yās te viśvāḥ samidhaḥ santy agne iti | [BaudhŚS, 8, 21 15]
upastaraṇābhighāraṇābhyām evaitad dhruvājyaṃ vicchiṃṣanti | [BaudhŚS, 8, 21 16]
samiṣṭayajur u haike juhvati | [BaudhŚS, 8, 21 17]
śaṃyvanta udayanīyaḥ saṃtiṣṭhate | [BaudhŚS, 8, 21 18]
atraitat pūrṇapātram antarvedi ninayati | [BaudhŚS, 8, 21 19]
atha pṛṣadājyavanty ājyāni gṛhītvā maitrāvaruṇīṃ vaśām upākaroti | [BaudhŚS, 8, 21 20]
tasyai prasiddhaṃ vapayā caritvā dakṣiṇe vedyante keśaśmaśru vapate | [BaudhŚS, 8, 21 21]
nakhāni nikṛntate | [BaudhŚS, 8, 21 22]
sarvasaṃsthāṃ paśoḥ kurvanti | [BaudhŚS, 8, 21 23]
atha yadi vaśāṃ na labhate maitrāvaruṇīm āmikṣāṃ gārhapatye śrapayitvā tayāhavanīye pracarati | [BaudhŚS, 8, 21 24]
sājyabhāgapratipatkeḍāntā saṃtiṣṭhate | [BaudhŚS, 8, 21 25]
{BaudhŚS, 10, 23}
atha prāyaṇīyena carati | [BaudhŚS, 10, 23 1]
prāyaṇīyena caritvā padena carati | [BaudhŚS, 10, 23 2]
padena caritvā rājānaṃ krītvohyātithyaṃ nirvapati | [BaudhŚS, 10, 23 3]
ātithyena pracarya prathamābhyāṃ pravargyopasadbhyāṃ pracarati | [BaudhŚS, 10, 23 4]
athopaniṣkramya saṃpraiṣam āha subrahmaṇya subrahmaṇyām āhvaya tristanavrataṃ prayacchateti | [BaudhŚS, 10, 23 5]
āhvayati subrahmaṇyaḥ subrahmaṇyām | [BaudhŚS, 10, 23 6]
tristanavrataṃ prayacchati | [BaudhŚS, 10, 23 7]
sa pucchād evāgre caturaḥ pratīcaḥ prakramān prakrāmati dakṣiṇā pañcamam | [BaudhŚS, 10, 23 8]
tat sphyaṃ nidadhāti | [BaudhŚS, 10, 23 9]
sa uparavāṇāṃ kālaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 10, 23 10]
atha mahāvedyā uttarād aṃsīyācchaṅkor vedyantena dvādaśa pratīcaḥ prakramān prakrāmaty udañcaṃ trayodaśam | [BaudhŚS, 10, 23 11]
tad āgnīdhra upasīdati | [BaudhŚS, 10, 23 12]
sa utkarasya kālaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 10, 23 13]
athoparavāṇāṃ kālāt stambayajur harati | [BaudhŚS, 10, 23 14]
idam eva prasiddham | [BaudhŚS, 10, 23 15]
pauroḍāśikaṃ trir yajuṣā tūṣṇīṃ caturtham | [BaudhŚS, 10, 23 16]
pūrvaṃ parigrāhaṃ parigṛhṇāti | [BaudhŚS, 10, 23 17]
karaṇaṃ japati | [BaudhŚS, 10, 23 18]
uddhatād āgnīdhras trir harati | [BaudhŚS, 10, 23 19]
yad āgnīdhras trir haraty athāgreṇa śālāṃ tiṣṭhan saṃpraiṣam āha vedikārā vediṃ kalpayateti | [BaudhŚS, 10, 23 20]
yathāsaṃpraiṣaṃ te kurvanti | [BaudhŚS, 10, 23 21]
atha kārṣṇājinīr upānaha upamuñcante cite tvety adhvaryur ācite tveti pratiprasthātā manaścite tveti brahmā tapaścite tveti yajamānaś cite tvā cite tvety eva vā sarve | [BaudhŚS, 10, 23 22]
api vā tūṣṇīm evātha yācati dhanur bāṇavac caturo 'śmana aindrīm iṣṭakāṃ vibhaktim udapātraṃ darbhastambaṃ dūrvām ājyasthālīṃ sasruvām iti | [BaudhŚS, 10, 23 23]
etat samādāyottare śroṇyante saṃsādayanti | [BaudhŚS, 10, 23 24]
atha dvābhyām ātmany agniṃ gṛhṇīte mayi gṛhṇāmy agre agnim yo no agnir iti | [BaudhŚS, 10, 23 25]
svayaṃcitiṃ japati yās te agne samidho yāni dhāmeti | [BaudhŚS, 10, 23 26]
śvetam aśvam abhimṛśyāntaḥśarkaram imām upadadhāti prajāpatis tvā sādayatu tayā devatayāṅgirasvad dhruvā sīdeti | [BaudhŚS, 10, 23 27]
athādatte dhanur bāṇavac caturo 'śmana iti | [BaudhŚS, 10, 23 28]
etat samādāya jaghanena dakṣiṇenāgniṃ parītyāgreṇa yūpāvaṭīyaṃ śaṅkuṃ tiṣṭhan dhanur adhijyaṃ kṛtvāyatyāntaḥśarkaram iṣuṃ nihanti | [BaudhŚS, 10, 23 29]
{BaudhŚS, 16, 1}
dvādaśāhena yakṣyamāṇo bhavaty eko vā bahavo vā | [BaudhŚS, 16, 1 1]
uto hy eko dakṣiṇāvatā yajate | [BaudhŚS, 16, 1 2]
sa yady eko yadi bahavo 'māvāsyāyā eva ṣaḍahenopariṣṭād dīkṣante | [BaudhŚS, 16, 1 3.1]
te gṛhapater araṇyoḥ saṃjānate pṛthag vā | [BaudhŚS, 16, 1 4.1]
te yadi gṛhapater araṇyoḥ saṃjānate mathitvā gārhapatyam āhavanīyam uddharanti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 1 5.1]
grāmād vrataśrapaṇam āharanti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 1 6]
yady u vai pṛthak saṃjānate gṛhapatir eva prathamo manthate | [BaudhŚS, 16, 1 7]
tad evetare paryupaviśya mathitvā mathitvaiva gārhapatyaṃ saṃnivapanti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 1 8.1]
tasmād ekavadbhūtād āhavanīyam uddharanti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 1 9.1]
grāmād vrataśrapaṇān āhṛtya saṃnivapanti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 1 10.1]
atha yadi paścād apara āgacchati mathitvaiva gārhapatye 'rdhaṃ nivapaty āhavanīye 'rdhaṃ grāmād vrataśrapaṇam āhṛtyāpyarjati | [BaudhŚS, 16, 1 11.1]
upo enaṃ pūrveṣu karmasu hvayante | [BaudhŚS, 16, 1 12.1]
athātaḥ pavanasyaiva mīmāṃsā | [BaudhŚS, 16, 1 13]
gṛhapatim evādhvaryuḥ prathamaṃ pavayaty atha hotāram atha brahmāṇam athodgātāram | [BaudhŚS, 16, 1 14]
pratiprasthātādhvaryuṃ pavayati prastotāraṃ praśāstāraṃ brāhmaṇācchaṃsinam | [BaudhŚS, 16, 1 15]
āgnīdhraḥ pratiprasthātāraṃ pavayaty acchāvākaṃ neṣṭāraṃ potāraṃ sadasyam | [BaudhŚS, 16, 1 16]
unnetāgnīdhraṃ pavayati grāvastutaṃ subrahmaṇyaṃ pratihartāram ātmānam antataḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 1 17]
te ced brūyur adhvaryur vāva sarvasya pavayitā sa naḥ sarvān pavayatv iti sa evainān sarvān pavayati | [BaudhŚS, 16, 1 18.1]
api vānyonyaṃ pavayanti yady adhīyanto bhavanti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 1 19.1]
{BaudhŚS, 16, 2}
teṣāṃ prasiddhā dīkṣaṇīyeṣṭis tāyate | [BaudhŚS, 16, 2 1]
sakṛd āśrāvite sa yatrāha bharatavad iti tad gṛhapater evārṣeyaṃ prathamaṃ vṛṇīte 'tha hotur athātmano 'tha brahmaṇo 'thodgātur atha pratiprasthātur atha prastotur atha praśāstur atha brāhmaṇācchaṃsino 'cchāvākasya sadasyasyāgnīdhaḥ potur neṣṭur grāvastuta unnetuḥ subrahmaṇyasya pratihartur antataḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 2 2]
brahmaṇvad iti samānam | [BaudhŚS, 16, 2 3]
te sarva eva dīkṣāhutiṣu samanvārabhante | [BaudhŚS, 16, 2 4]

tad evetare 'nunikrāmanti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 2 6]
api vānyonyaṃ vācayanti yady adhīyanto bhavanti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 2 7]
te yathotsāhaṃ vratadugham upayanty ekaikāṃ vā bahvīr vā | [BaudhŚS, 16, 2 8]
teṣāṃ yathaiva pravarānupūrvyam evaṃ gharmocchiṣṭe 'tigrāhyabhakṣeṣu ṣoḍaśini | [BaudhŚS, 16, 2 9]
ṣaṣṭhyām upasady uttaravediṃ saṃnivapanti yady anagnicityo bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 16, 2 10]
atha yadi sāgnicityaḥ prathamāyām evopasady uttaravediṃ saṃnivapanti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 2 11]
{BaudhŚS, 16, 3}
teṣāṃ dvādaśa dīkṣā dvādaśopasado dvādaśāhaṃ prasutāḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 3 1]
na dvādaśāhe 'gniṃ cinvītety eka āhuḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 3 2]
cinvata u haike | [BaudhŚS, 16, 3 3]
prasiddhena karmaṇopavasathād yanti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 3 4]
teṣāṃ jyotiṣṭomo vaiśvānaraḥ prāyaṇīyo 'tirātras tāyate | [BaudhŚS, 16, 3 5]
sa yatra mādhyaṃdine savane tṛtīyasavanāya vasatīvarībhyo 'vanayati tad vasatīvarīkalaśe yāvanmātrīr atiśiṣyāgnīdhraṃ drutvā chāyāyai cātapataś ca sandhau gṛhṇāti haviṣmatīr imā āpo haviṣmān devo adhvaro haviṣmāṁ āvivāsati haviṣmāṁ astu sūrya iti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 3 6]
eṣāhīnasaṃtatir etām eva punaḥpunaś codayiṣyāma iti vadantaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 3 7]
so 'tra vaiva yajñasya punarālambhaṃ japati yajñāyajñiyasya vā stotre śaṃyuvāke vā | [BaudhŚS, 16, 3 8]
teṣāṃ jyotiṣṭomo vaiśvānaraḥ prāyaṇīyo 'tirātraḥ saṃtiṣṭhate | [BaudhŚS, 16, 3 9]
tasmin saṃsthite vivartayanti paridhīn | [BaudhŚS, 16, 3 10]
anupraharanti prastaram | [BaudhŚS, 16, 3 11]
patnīsaṃyājāntaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 3 12]
atipraiṣeṇa brahmā vācaṃ yacchati | [BaudhŚS, 16, 3 13]
parihṛtāsu vasatīvarīṣv āhūtāyāṃ subrahmaṇyāyāṃ brahmā vācaṃ visṛjate | [BaudhŚS, 16, 3 14]
pratipadyate divā | [BaudhŚS, 16, 3 15]
prātaranuvākenāhnā saṃkrāman hotā chandāṃsy anvāha nimīlyādhvaryur upāṃśuṃ juhoti rātryai rūpam iti vadantaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 3 16]
tāyate trivṛd agniṣṭomo rathaṃtarasāmā | [BaudhŚS, 16, 3 17]
māhendrasya stotre ratho yukto 'tyādhāvati | [BaudhŚS, 16, 3 18]

etāvad evaitad ahaḥ śilpaṃ kriyate | [BaudhŚS, 16, 3 20]
ahīnasaṃtatiṃ karoti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 3 21]
atha śvo bhūte tāyate pañcadaśa ukthyo bṛhatsāmā | [BaudhŚS, 16, 3 22]
dundubhinaitad ahar adhvaryur māhendrasya stotram upākaroti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 3 23]
etāvad evaitad ahaḥ śilpaṃ kriyate | [BaudhŚS, 16, 3 24]
ahīnasaṃtatiṃ karoti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 3 25]
atha śvo bhūte tāyate saptadaśa ukthyo vairūpasāmā | [BaudhŚS, 16, 3 26]
ādhāvenaitad ahar adhvaryur māhendrasya stotram upākaroti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 3 27]
etāvad evaitad ahaḥ śilpaṃ kriyate | [BaudhŚS, 16, 3 28]
ahīnasaṃtatiṃ karoti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 3 29]
atha śvo bhūte tāyata ekaviṃśa ukthyo vairājasāmā | [BaudhŚS, 16, 3 30]
āgneyaś ca ṣoḍaśī cātigrāhyau | [BaudhŚS, 16, 3 31]
anatigrāhyaḥ ṣoḍaśīty eka āhuḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 3 32]
ekaviṃśam etad ahar nyūṅkhyaṃ bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 16, 3 33]

{BaudhŚS, 16, 4}
tasya mīmāṃsā | [BaudhŚS, 16, 4 1]

{BaudhŚS, 16, 5}

naitad ahar anyonyasyartuyājaṃ yajanti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 5 3]
sa yatrāha adhvaryū yajatam iti tad adhvaryū jaghanena havirdhāne upaviśya svayamṛtuyājaṃ yajato ye3 yajāmahe aśvinādhvaryū ādhvaryavād ṛtunā somaṃ pibatām arvāñcam adya yayyaṃ nṛvāhaṇam rathaṃ yuñjāthām iha vāṃ vimocanaṃ pṛṅktaṃ havīṃṣi madhunā hi kaṃ gatam athā somaṃ pibataṃ vājinīvasū ṛtunā somaṃ pibatām vau3ṣat iti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 5 4]
sa yatrāha gṛhapate yajeti tad gṛhapatir jaghanena gārhapatyam upaviśya svayamṛtuyājaṃ yajati ye3 yajāmahe agniṃ gṛhapatiṃ gārhapatyāt sugṛhapatayas tvayāgna ime sunvanto yajamānāḥ syuḥ sugṛhapatis tvam ebhiḥ sunvadbhir yajamānaiḥ syā agnir gṛhapatir gārhapatyāt ṛtunā somaṃ pibatu joṣy agne samidhaṃ joṣy āhutim joṣi brahma janyaṃ joṣi suṣṭutiṃ viśvebhir viśvāṁ ṛtunā vaso maha uśan devāṁ uśataḥ pāyayā haviḥ ṛtunā somaṃ pibatū vau3ṣaḍ iti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 5 5]
sāṃvāśinam etad ahar bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 16, 5 6]
uttarato vatsān dhārayanti dakṣiṇato mātṝḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 5 7]
māhendrasya stotre 'ntareṇa sadohavirdhāne saṃvāśya vatsān mātṛbhiḥ saṃsṛjanti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 5 8]
badhnanti vatsān | [BaudhŚS, 16, 5 9]
utsṛjanti mātṝḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 5 10]
māhendrasya stotram upākaroti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 5 11]
athāparāhṇa ukthyaparyāyeṣu śilpāni kriyante | [BaudhŚS, 16, 5 12]
pārucchepīr hotā śaṃsati | [BaudhŚS, 16, 5 13]
vālakhilyā maitrāvaruṇo viharati | [BaudhŚS, 16, 5 14]
vṛṣākapiṃ brāhmaṇācchaṃsī śaṃsaty evayāmarutam acchāvākaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 5 15]
saṃtiṣṭhate pṛṣṭhyaḥ ṣaḍahaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 5 16]
ahīnasaṃtatiṃ karoti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 5 17]
atha vasatīvarīḥ parihṛtya payāṃsi viśiṣyopavasanti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 5 18]
{BaudhŚS, 16, 6}
atha śvo bhūte caturviṃśaṃ chandomam upayanti bṛhatsāmānam | [BaudhŚS, 16, 6 1]

avivākyam etad ahar bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 16, 6 5]
naitad ahar anyonyasmā upahatāya vyāhuḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 6 6]

vibrūyād iti vai no brāhmaṇaṃ bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 16, 6 9]
naitad ādriyeta | [BaudhŚS, 16, 6 10]
nādriyeteti sthitiḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 6 11]
ananuṣṭubham etad ahar bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 16, 6 12]
nānuṣṭubho 'dhīyate | [BaudhŚS, 16, 6 13]
te ced anuṣṭubha uddharerann adhvaryur anuṣṭubha uddharet | [BaudhŚS, 16, 6 14]
amūr yā upa sūrye yābhir vā sūryaḥ saha tā no hinvantv adhvaram ity etayā sauryā gāyatryā vasatīvarīr gṛhṇīyāt | [BaudhŚS, 16, 6 15]
hṛde tvā manase tvety apoddhṛtyaitām anyayā saumyā gāyatryā rājānam upāvaharet | [BaudhŚS, 16, 6 16]
viṣṇo tvaṃ no antama ity apoddhṛtyaitām anyayā vaiṣṇavyā gāyatryā rājānam upatiṣṭheta | [BaudhŚS, 16, 6 17]
sa u ced avidvān anuṣṭubham abhivyāharati atyakramiṣam iti hotre prāha | [BaudhŚS, 16, 6 18]
hotānāptasyāpayitā | [BaudhŚS, 16, 6 19]
hotāsya tad akṣarair apivayati | [BaudhŚS, 16, 6 20]
sa u cen manyetāmitakāmo vā aham asmi yad ṛṅmayaṃ vede yajurmayam eva tad yāv evākṣaryau vedau tau saṃpādayetām iti naitad ādriyeta | [BaudhŚS, 16, 6 21]
nādriyeteti sthitiḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 6 22]
saṃtiṣṭhata eṣa caturviṃśo 'gniṣṭomo rathaṃtarasāmā | [BaudhŚS, 16, 6 23]
{BaudhŚS, 16, 7}
tasmin saṃsthite samiddhārā yanti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 7 1]
āhṛtya samidha āgnīdhrīye saṃnyasyanti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 7 2]
teṣu samanvārabdheṣv āhavanīye sruvāhutiṃ juhoti prajāpataye svāheti manasā | [BaudhŚS, 16, 7 3]
atha sadaḥ prasarpanti tūṣṇīṃstomāya | [BaudhŚS, 16, 7 4]
samprasṛptān viditvādhvaryur manasaiva prāṅ drutvā manasemāṃ pātraṃ kṛtvā manasānyaṃ grahaṃ prajāpataye gṛhṇāti upayāmagṛhīto 'si prajāpataye tvā juṣṭaṃ gṛhṇāmīti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 7 5]
yad idaṃ kiṃ ca tad iti manasā parimṛjya sādayati eṣa te yoniḥ prajāpataye tveti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 7 6]

tasmā adhvaryuḥ pratigṛṇāti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 7 18]
{BaudhŚS, 16, 8}
oṃ hotas tathā hotaḥ satyaṃ hotar arātsma hotar iti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 8 1]

tasmā u pratiprasthātā pratigṛṇāti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 8 3]

patnīśāle patnīḥ pariśrayanti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 8 15]
athānatisarpantāv adhvaryū dhiṣṇiyān barhirbhyām audumbarīṃ samanvārabhete iha dhṛtir iha vidhṛtir iha rantir iha ramatir iti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 8 16]

{BaudhŚS, 16, 9}
athātaḥ sarpaṇasyaiva mīmāṃsā | [BaudhŚS, 16, 9 1]

etena ha vai sarpāḥ sasṛpuḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 9 3]
tato vai te jīrṇās tanūr apāghnateti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 9 4]
tad u vā āhur yo vā apathena pratipadyate sthāṇuṃ vā hanti gartaṃ vā patati bhreṣaṃ sa nyeti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 9 5]
vaṣaṭkārapathenaiva sarpeyuḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 9 6]

teṣu samanvārabdheṣv āhavanīye sruvāhutiṃ juhoti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 9 11.1]

rāyaspoṣam iṣam ūrjam asmāsu dīdharat svāheti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 9 11.3]
samutkramya cātvāladeśe japanti vāg aitu vāg upaitu vāṅ mopaitu vāc yad akarma yan nākarma yad atyagāma yan nātyagāma yad atyarīricāma yan nātyarīricāma prajāpatau prajāpatiṃ tat pitaram apyetv iti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 9 12]
tad vācy antataḥ pratitiṣṭhanti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 9 13]

{BaudhŚS, 16, 10}

{BaudhŚS, 16, 11}
athātaḥ paśukﾱpter eva mīmāṃsā | [BaudhŚS, 16, 11 1]

{BaudhŚS, 16, 12}
tad u vā āhur yad dvādaśa dīkṣā dvādaśopasado dvādaśāhaṃ prasutāḥ katham asyaitāny ahānīṣṭāny āprītāni paśumanti bhavantīti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 12 1]

{BaudhŚS, 16, 13}
saṃvatsarāya dīkṣiṣyamāṇāḥ samavasyanti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 13 1]

uto hy ekaḥ śamarathasya kartā bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 16, 13 3]

{BaudhŚS, 16, 14}
teṣāṃ dvādaśa dīkṣā dvādaśopasadaḥ saṃvatsaraṃ prasutāḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 14 1]
na saṃvatsare 'gniṃ cinvītety eka āhuḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 14 2]

taṃ catur upayanti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 14 9]

pṛṣṭhyaḥ ṣaḍahaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 14 11]
sa māsaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 14 12]

trayo 'bhiplavāḥ ṣaḍahās tāny aṣṭādaśāhāni | [BaudhŚS, 16, 14 15]
prāyaṇīyārambhaṇīyau | [BaudhŚS, 16, 14 16]
tāni viṃśatir ahāni | [BaudhŚS, 16, 14 17]

atha vaiṣuvatam | [BaudhŚS, 16, 14 20]
athaitaṃ vaiṣuvate 'hany ekaviṃśam agniṣṭomam upayanti bṛhatsāmānam | [BaudhŚS, 16, 14 21]
tasya sauryo 'tigrāhyaḥ sauryaḥ paśur upālambhyaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 14 22]

tasya mahādivākīrtyaṃ hotuḥ pṛṣṭhaṃ vikarṇaṃ brahmasāmaṃ bhāso 'gniṣṭomaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 14 25]
athordhvaṃ vaiṣuvatāt trīn āvṛttān svarān upayanti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 14 26]
atha viśvajitam upayanti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 14 27]
athāvṛttaṃ pṛṣṭhyaṃ ṣaḍaham upayanti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 14 28]
trayastriṃśaprabhṛtyāgrayaṇāgram etad ahar bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 16, 14 29]
athāvṛttam evābhiplavaṃ ṣaḍaham upayanti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 14 30]
{BaudhŚS, 16, 15}
jyotir agniṣṭoma āyur ukthyo gaur ukthya āyur ukthyo gaur ukthyo jyotir evāgniṣṭomaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 15 1]
taṃ tathaiva catur upayanti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 15 2]
bṛhad rathaṃtaraṃ bṛhad rathaṃtaram iti viparyāsaṃ pṛṣṭhe bhavataḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 15 3]
pṛṣṭhyaḥ ṣaḍahaḥ purastāt | [BaudhŚS, 16, 15 4]
sa māsaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 15 5]
tenaivaṃ sampannena pañca māsān yanti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 15 6]
athaitaṃ ṣaṣṭhaṃ māsaṃ sambhāryaṃ saṃbharanti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 15 7]
dvāv abhiplavau ṣaḍahau tāni dvādaśāhāni | [BaudhŚS, 16, 15 8]
goāyuṣī tāni caturdaśa | [BaudhŚS, 16, 15 9]
catvāry ūrdhvaṃ vaiṣuvatāt tāny aṣṭādaśa | [BaudhŚS, 16, 15 10]
daśarātro mahāvrataṃ cātirātraś ca | [BaudhŚS, 16, 15 11]
sa māsaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 15 12]
tad etan māsipṛṣṭhaṃ gavāmayanam | [BaudhŚS, 16, 15 13]
{BaudhŚS, 16, 16}
anutsargaṃ bṛhadrathaṃtarābhyām itvottame māsi sakṛt pṛṣṭhāny upeyuḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 16 1]
tad dvitīyaṃ gavāmayanam | [BaudhŚS, 16, 16 2]
daśamāsyaṃ tṛtīyam | [BaudhŚS, 16, 16 3]
abhiplavāś cākṣīyanti ca tad aṅgirasāmayanam | [BaudhŚS, 16, 16 4]
pṛṣṭhyāś cākṣīyanti ca tad ādityānām ayanam | [BaudhŚS, 16, 16 5]
agniṣṭomāś cākṣīyanti ca tat prajāpater ayanam | [BaudhŚS, 16, 16 6]
prāyaṇīyodayanīyāv abhito madhye 'gniṣṭomās tad dvitīyaṃ prajāpaterayanam | [BaudhŚS, 16, 16 7]
sarvāgniṣṭomā eva syur iti tat tṛtīyaṃ prajāpaterayanam | [BaudhŚS, 16, 16 8]
athāto grahakﾱpter eva mīmāṃsā | [BaudhŚS, 16, 16 9]
taddhaitad eke sārasvatavaiṣṇavau grahau gṛhṇanti prāyaṇīyād evāgre 'tirātrād odayanīyāt vāg vai sarasvatī yajño viṣṇus te vācaṃ caiva yajñaṃ ca madhyataḥ parigṛhyānārtā udṛcaṃ gamiṣyāma iti vadantaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 16 10]
tad u vā āhur yad vācā yajñas tāyate tena sarasvaty āptā yad u yajñas tena viṣṇuḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 16 11]
na vai no brāhmaṇaṃ bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 16, 16 12]
sārasvatavaiṣṇavau grahau gṛhṇīyād iti naitad ādriyeta | [BaudhŚS, 16, 16 13]
nādriyeteti sthitiḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 16 14]
{BaudhŚS, 16, 17}
athāto 'ṃśvadābhyayor eva grahaṇam | [BaudhŚS, 16, 17 1]
prāyaṇīye 'dābhyaṃ gṛhṇīyād aṃśuṃ vaiṣuvate 'dābhyaṃ mahāvrata ubhau prāyaṇīya ubhau vaiṣuvata ubhau mahāvrate | [BaudhŚS, 16, 17 2]
yatra kva caivainau gṛhṇīyād ity etad aparam | [BaudhŚS, 16, 17 3]
athātaḥ paraḥsāmnām eva grahaṇam | [BaudhŚS, 16, 17 4]
te vā ete paraḥsāmānaḥ purastād vaiṣuvatāt tryaham anvaham itaḥ parāñco gṛhyante upayāmagṛhīto 'si adbhyas tvauṣadhībhyo juṣṭaṃ gṛhṇāmi upayāmagṛhīto 'si oṣadhībhyas tvā prajābhyo juṣṭaṃ gṛhṇāmi upayāmagṛhīto 'si prajābhyas tvā prajāpataye juṣṭaṃ gṛhṇāmīti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 17 5]
atha vaiṣuvate 'hni śukrāgrā grahā gṛhyante | [BaudhŚS, 16, 17 6]
samānaṃ karmāgrayaṇād grahāt | [BaudhŚS, 16, 17 7]
āgrayaṇaṃ gṛhītvā trīn paraḥsāmno gṛhṇāti upayāmagṛhīto 'si adbhyas tvauṣadhībhyo juṣṭaṃ gṛhṇāmi upayāmagṛhīto 'si oṣadhībhyas tvā prajābhyo juṣṭaṃ gṛhṇāmi upayāmagṛhīto 'si prajābhyas tvā prajāpataye juṣṭaṃ gṛhṇāmīti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 17 8]
atha sauryarcā sauryam atigrāhyaṃ gṛhṇāti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 17 9]
{BaudhŚS, 16, 18}
taraṇir viśvadarśata ity anudrutyopayāmagṛhīto 'si sūryāya tvā bhrājasvate juṣṭaṃ gṛhṇāmīti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 18 1]
parimṛjya sādayaty eṣa te yoniḥ sūryāya tvā bhrājasvata iti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 18 2]
athāvṛttān gṛhṇāty upayāmagṛhīto 'si prajābhyas tvā prajāpataye juṣṭaṃ gṛhṇāmy upayāmagṛhīto 'si oṣadhībhyas tvā prajābhyo juṣṭaṃ gṛhṇāmy upayāmagṛhīto 'si adbhyas tvauṣadhībhyo juṣṭaṃ gṛhṇāmīti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 18 3]
saptaitad ahar atigrāhyā gṛhyanta iti brāhmaṇam | [BaudhŚS, 16, 18 4]
athordhvaṃ vaiṣuvatāt tryaham anvaham āvṛttān eva gṛhṇāti vaiśvakarmaṇādityābhyāṃ viparyāsam | [BaudhŚS, 16, 18 5]
upayāmagṛhīto 'si prajābhyas tvā prajāpataye juṣṭaṃ gṛhṇāmīti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 18 6]
atha vaiśvakarmaṇam | [BaudhŚS, 16, 18 7]
viśvakarman haviṣā vāvṛdhāna ity anudrutyopayāmagṛhīto 'si oṣadhībhyas tvā prajābhyo juṣṭaṃ gṛhṇāmīti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 18 8]
athādityam | [BaudhŚS, 16, 18 9]
aditir na uruṣyatv ity anudrutyopayāmagṛhīto 'si adbhyas tvauṣadhībhyo juṣṭaṃ gṛhṇāmīti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 18 10]
atha vaiśvakarmaṇam | [BaudhŚS, 16, 18 11]
athādityam | [BaudhŚS, 16, 18 12]
athordhvaṃ tryahād vaiśvakarmaṇādityābhyām eva viparyāsam ety ā mahāvratāt | [BaudhŚS, 16, 18 13]
tāv ubhau saha mahāvrate gṛhyete | [BaudhŚS, 16, 18 14]
athaitaṃ mahāvratīye 'hni prājāpatyam atigrāhyaṃ gṛhṇāti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 18 15]
tve kratum api vṛñjanti viśva ity anudrutyopayāmagṛhīto 'si prajāpataye tvā juṣṭaṃ gṛhṇāmīti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 18 16]
parimṛjya sādayaty eṣa te yoniḥ prajāpataye tveti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 18 17]
{BaudhŚS, 16, 19}
athātaḥ paśukﾱpter eva mīmāṃsā | [BaudhŚS, 16, 19 1]
uktaindrāgnānāṃ praśaṃsā | [BaudhŚS, 16, 19 2]

{BaudhŚS, 16, 20}
śvo mahāvratam ity upakalpayate 'parimitān rathān aparimitān dundubhīṃs tāvata uv evājisṛtaś carma ceḍasaṃvartaṃ ca bhūmidundubhim ārṣabhaṃ carma salāṅgūlaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ ca śūdraṃ cārdraṃ ca carmakartam | [BaudhŚS, 16, 20 1]

{BaudhŚS, 16, 21}

taṃ kāla eva śastryātṛṇatti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 21 2]

prastute sāmni saṃpraiṣam āha ājisṛta ājiṃ dhāvata dundubhīn samāghnata abhiṣotāro 'bhiṣuṇuta agnīd āśiraṃ vinayolūkhalam udvādaya pratiprasthātaḥ saumyasya viddhi iti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 21 13]
yathāsaṃpraiṣaṃ te kurvanti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 21 14]

{BaudhŚS, 16, 22}
bhadram u nāma sāmāsti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 22 1]

{BaudhŚS, 16, 23}

{BaudhŚS, 16, 24}

{BaudhŚS, 16, 25}

tāyate dvitīye 'hany ukthyaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 25 6]
tasya pañcadaśaṃ prātaḥsavanaṃ saptadaśaṃ mādhyaṃdinaṃ savanam ekaviṃśaṃ tṛtīyasavanam | [BaudhŚS, 16, 25 7]
sa dākṣiṇāni hutvāgnīdhre sruvāhutiṃ juhoti ūrg asy āṅgirasy ūrṇamradā ūrjaṃ me yaccha pāhi mā mā hiṃsīḥ sā mā sahasra ābhaja prajayā paśubhiḥ saha punar māviśatād rayir iti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 25 8]
vehad eteṣāṃ trayāṇāṃ triṃśacchatānāṃ prathamā nīyate | [BaudhŚS, 16, 25 9]
ahīnasaṃtatiṃ karoti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 25 10]
tāyate tṛtīye 'hann atirātraḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 25 11]
tasya saptadaśaṃ prātaḥsavanam ekaviṃśaṃ mādhyaṃdinaṃ savanaṃ triṇava ārbhavaḥ pavamānas trayastriṃśam agniṣṭomasāmaikaviṃśāny ukthāni saṣoḍaśikāni | [BaudhŚS, 16, 25 12]
ṣoḍaśaṃ prathamaṃ rātrisāma pañcadaśānītarāṇi trivṛd rāthaṃtaraḥ sandhiḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 25 13]
sa dākṣiṇāni hutvāgnīdhre sruvāhutiṃ juhoti tvaṃ sahasrasya pratiṣṭhāsi vaiṣṇavo vāmanas tvam | [BaudhŚS, 16, 25 14.1]
sā mā sahasra ābhaja prajayā paśubhiḥ saha punar māviśatād rayir iti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 25 14.2]
vāmana eteṣāṃ trayāṇāṃ catvāriṃśacchatānāṃ prathamo nīyate | [BaudhŚS, 16, 25 15]
nātrāhīnasaṃtatiṃ karoti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 25 16]
{BaudhŚS, 16, 26}
athaitāṃ sahasratamīm uttareṇāgnīdhraṃ paryāṇīyāhavanīyasyānte droṇakalaśam avaghrāpayed ājighra kalaśaṃ mahi urudhārā payasvati ā tvā viśantv indavaḥ samudram iva sindhavaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 26 1.1]
sā mā sahasra ābhaja prajayā paśubhiḥ saha punar māviśatād rayir iti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 26 1.2]
prajayaivainaṃ paśubhī rayyā samardhayati prajāvān paśumān rayimān bhavati ya evaṃ veda iti brāhmaṇam | [BaudhŚS, 16, 26 2]
atha vai bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 16, 26 3]
tayā sahāgnīdhraṃ paretya purastāt pratīcyāṃ tiṣṭhantyāṃ juhuyād iti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 26 4]
sa tayā sahāgnīdhraṃ paretya purastāt pratīcyāṃ tiṣṭhantyāṃ juhoty ubhā jigyathur na parājayethe na parājigye kataraś canainoḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 26 5.1]
indraś ca viṣṇo yad apaspṛdhethām tredhā sahasraṃ vi tad airayethām iti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 26 5.2]
tredhāvibhaktaṃ vai trirātre sahasram | [BaudhŚS, 16, 26 6]
sāhasrīm evaināṃ karoti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 26 7]
sahasrasyaivaināṃ mātrāṃ karotīti brāhmaṇam | [BaudhŚS, 16, 26 8]
athāsyai rūpāṇi juhoty añjyetāyai svāhā kṛṣṇāyai svāhā śvetāyai svāheti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 26 9]
athāsyā upotthāya nāmabhir dakṣiṇaṃ karṇam ājapatīḍe rante 'dite sarasvati priye preyasi mahi viśruti etāni te aghniye nāmāni sukṛtaṃ mā deveṣu brūtād iti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 26 10]
devebhya evainam āvedayaty anv enaṃ devā budhyante iti brāhmaṇam | [BaudhŚS, 16, 26 11]
{BaudhŚS, 16, 27}
athaitāṃ sahasratamīm antareṇa cātvālotkarāv udīcīṃ nīyamānām anumantrayate sā mā suvargaṃ lokaṃ gamaya sā mā jyotiṣmantaṃ lokaṃ gamaya sā mā sarvān puṇyān lokān gamaya sā mā pratiṣṭhāṃ gamaya prajayā paśubhiḥ saha punar māviśatād rayir iti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 27 1]
prajayaivainaṃ paśubhī rayyāṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati | [BaudhŚS, 16, 27 2]
prajāvān paśumān rayimān bhavati ya evaṃ veda iti brāhmaṇam | [BaudhŚS, 16, 27 3]
atha vai bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 16, 27 4]
tām agnīdhe vā brahmaṇe vā hotre vodgātre vādhvaryave vā dadyāt | [BaudhŚS, 16, 27 5]
sahasram asya sā dattā bhavati sahasram asya pratigṛhītaṃ bhavatīti brāhmaṇam | [BaudhŚS, 16, 27 6]
atha vai bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 16, 27 7]
yas tām avidvān pratigṛhṇāti tāṃ pratigṛhṇīyād ekāsi na sahasram ekāṃ tvā bhūtāṃ pratigṛhṇāmi na sahasram ekā mā bhūtāviśa mā sahasram iti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 27 8]
ekām evaināṃ bhūtāṃ pratigṛhṇāti na sahasraṃ ya evaṃ veda iti brāhmaṇam | [BaudhŚS, 16, 27 9]
atha vai bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 16, 27 10]
syonāsi suṣadā suśevā syonā māviśa suṣadā māviśa suśevā māviśa ity āha | [BaudhŚS, 16, 27 11]
syonaivainaṃ suṣadā suśevā bhūtāviśati nainaṃ hinastīti brāhmaṇam | [BaudhŚS, 16, 27 12]
atha vai bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 16, 27 13]
brahmavādino vadanti sahasraṃ sahasratamy anvetī3 sahasratamīṃ sahasrā3m iti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 27 14]
yat prācīm utsṛjet sahasraṃ sahasratamy anviyāt | [BaudhŚS, 16, 27 15]
tat sahasram aprajñātram | [BaudhŚS, 16, 27 16]
suvargaṃ lokaṃ na prajānīyāt | [BaudhŚS, 16, 27 17]
pratīcīm utsṛjati | [BaudhŚS, 16, 27 18]
tāṃ sahasram anu paryāvartate | [BaudhŚS, 16, 27 19]
sā prajānatī suvargaṃ lokam eti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 27 20]
yajamānam abhyutsṛjatīti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 27 21]
tāṃ purastāt pratīcīṃ yajamānam abhyutsṛjati | [BaudhŚS, 16, 27 22]
kṣipre sahasraṃ prajāyata uttamā nīyate prathamā devān gacchatīti brāhmaṇam | [BaudhŚS, 16, 27 23]
tena haitena rauhiṇeyaḥ krothuniḥ kaulāśvo yāska ṛtumukheṣu vihṛteneje | [BaudhŚS, 16, 27 24]
atho hājagāma maśako gārgya āruṇer antevāsī | [BaudhŚS, 16, 27 25]
sa ha saṃsthām adṛṣṭvovāca nanu mata ekāhā3ṃ iti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 27 26]
neti hainaṃ pratyuvāca | [BaudhŚS, 16, 27 27]
taṃ hopeyāya | [BaudhŚS, 16, 27 28]
tasmā u hainaṃ sa uvāca | [BaudhŚS, 16, 27 29]
tena ha sma samastenaiva yajate | [BaudhŚS, 16, 27 30]
tam etaṃ gargatrirātra ity ācakṣate | [BaudhŚS, 16, 27 31]
{BaudhŚS, 16, 28}
caturo vīrān avarurutsamānaś catūrātrāya dīkṣate | [BaudhŚS, 16, 28 1]
tasyāparimitā dīkṣā dvādaśopasadaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 28 2]
tasyāhāny agniṣṭomā evaite caturviṃśāḥ pavamānā udyatstomāḥ syur ity etad ekam | [BaudhŚS, 16, 28 3]
eko 'gniṣṭomo dvāv ukthyāv athātirātraḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 28 4]
chandogān nu sāmavikalpaṃ pṛccheyur ity etad aparam | [BaudhŚS, 16, 28 5]
atriṃ śraddhādevaṃ yajamānaṃ catvāri vīryāṇi nopānaman teja indriyaṃ brahmavarcasam annādyam iti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 28 6]
etān kāmān avarurutsamānaś catūrātrāya dīkṣate | [BaudhŚS, 16, 28 7]
tasyāparimitā dīkṣā dvādaśopasadaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 28 8]
tasyāhāny agniṣṭomā evaite catuṣṭomāḥ syur ity etad ekam | [BaudhŚS, 16, 28 9]
eko 'gniṣṭomo dvāv ukthyāv athātirātraḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 28 10]
chandogān nu sāmavikalpaṃ pṛccheyur ity etad aparam | [BaudhŚS, 16, 28 11]
puṣṭikāmaś catūrātrāya dīkṣate | [BaudhŚS, 16, 28 12]
tasyāparimitā dīkṣā dvādaśopasadaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 28 13]
atha vai bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 16, 28 14]
puroḍāśinya upasado bhavantīti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 28 15]
prathame catūrātra āgneya ājya āgneyam aṣṭākapālaṃ sāyaṃ prātar anvavadhāya juhoti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 28 16]
dvitīye catūrātre saumya ājye saumyaṃ catuṣkapālaṃ sāyaṃ prātar anvavadhāya juhoti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 28 17]
tṛtīye catūrātre vaiṣṇava ājye vaiṣṇavaṃ trikapālaṃ sāyaṃ prātar anvavadhāya juhoti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 28 18]
tasya trivṛtsaptadaśau viparyāsaṃ stomau bhavataḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 28 19]
prāṇo vai trivṛd annam | [BaudhŚS, 16, 28 20]
saptadaśaḥ prajāpatiḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 28 21]
prāṇāc ca khalu vā idam annādyāc ca parigṛhya prajāpatiḥ prājāyata | [BaudhŚS, 16, 28 22]
prāṇāc caivaitad annādyāc ca parigṛhya yajamānaḥ prajāyate | [BaudhŚS, 16, 28 23]
tasyāhāny agniṣṭomā evaite catustriṃśapavamānāḥ syur ity etad ekam | [BaudhŚS, 16, 28 24]
eko 'gniṣṭomo dvāv ukthyāv athātirātraḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 28 25]
chandogān nu sāmavikalpaṃ pṛccheyur ity etad aparam | [BaudhŚS, 16, 28 26]
{BaudhŚS, 16, 29}
prajātikāmo vā vyāvṛtkāmo vā paśukāmo vā vāco vāntaṃ parijigāṃsan pañcarātrāya dīkṣate | [BaudhŚS, 16, 29 1]
tasyāparimitā dīkṣā dvādaśopasadaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 29 2]
tasyāhāni trivṛd agniṣṭomaḥ pañcadaśa ukthyaḥ saptadaśa ukthyaḥ pañcaviṃśo 'gniṣṭomo mahāvratavān viśvajit sarvapṛṣṭho 'tirātraḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 29 3]
sārasvatenāyanenaiṣyanto dvayīr gā upakalpayanta ṛṣabhaikādaśā anyā ṛṣabhaikaśatā anyāḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 29 4]
teṣām āśvatthī havirdhānaṃ cāgnīdhraṃ ca bhavataḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 29 5]
taddhi suvargyam | [BaudhŚS, 16, 29 6]
cakrīvatī bhavataḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 29 7]
ulūkhalabudhna eṣāṃ yūpo bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 16, 29 8]
te sarasvatyai jaghanyodake dīkṣante | [BaudhŚS, 16, 29 9]
teṣām ayam eva trivṛd agniṣṭomaḥ saṃtiṣṭhate | [BaudhŚS, 16, 29 10]
tasmin saṃsthite 'bhi yūpaṃ vahanty abhi dhiṣṇiyān haranty agniṣṭhe 'nasi samavaśamayante yad eṣāṃ samavaśamayitavyaṃ bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 16, 29 11]
te 'nenaiva pṛṣṭhyena ṣaḍahena pratipadyante | [BaudhŚS, 16, 29 12]
aharahaḥ śamyānyāse śamyānyāse yajamānā ākrośanto 'jyānim icchamānā yadā daśa śataṃ kurvanty athaikam utthānam | [BaudhŚS, 16, 29 13]
yadā śataṃ sahasraṃ kurvanty athaikam utthānam | [BaudhŚS, 16, 29 14]
yadaiṣāṃ pramīyeta yadā vā jīyerann athaikam utthānaṃ plākṣe vā prasravaṇe | [BaudhŚS, 16, 29 15]
{BaudhŚS, 16, 30}
athāto munyayanam ity ācakṣate | [BaudhŚS, 16, 30 1]
śramaṇaḥ khārīvivadhī sarasvatyai jaghanyodake 'gnaye vratapataye puroḍāśam aṣṭākapālaṃ nirvapati | [BaudhŚS, 16, 30 2]
sā prasiddheṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate | [BaudhŚS, 16, 30 3]
athaitāṃ savaneṣṭiṃ nirvapaty āgneyam aṣṭākapālam aindram ekādaśakapālaṃ vaiśvadevaṃ dvādaśakapālam iti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 30 4]
tayā samastayā vā vihṛtayā vā pratipadyate | [BaudhŚS, 16, 30 5]
aharahaḥ śamyānyāse śamyānyāse yajamāna ākrośann ajyānim icchamāno yadainaṃ pratirādhnuvanti yadā vāsyaitaṃ khārīvivadham ācchindanty athaikam utthānaṃ plākṣe vā prasravaṇe | [BaudhŚS, 16, 30 6]
{BaudhŚS, 16, 31}
paśukāmaḥ saptarātrāya dīkṣate | [BaudhŚS, 16, 31 1]
tasyāparimitā dīkṣā dvādaśopasadaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 31 2]
tasyāhāni trivṛd agniṣṭomaḥ pañcadaśa ukthyaḥ saptadaśa ukthya ekaviṃśa ukthyas triṇava ukthyaḥ pañcaviṃśo 'gniṣṭomo mahāvratavān viśvajit sarvapṛṣṭho 'tirātraḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 31 3]
bṛhadrathaṃtare pūrveṣv ahaḥsūpetya pratyakṣaṃ viśvajiti pṛṣṭhāny upayanti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 31 4]
brahmavarcasakāmo 'ṣṭarātrāya dīkṣate | [BaudhŚS, 16, 31 5]
tasyāparimitā dīkṣā dvādaśopasadaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 31 6]
tasyāhāni trivṛd agniṣṭomaḥ pañcadaśa ukthyaḥ saptadaśa ukthya ekaviṃśa ukthyas triṇava ukthyas trayastriṃśa ukthyaḥ pañcaviṃśo 'gniṣṭomo mahāvratavān viśvajit sarvapṛṣṭho 'tirātraḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 31 7]
prajāsu vā kṣudyuktāsu jyogāmayāvī vā navarātrāya dīkṣate | [BaudhŚS, 16, 31 8]
tasyāparimitā dīkṣā dvādaśopasadaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 31 9]
tasyāhāni jyotir gaur āyur ity etam eva tryahaṃ trir upayanti | [BaudhŚS, 16, 31 10]
teṣām āyuratirātra uttamam ahar bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 16, 31 11]
prajātikāmo vā vyāvṛtkāmo vābhicaran vābhicaryamāṇo vā daśarātrāya dīkṣiṣyamāṇo daśahotāraṃ hutvā daśarātrāya dīkṣate | [BaudhŚS, 16, 31 12]
tasyāparimitā dīkṣā dvādaśopasadaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 31 13]
tasyāhāni trivṛd agniṣṭomo 'gniṣṭud āgneyīṣu bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 16, 31 14]
pañcadaśa ukthya aindrīṣu | [BaudhŚS, 16, 31 15]
trivṛd agniṣṭomo vaiśvadevīṣu | [BaudhŚS, 16, 31 16]
saptadaśo 'gniṣṭomaḥ prājāpatyāsu tīvrasomaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 31 17]
ekaviṃśa ukthyaḥ saurīṣu | [BaudhŚS, 16, 31 18]
saptadaśo 'gniṣṭomaḥ prājāpatyāsūpahavyaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 31 19]
triṇavāv agniṣṭomāv abhita aindrīṣu | [BaudhŚS, 16, 31 20]
trayastriṃśa ukthyo vaiśvadevīṣu | [BaudhŚS, 16, 31 21]
viśvajit sarvapṛṣṭho 'tirātraḥ | [BaudhŚS, 16, 31 22]
{BaudhŚS, 16, 32}

{BaudhŚS, 16, 36}

{BaudhŚS, 18, 1}
bṛhaspatisavena yakṣyamāṇo bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 1 1]
sa upakalpayate 'śvacatustriṃśā dakṣiṇāḥ kṛṣṇājinaṃ suvarṇarajatau ca rukmau parṇamayaṃ pātram ājyam abhiṣecanāya | [BaudhŚS, 18, 1 2]
atha vai brāhmaṇaṃ bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 1 3]
parisrajī hotā bhavaty aruṇo mirmiras triśukra iti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 1 4]
eṣa ha vai parisrajī yaḥ khalatiḥ parikeśyaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 1 5]
atha haiṣa mirmiro yaḥ śuklo viklidhas tilakavān piṅgākṣaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 1 6]
atha haiṣa triśukro yas trivedaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 1 7]
dīkṣate | [BaudhŚS, 18, 1 8]
tasyaikarātrīṇasya somaṃ krīṇanti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 1 9]
tisra upasadaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 1 10]
tāyate trivṛd agniṣṭomo rathaṃtarasāmā pravargyavān | [BaudhŚS, 18, 1 11]
gāyatrīṣv ekastomaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 1 12]
prajñātaṃ devasuvāṃ haviṣāṃ karaṇam | [BaudhŚS, 18, 1 13]
tasya bārhaspatyo 'tigrāhyaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 1 14]
bārhaspatyaḥ paśur upālambhyaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 1 15]
samānam ābhiṣekasya kālāt | [BaudhŚS, 18, 1 16]
abhiṣekasya kāle yajamānāyatane kṛṣṇājinaṃ prācīnagrīvam uttaralomopastṛṇāti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 1 17]
tad yajamānaṃ prāñcam upaveśya suvarṇarajatābhyāṃ rukmābhyāṃ paryupāsya parṇamaye pātra ājyam ānīyābhiṣiñcati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 1 18.1]
bṛhaspatiḥ prathamaṃ jāyamāno maho jyotiṣaḥ parame vyoman | [BaudhŚS, 18, 1 18.2]
saptāsyas tuvijāto raveṇa vi saptaraśmir adhamat tamāṃsi | [BaudhŚS, 18, 1 18.3]
devasya tvā savituḥ prasave 'śvinor bāhubhyāṃ pūṣṇo hastābhyāṃ sarasvatyai vāco yantur yantreṇa bṛhaspatisavenābhiṣiñcāmīti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 1 19]
samunmṛṣṭe samutkrośantīti samānam ā mukhasya vimārjanāt | [BaudhŚS, 18, 1 20]
{BaudhŚS, 18, 2}
tasya prātaḥsavane sanneṣu nārāśaṃseṣv ekādaśa dakṣiṇā nīyante | [BaudhŚS, 18, 2 1]
ekādaśa mādhyaṃdine savane sanneṣu nārāśaṃseṣu | [BaudhŚS, 18, 2 2]
aśvadvādaśās tṛtīyasavane sanneṣu nārāśaṃseṣu | [BaudhŚS, 18, 2 3]
mādhyaṃdina eva savane 'śvaṃ dadyād iti ha smāha maudgalyaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 2 4]
sa vā eṣa naimārjano yajñaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 2 5]
sa yathā ha vā iyaṃ gaireyī nadī nimṛjanty ety evaṃ ha vā eṣa etena yajñakratuneṣṭvā pāpmānaṃ bhrātṛvyaṃ nimṛjann eti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 2 6]
sa etasminn eva pūrvapakṣe catuṣṭomenāgniṣṭomena yajeta purā bhreṣāc chāntyai | [BaudhŚS, 18, 2 7]
rājā rājasūyenejāna icchati bṛhaspatisavenābhiṣicyeyeti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 2 8]
tad u vā āhur na vai rājasūyābhiṣikto 'nyena yajñakratunābhiṣicyeta | [BaudhŚS, 18, 2 9]
apratyavarohī ha bhavatīti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 2 10]
ubhābhyāṃ brahmakṣatrābhyām abhiṣicyā ity abhiṣicyetaiveti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 2 11]
dīkṣate | [BaudhŚS, 18, 2 12]
tasya tisro dīkṣās tisra upasadaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 2 13]
samānam ābhiṣekasya kālāt | [BaudhŚS, 18, 2 14]
abhiṣekasya kāle mādhyaṃdinīyā evainaṃ camasā nimṛjanto yanti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 2 15]
caturviṃśa eṣa bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 2 16]
rājā rājasūyena yakṣyamāṇa ādhyāyati triṣu varṇeṣv abhiṣikteṣv adhyabhiṣicyeya purohite sthapatau sūta iti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 2 17]
purohito dīkṣate | [BaudhŚS, 18, 2 18]
tasya tisro dīkṣās tisra upasadaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 2 19]
samānam ābhiṣekasya kālāt | [BaudhŚS, 18, 2 20]
abhiṣekasya kāle śukrāmanthinoḥ saṃsrāveṇābhiṣiñcati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 2 21]
catuṣṭoma eṣa bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 2 22]
{BaudhŚS, 18, 3}
sthapati sthapatisavena yakṣyamāṇo bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 3 1]
sa upakalpayata ārṣabhaṃ carma suvarṇarajatau ca rukmāv audumbaraṃ pātraṃ dadhy abhiṣecanāya | [BaudhŚS, 18, 3 2]
dīkṣate | [BaudhŚS, 18, 3 3]
tasya tisro dīkṣās tisra upasadaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 3 4]
āgneyasya mārutī pṛśniḥ paṣṭhauhy upālambhyā bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 3 5]
sapta havīṃṣi prātaḥsavanīyān anuvartante yad āgneyo bhavaty agnimukhād vyṛddhir ity etāni | [BaudhŚS, 18, 3 6]
samānam ābhiṣekasya kālāt | [BaudhŚS, 18, 3 7]
abhiṣekasya kāle yajamānāyatana ārṣabhaṃ carma prācīnagrīvam uttaralomopastṛṇāti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 3 8]
tad yajamānaṃ prāñcam upaveśya suvarṇarajatābhyāṃ rukmābhyāṃ paryupāsyaudumbare pātre dadhy ānīyābhiṣiñcati devasya tvā savituḥ prasave 'śvinor bāhubhyāṃ pūṣṇo hastābhyāṃ sarasvatyai vāco yantur yantreṇa sthapatisavenābhiṣiñcāmīti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 3 9]
samunmṛṣṭe samutkrośantīti samānam ā mukhasya vimārjanāt | [BaudhŚS, 18, 3 10]
sa eṣa sthapatisavaḥ saptadaśo 'gniṣṭomaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 3 11]
eṣa eva sthapatisavaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 3 12]
eṣa vaiśyasavaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 3 13]
eṣa māsasavaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 3 14]
māsā hainenātaḥ pūrvam ījire | [BaudhŚS, 18, 3 15]
{BaudhŚS, 18, 4}
sūtaḥ sūtasavena yakṣyamāṇo bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 4 1]
sa upakalpayate kṛṣṇājinaṃ suvarṇarajatau ca rukmau parṇamayaṃ pātraṃ hiraṇyaṃ ghṛtam abhiṣecanāya | [BaudhŚS, 18, 4 2]
dīkṣate | [BaudhŚS, 18, 4 3]
tasya tisro dīkṣās tisra upasadaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 4 4]
aṣṭau havīṃṣi prātaḥsavanīyān anuvartante yad āgneyo bhavaty āgneyo vai brāhmaṇa ity etāni | [BaudhŚS, 18, 4 5]
samānam ābhiṣekasya kālāt | [BaudhŚS, 18, 4 6]
abhiṣekasya kāle yajamānāyatane kṛṣṇājinaṃ prācīnagrīvam uttaralomopastṛṇāti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 4 7]
tad yajamānaṃ prāñcam upaveśya suvarṇarajatābhyāṃ rukmābhyāṃ paryupāsya parṇamaye pātre ghṛtam ānīya hiraṇyenotpūyābhiṣiñcati devasya tvā savituḥ prasave 'śvinor bāhubhyāṃ pūṣṇo hastābhyāṃ sarasvatyai vāco yantur yantreṇa sūtasavenābhiṣiñcāmīti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 4 8]
samunmṛṣṭe samutkrośantīti samānam ā mukhasya vimārjanāt | [BaudhŚS, 18, 4 9]
sa eṣa sūtasavaḥ saptadaśo 'gniṣṭomaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 4 10]
eṣa eva sūtasavaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 4 11]
eṣa grāmaṇīsavaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 4 12]
eṣa ṛtusavaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 4 13]
ṛtavo hainenātaḥ pūrvam ījire | [BaudhŚS, 18, 4 14]
{BaudhŚS, 18, 5}
somasavena yakṣyamāṇo bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 5 1]
sa upakalpayate saumīṃ sūtavaśāṃ kṛṣṇājinaṃ suvarṇarajatau ca rukmau parṇamayaṃ pātraṃ payo 'bhiṣecanāya | [BaudhŚS, 18, 5 2]
atha vai brāhmaṇaṃ bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 5 3]
yat kiṃca rājasūyam ṛte somaṃ tat sarvaṃ bhavati iti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 5 4]
sa āmāvāsyena haviṣeṣṭvāṣṭāv ahāny ānumataprabhṛtibhir eti saṃvatsaraṃ cāturmāsyaiḥ saptendraturīyaprabhṛtibhiḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 5 5]
atha ratnināṃ havirbhir yajate | [BaudhŚS, 18, 5 6]
atha devasuvāṃ havirbhir yajate | [BaudhŚS, 18, 5 7]
athaitāṃ saumīṃ sūtavaśām ālabhate | [BaudhŚS, 18, 5 8]
tasyā asamudite yajamānāyatane kṛṣṇājinaṃ prācīnagrīvam uttaralomopastṛṇāti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 5 9]
tad yajamānaṃ prāñcam upaveśya suvarṇarajatābhyāṃ rukmābhyāṃ paryupāsya parṇamaye pātre paya ānīyābhiṣiñcati aṣāḍhaṃ yutsu pṛtanāsu paprim suvarṣām apsvāṃ vṛjanasya gopāṃ bhareṣujāṃ sukṣitiṃ suśravasam jayantaṃ tvām anu madema soma | [BaudhŚS, 18, 5 10]
devasya tvā savituḥ prasave 'śvinor bāhubhyāṃ pūṣṇo hastābhyāṃ sarasvatyai vāco yantur yantreṇa somasavenābhiṣiñcāmi iti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 5 11]
samunmṛṣṭe samutkrośantīti samānam ā mukhasya vimārjanāt | [BaudhŚS, 18, 5 12]
atha saṃsṛpāṃ havirbhir yajate | [BaudhŚS, 18, 5 13]
atha pañcahaviṣā diśām aveṣṭyā yajate | [BaudhŚS, 18, 5 14]
atha dvipaśunā paśubandhena yajate | [BaudhŚS, 18, 5 15]
atha sātyadūtānāṃ havirbhir yajate | [BaudhŚS, 18, 5 16]
atha pūrvaiḥ prayujāṃ havirbhir yajate | [BaudhŚS, 18, 5 17]
atha paurṇamāsavaimṛdhābhyām iṣṭvottaraiḥ prayujāṃ havirbhir yajate | [BaudhŚS, 18, 5 18]
atha devikāhavirbhir yajate | [BaudhŚS, 18, 5 19]
atha traidhātavīyayā yajate | [BaudhŚS, 18, 5 20]
atha sautrāmaṇyā yajate | [BaudhŚS, 18, 5 21]
saṃtiṣṭhate somasavo 'rdhacaturdaśair māsaiḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 5 22]
{BaudhŚS, 18, 6}
pṛthisavena yakṣyamāṇo bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 6 1]
sa upakalpayate rohitaṃ carmānaḍuhaṃ suvarṇarajatau ca rukmāv audumbaraṃ droṇaṃ catuḥsrakti catuṣṭayīr apo digbhyaḥ saṃbhṛtāḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 6 2]
atha vai brāhmaṇaṃ bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 6 3]
yat kiṃca rājasūyam anuttaravedīkaṃ tat sarvaṃ bhavatīti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 6 4]
sa āmāvāsyena haviṣeṣṭvāṣṭāv ahāny ānumataprabhṛtibhir eti saptendraturīyaprabhṛtibhiḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 6 5]
atha ratnināṃ havirbhir yajate | [BaudhŚS, 18, 6 6]
atha devasuvāṃ havirbhir yajate | [BaudhŚS, 18, 6 7]
athaitāṃ caturhaviṣam iṣṭiṃ nirvapaty āgneyam aṣṭākapālam aindram ekādaśakapālaṃ vaiśvadevaṃ dvādaśakapālaṃ bārhaspatyaṃ carum iti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 6 8]
tasyā asamudite yajamānāyatane rohitaṃ carmānaḍuhaṃ prācīnagrīvam uttaralomopastṛṇāti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 6 9]
tad yajamānaṃ prāñcam upaveśya suvarṇarajatābhyāṃ rukmābhyāṃ paryupāsyaudumbare droṇe catuṣṭayīr apaḥ samavanīyābhiṣiñcati ye me pañcāśataṃ dadur aśvānāṃ sadhastutiḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 6 10.1]
dyumad agne mahi śravo bṛhat kṛdhi maghonām nṛvad amṛta nṛṇām | [BaudhŚS, 18, 6 10.2]
devasya tvā savituḥ prasave 'śvinor bāhubhyāṃ pūṣṇo hastābhyāṃ sarasvatyai vāco yantur yantreṇa pṛthisavenābhiṣiñcāmīti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 6 11]
samunmṛṣṭe samutkrośantīti samānam ā mukhasya vimārjanāt | [BaudhŚS, 18, 6 12]
atha saṃsṛpāṃ havirbhir yajate | [BaudhŚS, 18, 6 13]
atha pañcahaviṣā diśām aveṣṭyā yajate | [BaudhŚS, 18, 6 14]
athopātītya dvipaśuṃ paśubandhaṃ sātyadūtānāṃ havirbhir yajate | [BaudhŚS, 18, 6 15]
atha pūrvaiḥ prayujāṃ havirbhir yajate | [BaudhŚS, 18, 6 16]
atha paurṇamāsavaimṛdhābhyām iṣṭvottaraiḥ prayujāṃ havirbhir yajate | [BaudhŚS, 18, 6 17]
atha devikāhavirbhir yajate | [BaudhŚS, 18, 6 18]
atha traidhātavīyayā yajate | [BaudhŚS, 18, 6 19]
atha sautrāmaṇyā yajate | [BaudhŚS, 18, 6 20]
saṃtiṣṭhate pṛthisavo 'dhyardhena māsena | [BaudhŚS, 18, 6 21]
{BaudhŚS, 18, 7}
gosavena yakṣyamāṇo bhavati sa upakalpayate 'yutaṃ dakṣiṇāḥ suvarṇarajatau ca rukmau parṇamayaṃ pātraṃ pratidhug abhiṣecanāya | [BaudhŚS, 18, 7 1]
dīkṣate | [BaudhŚS, 18, 7 2]
tasya ṣaḍ dīkṣāḥ ṣaḍ upasadaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 7 3]
samānam ābhiṣekasya kālāt | [BaudhŚS, 18, 7 4]
abhiṣekasya kāle yajamānāyatane kṛṣṇājinamātraṃ veder anuddhataṃ bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 7 5]
tad yajamānaṃ prāñcam upaveśya suvarṇarajatābhyāṃ rukmābhyāṃ paryupāsya parṇamaye pātre pratidhug ānīya bṛhata stotraṃ pratyabhiṣiñcati revaj jātaḥ sahasā vṛddhaḥ kṣatrāṇāṃ kṣatrabhṛttamo vayodhāḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 7 6.1]
mahān mahitve tastabhānaḥ kṣatre rāṣṭre ca jāgṛhi | [BaudhŚS, 18, 7 6.2]
prajāpates tvā parameṣṭhinaḥ svārājyenābhiṣiñcāmi | [BaudhŚS, 18, 7 6.3]
devasya tvā savituḥ prasave 'śvinor bāhubhyāṃ pūṣṇo hastābhyāṃ sarasvatyai vāco yantur yantreṇa gosavenābhiṣiñcāmīti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 7 7]
samunmṛṣṭe samutkrośantīti samānam ā mukhasya vimārjanāt | [BaudhŚS, 18, 7 8]
sa eṣa gosavaḥ ṣaṭtriṃśaḥ sarva ukthya ubhayasāmāyutadakṣiṇaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 7 9]
pavamāne kaṇvarathaṃtaraṃ kurvanti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 7 10]
{BaudhŚS, 18, 8}
odanasavena yakṣyamāṇo bhavati sa upakalpayate rohitaṃ carmānaḍuhaṃ suvarṇarajatau ca rukmau śatamānaṃ ca pravartaṃ caturo varṇān brāhmaṇaṃ rājanyaṃ vaiśyaṃ śūdraṃ caturo rasān madhu surāṃ payo 'paś catvāri pātrāṇi sauvarṇaṃ rājataṃ kāṃsyaṃ mṛnmayaṃ catasro dakṣiṇāḥ śatamānaṃ hiraṇyaṃ tisṛdhanvam aṣṭrāṃ māṣaiḥ pūrṇaṃ kamaṇḍaluṃ catuṣṭayīḥ śalākāḥ parṇamayyau naiyagrodhyāv āśvatthyau phālgunapācyau catvāri nānāvṛkṣyāṇi pātrāṇi saktūṃs trīṇi darbhapuñjīlāny audumbaraṃ droṇaṃ catuḥsrakti catuṣṭayīr apo digbhyaḥ saṃbhṛtāḥ śataṃ ca rathaṃ ca | [BaudhŚS, 18, 8 1]
etenopakﾱptena rohiṇīm āyatīm uparamati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 8 2]
adya rohiṇyeti pūrvāgnim anvavasyaty uttapanīyaṃ śālīno 'nvāhāryapacanam āhitāgniḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 8 3]
athādhvaryur apararātra ādrutya saṃśāsty ekaudanaṃ śrapayateti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 8 4]
taṃ tathā śrapayanti yathā purādityasyodayācchṛto bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 8 5]
udyatā sūryeṇa kārya iti brāhmaṇam | [BaudhŚS, 18, 8 6]
athaitam odanaṃ śrapayitvābhighāryodañcam udvāsayati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 8 7]
athaitāṃ pātrīṃ nirṇijyopastīrya tasyām enam asaṃghnann ivoddharati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 8 8]
sarpirāsecanaṃ kṛtvā prabhūtam ājyam ānīya | [BaudhŚS, 18, 8 9]
athaitāṃś caturo varṇān dakṣiṇata udaṅmukhān upaveśayati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 8 10]
athānvārabdhe yajamāne juhoti siṃhe vyāghra uta yā pṛdākāv iti catasraḥ sruvāhutīḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 8 11]
hutvā hutvaiva saṃsrāvaiḥ pravartam abhighārayati rāḍ asi virāḍ asi saṃrāḍ asi svarāḍ asīti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 8 12]
athaitaṃ pravartam agreṇāhavanīyaṃ paryāhṛtya dakṣiṇato nidadhāti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 8 13]
{BaudhŚS, 18, 9}
athaitat sauvarṇaṃ pātraṃ yācati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 9 1.1]
tasmiṃs tiraḥ pavitraṃ madhv ānīya saktūn opya parṇamayībhyāṃ śalākābhyām upamanthatīndrāya tvā tejasvate tejasvantaṃ śrīṇāmīti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 9 2.1]
tejo 'sīti brāhmaṇāya prayacchati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 9 3.1]
tat te prayacchāmīti brāhmaṇaḥ pratigṛhṇāti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 9 4.1]
atha yajamāno mukhaṃ vimṛṣṭe tejasvad astu me mukham tejasvacchiro astu me | [BaudhŚS, 18, 9 5.1]
tejasvān viśvataḥ pratyaṅ tejasā saṃ pipṛgdhi meti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 9 5.2]
trir ācamya praśaṃsati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 9 6.1]
tasmā etac caiva pātraṃ dadāti śatamānaṃ ca hiraṇyam | [BaudhŚS, 18, 9 7.1]
athaitad rājataṃ pātraṃ yācati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 9 8.1]
tasmiṃs tiraḥ pavitraṃ surām ānīya saktūn opya naiyagrodhībhyāṃ śalākābhyām upamanthatīndrāya tvaujasvata ojasvantaṃ śrīṇāmīti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 9 9.1]
ojo 'sīti rājanyāya prayacchati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 9 10.1]
tat te prayacchāmīti rājanyaḥ pratigṛhṇāti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 9 11.1]
atha yajamāno mukhaṃ vimṛṣṭe ojasvad astu me mukham ojasvacchiro astu me | [BaudhŚS, 18, 9 12.1]
ojasvān viśvataḥ pratyaṅ ojasā saṃ pipṛgdhi meti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 9 12.2]
trir ācamya praśaṃsati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 9 13.1]
tasmā etac caiva pātraṃ dadāti tisṛdhanvaṃ ca | [BaudhŚS, 18, 9 14.1]
athaitat kāṃsyaṃ pātraṃ yācati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 9 15.1]
tasmiṃs tiraḥ pavitraṃ paya ānīya saktūn opyāśvatthībhyāṃ śalākābhyām upamanthatīndrāya tvā payasvate payasvantaṃ śrīṇāmīti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 9 16.1]
payo 'sīti vaiśyāya prayacchati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 9 17.1]
tat te prayacchāmīti vaiśyaḥ pratigṛhṇāti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 9 18.1]
atha yajamāno mukhaṃ vimṛṣṭe payasvad astu me mukham payasvacchiro astu me | [BaudhŚS, 18, 9 19.1]
payasvān viśvataḥ pratyaṅ payasā saṃ pipṛgdhi meti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 9 19.2]
trir ācamya praśaṃsati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 9 20.1]
tasmā etac caiva pātraṃ dadāty aṣṭrāṃ ca | [BaudhŚS, 18, 9 21.1]
athaitan mṛnmayaṃ pātraṃ yācati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 9 22.1]
tasmiṃs tiraḥ pavitram apa ānīya saktūn opya phālgunapācībhyāṃ śalākābhyām upamanthatīndrāya tvāyuṣmata āyuṣmantaṃ śrīṇāmīti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 9 23.1]
āyur asīti śūdrāya prayacchati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 9 24.1]
tat te prayacchāmīti śūdraḥ pratigṛhṇāti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 9 25.1]
atha yajamāno mukhaṃ vimṛṣṭe āyuṣmad astu me mukham āyuṣmacchiro astu me | [BaudhŚS, 18, 9 26.1]
āyuṣmān viśvataḥ pratyaṅ āyuṣā saṃ pipṛgdhi meti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 9 26.2]
trir ācamya praśaṃsati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 9 27.1]
tasmā etac caiva pātraṃ dadāti māṣaiś ca pūrṇaṃ kamaṇḍalum | [BaudhŚS, 18, 9 28.1]
athaitam odanam abhyutsṛpya prāśnāti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 9 29.1]
tasya yan na sahate tad apsu praveśayati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 9 30.1]
atha hiraṇyād ghṛtaṃ niṣpibati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 9 31.1]
niṣpibantam anumantrayate imam agna āyuṣe varcase kṛdhi priyaṃ reto varuṇa soma rājan | [BaudhŚS, 18, 9 32.1]
mātevāsmā adite śarma yaccha viśve devā jaradaṣṭir yathāsad iti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 9 32.2]
athaitaṃ pravartam adbhiḥ prakṣālya dakṣiṇe karṇa ābadhnīte āyuṣ ṭe viśvato dadhad iti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 9 33.1]
athainam anuparivartayate āyur asi viśvāyur asi sarvāyur asi sarvam āyur asīti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 9 34.1]
athainaṃ tribhir darbhapuñjīlaiḥ pavayati yato vāto manojavā yataḥ kṣaranti sindhavaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 9 35.1]
tāsāṃ tvā sarvāsāṃ rucā abhiṣiñcāmi varcaseti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 9 35.2]
athāsya dakṣiṇam akṣikaṭaṃ nyacati samudra ivāsi gahmanā soma ivāsy adābhyaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 9 36.1]
agnir iva viśvataḥ pratyaṅ sūrya iva jyotiṣā vibhūr iti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 9 36.2]
{BaudhŚS, 18, 10}
yāvad evātrādhvaryuś ceṣṭati tāvad eṣa pratiprasthātaudumbare droṇe catuṣṭayīr apaḥ samavanīya caturo grahān gṛhṇāty apāṃ yo dravaṇe rasas tam aham asmā āmuṣyāyaṇāya tejase brahmavarcasāya gṛhṇāmīti parṇamayena | [BaudhŚS, 18, 10 1]
apāṃ ya ūrmau rasas tam aham asmā āmuṣyāyaṇāyaujase vīryāya gṛhṇāmīti naiyagrodhena | [BaudhŚS, 18, 10 2]
apāṃ yo madhyato rasas tam aham asmā āmuṣyāyaṇāya puṣṭyai prajananāya gṛhṇāmīty āśvatthena | [BaudhŚS, 18, 10 3]
apāṃ yo yajñiyo rasas tam aham asmā āmuṣyāyaṇāyāyuṣe dīrghāyutvāya gṛhṇāmīty audumbareṇa | [BaudhŚS, 18, 10 4]
athaitad rohitaṃ carmānaḍuhaṃ prācīnagrīvam uttaralomopastṛṇāti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 10 5]
tad yajamānaṃ prāñcam upaveśya suvarṇarajatābhyāṃ rukmābhyāṃ paryupāsyābhiṣiñcaty apāṃ yo dravaṇe rasas tenāham imam āmuṣyāyaṇaṃ tejase brahmavarcasāyābhiṣiñcāmīti parṇamayena | [BaudhŚS, 18, 10 6]
apāṃ ya ūrmau rasas tenāham imam āmuṣyāyaṇam ojase vīryāyābhiṣiñcāmīti naiyagrodhena | [BaudhŚS, 18, 10 7]
apāṃ yo madhyato rasas tenāham imam āmuṣyāyaṇaṃ puṣṭyai prajananāyābhiṣiñcāmīty āśvatthena | [BaudhŚS, 18, 10 8]
apāṃ yo yajñiyo rasas tenāham imam āmuṣyāyaṇam āyuṣe dīrghāyutvāyābhiṣiñcāmīty audumbareṇa | [BaudhŚS, 18, 10 9]
samunmṛṣṭe samutkrośantīti samānam ā mukhasya vimārjanāt | [BaudhŚS, 18, 10 10]
uttarata etad dhūpāyitaṃ śataṃ tiṣṭhati rathaś ca | [BaudhŚS, 18, 10 11]
tad abhipraity abhiprehi vīrayasva ugraś cettā sapatnahā | [BaudhŚS, 18, 10 12.1]
ātiṣṭha mitravardhanas tubhyaṃ devā adhi bravann iti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 10 12.2]
atha rathasya pakṣasī saṃmṛśaty aṅkau nyaṅkāv abhito rathaṃ yāv iti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 10 13]
ratham ātiṣṭhaty ātiṣṭha vṛtrahan iti pratipadya āyaṃ pṛṇaktu rajasī upastham ity ātaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 10 14]
athaitac chataṃ triḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ pariyāya puraskṛtyāyāti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 10 15]
tad adhvaryave dadāti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 10 16]
sa eṣa odanasavo rājño vā brāhmaṇasya vā vaiśyasya vā puṣṭikāmasya yajñaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 10 17]
{BaudhŚS, 18, 11}
pañcaśāradīyena yakṣyamāṇo bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 11 1]
sa upakalpayate saptadaśa niraṣṭān vatsatarān ekahāyanān | [BaudhŚS, 18, 11 2]
sa purastān mārgaśīrṣyai paurṇamāsyā āmāvāsyena haviṣeṣṭvā saptadaśa mārutīḥ pṛśnīr vatsatarīr ālabhate | [BaudhŚS, 18, 11 3]
abhiprokṣaṇato vatsatarān sthāpayitvotsṛjanti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 11 4]
athetarābhiḥ saṃsthāṃ kurvanti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 11 5]
saṃvatsare paryavete marudbhyaḥ sāṃtapanebhyaḥ saptadaśa pṛṣatīr vatsatarīr ālabhate | [BaudhŚS, 18, 11 6]
abhiprokṣaṇato vatsatarān sthāpayitvotsṛjanti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 11 7]
athetarābhir eva saṃsthāṃ kurvanti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 11 8]
dvitīye saṃvatsare paryavete marudbhyo gṛhamedhibhyaḥ saptadaśa kalmāṣīr vatsatarīr ālabhate | [BaudhŚS, 18, 11 9]
abhiprokṣaṇato vatsatarān sthāpayitvotsṛjanti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 11 10]
athetarābhir eva saṃsthāṃ kurvanti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 11 11]
tṛtīye saṃvatsare paryavete marudbhyaḥ krīḍibhyaḥ saptadaśāvaliptā vatsatarīr ālabhate | [BaudhŚS, 18, 11 12]
abhiprokṣaṇato vatsatarān sthāpayitvotsṛjanti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 11 13]
athetarābhir eva saṃsthāṃ kurvanti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 11 14]
caturthe saṃvatsare paryavete marudbhyaḥ svatavadbhyaḥ saptadaśa rājīvā vatsatarīr ālabhate | [BaudhŚS, 18, 11 15]
abhiprokṣaṇato vatsatarān sthāpayitvotsṛjanti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 11 16]
athetarābhir eva saṃsthāṃ kurvanti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 11 17]
etad evāhar dīkṣate | [BaudhŚS, 18, 11 18]
saṃvatsaram ukhyaṃ bibharti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 11 19]
dvādaśopasadaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 11 20]
tasyāhāni trivṛd agniṣṭomaḥ pañcadaśa ukthyaḥ saptadaśa ukthyaḥ pañcadaśa ukthyaḥ saptadaśo 'tirātraḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 11 21]
tasya māruta stomo bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 11 22]
athaiteṣāṃ paśūnāṃ trayaḥ prathame 'hann aindrāmārutā ukṣāṇaḥ savanīyā ālabhyante | [BaudhŚS, 18, 11 23]
evaṃ dvitīya evaṃ tṛtīya evaṃ caturthe | [BaudhŚS, 18, 11 24]
pañcottame 'hann ālabhyante | [BaudhŚS, 18, 11 25]
varṣiṣṭham iva hy etad ahar manyante varṣiṣṭhaḥ samānānāṃ bhavatīti brāhmaṇam | [BaudhŚS, 18, 11 26]
athaiteṣāṃ paśūnāṃ yadi naśyati mriyate vā yāśvamedhe prāyaścittis tāṃ kṛtvāthānyaṃ taddaivatyaṃ tadrūpaṃ tajjātīyaṃ paśum ālabhante | [BaudhŚS, 18, 11 27]
sa eṣa pañcaśāradīyo rājño vā brāhmaṇasya vā | [BaudhŚS, 18, 11 28]
yaḥ kāmayeta bahor bhūyān syām iti sa etena yajñakratunā yajeta | [BaudhŚS, 18, 11 29]
bahor eva bhūyān bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 11 30]
{BaudhŚS, 18, 12}
agniṣṭutā yakṣyamāṇo bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 12 1]
tasya sarvam eva samānaṃ puroruca evānyāḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 12 2]
asyājarāso 'gna āyūṃṣi pavasa ity aindravāyavasya | [BaudhŚS, 18, 12 3]
yajā no mitrāvaruṇā iti maitrāvaruṇasya | [BaudhŚS, 18, 12 4]
aśvinā pibataṃ sutam ity āśvinasya | [BaudhŚS, 18, 12 5]
dve virūpe carataḥ pūrvāparaṃ carato māyathaitāv iti śukrāmanthinoḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 12 6]
trīṇi śatā trī ṣahasrāṇy agnim ity āgrayaṇasya | [BaudhŚS, 18, 12 7]
niyunakty ukthyasya | [BaudhŚS, 18, 12 8]
nityā dhruvasya | [BaudhŚS, 18, 12 9]
agnināgniḥ samidhyata ity aindrāgnasya | [BaudhŚS, 18, 12 10]
agnir devānāṃ jaṭharam iti vaiśvadevasya | [BaudhŚS, 18, 12 11]
agniśriyo yad uttama īḍe agniṃ svavasam iti tisro marutvatīyānām | [BaudhŚS, 18, 12 12]
śrudhi śrutkarṇa vahnibhir iti māhendrasya | [BaudhŚS, 18, 12 13]
viśveṣām aditir yajñiyānām tve agne tvām agna iti tisra ādityasya grahasya | [BaudhŚS, 18, 12 14]
ni tvā yajñasya sādhanam iti sāvitrasya | [BaudhŚS, 18, 12 15]
nityā pātnīvatasya | [BaudhŚS, 18, 12 16]
niyunakti hāriyojanasya | [BaudhŚS, 18, 12 17]
sa eṣa trivṛd agniṣṭut pavitram | [BaudhŚS, 18, 12 18]
yathā ha vā idaṃ dāvādabhidūnā abhivṛṣṭāḥ punarṇavā oṣadhayaḥ samuttiṣṭhanty evaṃ ha vā eṣa etena yajñakratuneṣṭvā śuciḥ pūto medhyo bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 12 19]
sa yadi mukhena pāpakṛn manyeta trivṛtaṃ kurvīta | [BaudhŚS, 18, 12 20]
eṣa ha vai mukhena pāpaṃ karoti yo 'nūcānasya vā muner vā duravagatam avagacchati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 12 21]
yadi bāhubhyāṃ pañcadaśaṃ kurvīta | [BaudhŚS, 18, 12 22]
eṣa ha vai bāhubhyāṃ pāpaṃ karoti yo brāhmaṇāyodyacchate | [BaudhŚS, 18, 12 23]
yady udareṇa saptadaśaṃ kurvīta | [BaudhŚS, 18, 12 24]
eṣa ha vā udareṇa pāpaṃ karoti yo 'nāśyānnasyānnam aśnāti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 12 25]
yadi padbhyām ekaviṃśaṃ kurvīta | [BaudhŚS, 18, 12 26]
eṣa ha vai padbhyāṃ pāpaṃ karoti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 12 27]
{BaudhŚS, 18, 13}
ya āraṭṭān vā gāndhārān vā sauvīrān vā karaskarān vā kaliṅgān vā gacchati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 13 1]
sa yadi sarvaśa eva pāpakṛn manyeta catuṣṭomenāgniṣṭomena yajeta | [BaudhŚS, 18, 13 2]
tena haitenartuparṇo bhāṅgāśvina īje śaphālānāṃ rājā | [BaudhŚS, 18, 13 3]
tena heṣṭvā mṛgayām abhiprayayau | [BaudhŚS, 18, 13 4]
taṃ hendro 'nukhyāyaivekṣāṃcakre 'ham u tvā tad yātaye yan mā yajñakrator antarāya iti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 13 5]
sa ha svinna udakam abhyaveyāya | [BaudhŚS, 18, 13 6]
taṃ ha tatraiva striyaṃ cakāra | [BaudhŚS, 18, 13 7]
sā sudevalā nāmāsa | [BaudhŚS, 18, 13 8]
sā haitad eva rāṣṭram abhyāruroha | [BaudhŚS, 18, 13 9]
sā strī satī putrān janayāṃcakāra | [BaudhŚS, 18, 13 10]
tebhyo hendraḥ samadaṃ dadhau | [BaudhŚS, 18, 13 11]
te hatā vidṛḍhāḥ śiśyire | [BaudhŚS, 18, 13 12]
tān ubhayān antareṇa rudanty āsāṃcakre | [BaudhŚS, 18, 13 13]
atho hendra ājagāma | [BaudhŚS, 18, 13 14]
tām u hābhyupeyāya | [BaudhŚS, 18, 13 15]
tāṃ hovāca sudevalā3 iti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 13 16]
bhagava iti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 13 17]
priyaṃ tavaitad iti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 13 18]
kiṃ me bhagavaḥ priyaṃ bhaviṣyatīti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 13 19]
evaṃ vai mama tad apriyam āsīd yan mā yajñakrator antarāyo vṛṇīṣva nu yatare te putrā jīveyur iti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 13 20]
yān eva bhagava strī saty adhyagamam iti hovāca | [BaudhŚS, 18, 13 21]
tasmād āhuḥ striyāḥ putrāḥ preyāṃso bhavantīti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 13 22]
sa etasminn eva pūrvapakṣe catuṣṭomenāgniṣṭomena yajeta purā bhreṣācchāntyai | [BaudhŚS, 18, 13 23]
{BaudhŚS, 18, 14}
indrastutā yakṣyamāṇo bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 14 1]
tasya sarvam eva samānaṃ puroruca evānyāḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 14 2]
tiṣṭhā harī kasya vṛṣā sute sacety aindravāyavasya | [BaudhŚS, 18, 14 3]
indraṃ vayaṃ mahādhana iti maitrāvaruṇasya | [BaudhŚS, 18, 14 4]
dvitā yo vṛtrahantama ity āśvinasya | [BaudhŚS, 18, 14 5]
sa sūra ājanayañjyotir indram uta tyad āśvaśviyam iti śukrāmanthinoḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 14 6]
bhareṣv indram ity āgrayaṇasya | [BaudhŚS, 18, 14 7]
nityokthyasya | [BaudhŚS, 18, 14 8]
niyunakti dhruvasya | [BaudhŚS, 18, 14 9]
mahi kṣetraṃ puruś candram ity aindrāgnasya | [BaudhŚS, 18, 14 10]
uruṃ no lokam anuneṣi vidvān iti vaiśvadevasya | [BaudhŚS, 18, 14 11]
nityā marutvatīyānām | [BaudhŚS, 18, 14 12]
nityā māhendrasya | [BaudhŚS, 18, 14 13]
ā no viśvābhir ūtibhiḥ kadācana starīr asīndrāya gāva āśiram iti tisra ādityasya grahasya | [BaudhŚS, 18, 14 14]
imāṃ te dhiyam iti sāvitrasya | [BaudhŚS, 18, 14 15]
niyunakti pātnīvatasya | [BaudhŚS, 18, 14 16]
nityā hāriyojanasya | [BaudhŚS, 18, 14 17]
sa eṣa pañcadaśa indrastud indriyakāmasya | [BaudhŚS, 18, 14 18]
yo vā jyeṣṭhabandhur apabhūtaḥ syāt sa etena yajñakratunā yajeta | [BaudhŚS, 18, 14 19]
aśnute haiva jyeṣṭhatām | [BaudhŚS, 18, 14 20]
{BaudhŚS, 18, 15}
aptoryāmeṇa yakṣyamāṇo bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 15 1]
dīkṣate | [BaudhŚS, 18, 15 2]
tasyāparimitā dīkṣā dvādaśopasadaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 15 3]
trivṛd bahiṣpavamānaḥ pañcadaśaṃ hotur ājyaṃ saptadaśaṃ maitrāvaruṇasyaikaviṃśaṃ brāhmaṇācchaṃsinas triṇavam acchāvākasya | [BaudhŚS, 18, 15 4]
trayastriṃśo mādhyaṃdinaḥ pavamānaḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 15 5]
caturviṃśaṃ hotuḥ pṛṣṭhaṃ rathaṃtaraṃ ca vairājaṃ ca sāmanī anyatareṇānyatarat pariṣṭuvanti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 15 6]
catuścatvāriṃśaṃ maitrāvaruṇasya vāmadevyaṃ ca śākvaraṃ ca sāmanī anyatareṇānyatarat pariṣṭuvanti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 15 7]
aṣṭācatvāriṃśaṃ brāhmaṇācchaṃsino naudhasaṃ ca vairūpaṃ ca sāmanī anyatareṇānyatarat pariṣṭuvanti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 15 8]
ekaviṃśam acchāvākasya kāleyaṃ ca raivataṃ ca sāmanī anyatareṇānyatarat pariṣṭuvanti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 15 9]
tam etam aṣṭāpṛṣṭha iti chandogā ācakṣate | [BaudhŚS, 18, 15 10]
triṇava ārbhavaḥ pavamānas trayastriṃśam agniṣṭomasāmaikaviṃśāny ukthyāni saṣoḍaśikāni pañcadaśānītarāṇi trivṛd rāthaṃtaraḥ sandhiḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 15 11]
tat kṣudrāḥ paśavo 'tiseduḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 15 12]
somo vā etad atiricyamāna iyāya | [BaudhŚS, 18, 15 13]
te devā abruvann aptor vā ayam atyareci tasya ko yāma iti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 15 14]
tad aptoryāmasyāptoryāmatvam | [BaudhŚS, 18, 15 15]
tasmā etāny atiriktastotrāṇy avakalpayāṃcakrus trivṛddhotur jarābodhīyaṃ pañcadaśaṃ maitrāvaruṇasya sauhaviṣaṃ saptadaśaṃ brāhmaṇācchaṃsina udvaṃśīyam ekaviṃśam acchāvākasya vāravantīyam | [BaudhŚS, 18, 15 16]
tad u vā āhur yad acchāvākacamasam anu yajñaḥ saṃtiṣṭhetāntaṃ yajñaṃ gamayet | [BaudhŚS, 18, 15 17]
atho hāntaṃ yajamāno gāmukaḥ syāt | [BaudhŚS, 18, 15 18]
hotra eva stuvīran hotānuśaṃsyāt tathā madhyato yajñaḥ samādhīyata iti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 15 19]
tad u vā āhuḥ sarvāṇy evāśvināni stutaśastrāṇi syuḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 15 20]
yaddha kiṃca rātrim upātiricyate sarvaṃ tad āśvinam iti nv ekam | [BaudhŚS, 18, 15 21]
athāparaṃ trivṛt pañcadaśaṃ saptadaśam ekaviṃśam | [BaudhŚS, 18, 15 22]
athaiteṣāṃ devatā agnir indro viśve devā viṣṇur iti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 15 23]
{BaudhŚS, 18, 16}
mṛtyusavena yakṣyamāṇo bhavati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 16 1]
sa upakalpayate śārdūlacarma suvarṇarajatau ca rukmau vaiyāghryāv upānahau cārmapakṣyāv upānahau vṛṣṇivāsasaṃ ca kṣaumaṃ ca tisṛdhanvam āsandīṃ sādhīvāsāṃ dundubhiṃ vimitam audumbaraṃ droṇaṃ catuḥsrakti catuṣṭayīr apo digbhyaḥ saṃbhṛtāḥ śataṃ ca rathaṃ ca | [BaudhŚS, 18, 16 2]
etenopakﾱptena citrām āyatīm uparamati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 16 3]
atha citrayeti pūrvāgnim anvavasyaty uttapanīyaṃ śālīno 'nvāhāryapacanam āhitāgniḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 16 4]
athānvārabdhe yajamāne juhoti vyāghro 'yam agnau carati praviṣṭa iti ṣaṭ sruvāhutīḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 16 5]
atha yajamānāyatane śārdūlacarma prācīnagrīvam uttaralomopastṛṇāti yat te śilpaṃ kaśyapa rocanāvat indriyāvat puṣkalaṃ citrabhānu | [BaudhŚS, 18, 16 6.1]
yasmint sūryā arpitāḥ sapta sākam tasmin rājānam adhiviśrayemam iti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 16 6.2]
atha vaiyāghryāv upānahāv upamuñcate dyaur asīti dakṣiṇe pāde pṛthivy asīty uttare | [BaudhŚS, 18, 16 7]
atha dakṣiṇaṃ jānv ācyābhisarpati vyāghro vaiyāghre 'dhi viśrayasva diśo mahīḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 16 8.1]
viśas tvā sarvā vāñchantu mā tvad rāṣṭram adhi bhraśad iti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 16 8.2]
athāsmai dhanuḥ prayacchati yathā rājasūye tathā | [BaudhŚS, 18, 16 9]
tad yajamānaṃ prāñcam upaveśya suvarṇarajatābhyāṃ rukmābhyāṃ paryupāsyaudumbare droṇe catuṣṭayīr apaḥ samavanīyābhiṣiñcati | [BaudhŚS, 18, 16 10]
{BaudhŚS, 18, 17}
yā divyā āpaḥ payasā saṃbabhūvur yā antarikṣa uta pārthivīr yāḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 17 1.1]
tāsāṃ tvā sarvāsāṃ rucā abhiṣiñcāmi varcasā | [BaudhŚS, 18, 17 1.2]
abhi tvā varcasāsicam divyena payasā saha | [BaudhŚS, 18, 17 2.1]
yathāsā rāṣṭravardhanas tathā tvā savitā karat | [BaudhŚS, 18, 17 2.2]
indraṃ viśvā avīvṛdhan samudravyacasaṃ giraḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 17 3.1]
rathītamaṃ rathīnām vājānāṃ satpatiṃ patim | [BaudhŚS, 18, 17 3.2]

etā eva tisro 'nudrutya rudrās tvā dakṣiṇato 'bhiṣiñcantu traiṣṭubhena chandaseti dakṣiṇataḥ | [BaudhŚS, 18, 17 5.1]

athāsyora ūrdhvam unmṛjyate aruṇaṃ tvā vṛkam ugraṃ khajaṃkaram iti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 17 9.1]

athaināv upāvaharatīndrasya te vīryakṛto bāhū upāvaharāmīti | [BaudhŚS, 18, 17 11.1]
